# gr-qc [[Back]](#toc)

### [1] [Gravitational helicity in connection variables](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27493)
*Xiao-Kan Guo,Shupeng Song*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文利用协变相空间方法，在联络变量和自对偶Ashtekar变量框架下研究了引力手征性（gravitational helicity），发现其与Nieh-Yan拓扑项存在直接联系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旨在从协变相空间（covariant phase space）出发，在联络变量框架下系统地构建引力手征性，并阐明其与拓扑不变量的关系。

Method: 采用协变相空间方法，在广义相对论的联络变量表述中构造辛形式（symplectic form）；通过内部霍奇对偶（internal Hodge dual）识别对偶变换；引入复自对偶Ashtekar变量将对偶性简化为U(1)相位旋转，并由此导出诺特荷（Noether charge）。

Result: 由对偶变换的诺特荷得到守恒量，即引力手征性；该手征性在实变量表述下可关联至Nieh-Yan拓扑项，建立引力手征性与拓扑不变量（topological invariant）之间的直接联系。

Conclusion: 引力手征性在协变相空间框架下得以明确定义，其与Nieh-Yan拓扑项的关系揭示了该物理量深层的拓扑本质。

Abstract: We study the gravitational helicity using the covariant phase space method. Starting from the covariant phase space of general relativity expressed in terms of connection variables, we construct the symplectic form and identify a duality transformation based on the internal Hodge dual. To make the symmetry manifest, we employ the complex self-dual Ashtekar variables, where the duality becomes a simple $U(1)$ phase rotation. The Noether charge associated with this duality yields a conserved quantity which is interpreted as the gravitational helicity. Remarkably, this helicity can be related to the Nieh-Yan topological term, when expressed in terms of the real variables, establishing a direct link between the gravitational helicity and a topological invariant.

</details>


### [2] [Constraining Gravitational Wave Memory with Hierarchical Inference](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27500)
*Keefe Mitman,Maximiliano Isi,Will M. Farr*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文利用层次贝叶斯推断（hierarchical Bayesian inference）对GWTC-4.0目录中的双黑洞引力波事件进行分析，以测量引力波零记忆效应（gravitational wave null memory effect）的观测证据。研究将记忆增强因子（memory enhancement factor）约束为0.32^{+6.30}_{-5.12}，与广义相对论预测值1一致，并预计需约2,500次探测才能在1σ水平上排除零值。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 过去十年引力波观测的增多使探测强引力场的动力学和非线性特性成为可能。引力波零记忆效应是广义相对论（general relativity, GR）的一个非线性预言，但此前利用贝叶斯因子（Bayes factors）进行的记忆分析对先验敏感，且在多事件叠加时可能导向错误结论，亟需更严谨的统计方法。

Method: 采用层次贝叶斯推断（hierarchical Bayesian inference）方法，基于GWTC-4.0目录中的双黑洞并合观测数据，测量记忆增强因子（memory enhancement factor）——即应变中超动量通量（supermomentum flux）贡献前的常数——的后验分布，以避免贝叶斯因子方法中的先验敏感性和多事件累乘问题。

Result: 记忆增强因子被约束为0.32^{+6.30}_{-5.12}（±值表示68%置信区间），与GR预测值1一致。预测需要约2,500次引力波探测才能在1σ水平上将该因子约束至不为零。

Conclusion: 当前LVK观测数据尚无法对记忆增强因子提供显著的非零约束，但层次贝叶斯推断为未来更大样本的引力波记忆效应检验提供了更可靠的统计框架。

Abstract: With the multitude of gravitational wave observations that have been made in the past ten years, probing the dynamical and nonlinear nature of strong gravity is becoming more and more feasible. One promising way to test the nonlinear nature of Einstein's theory of general relativity (GR) is through the gravitational wave null memory effect: a nonlinear prediction of GR which corresponds to initially comoving observers being permanently displaced due to a burst of gravitational radiation. Previous studies have shown that, while it is unlikely that the memory effect will be observed in a single event by the LIGO-Virgo-KAGRA (LVK) detectors, evidence for memory in the population of LVK events should be attainable after $\sim$2,000 gravitational wave detections. These works, however, largely relied on Bayes factors to perform their memory analyses: an approach that can depend sensitively on the analysis priors and, when naively multiplied across many events, can even favor incorrect conclusions. In this work, using the GWTC-4.0 catalog of binary black hole observations, we instead perform hierarchical Bayesian inference -- which is not subject to the issues associated with Bayes factors -- to measure the evidence for memory in current LVK observations. We find that we can constrain what we call the memory enhancement factor -- the constant appearing in front of the contribution to the strain from the supermomentum flux -- to $0.32^{+6.30}_{-5.12}$ (with $\pm$ values denoting the 68% credible interval), consistent with its GR value of 1. We forecast that $\sim$2,500 detections will be needed to constrain the memory enhancement factor away from zero at the $1σ$ level.

</details>


### [3] [Charting causal set configuration space with graph observables](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27514)
*Astrid Eichhorn,Harald Mack,Kim Tuyen Le,Fabian Wagner*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文系统研究了九类因果集（causal sets）的构型空间，通过图观测量（graph observables）而非连续几何观测量来区分不同类别，发现链接度分布、对称化Hasse图的图拉普拉斯特征值以及因果区间的丰度这三个观测量能够有效区分各类因果集。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 因果集的构型空间极为庞大，绘制该空间的结构是核心目标。此前大多数因果集类别尚未被研究，且基于连续几何的观测量（如曲率不变量）存在涨落大、计算成本高的问题。

Method: 研究了九类因果集，包括具有非均匀里奇曲率（Ricci curvature）的类流形因果集（拓扑平凡与非平凡）、非类流形因果集（格点、分层序、洛伦兹准晶），以及当前非类流形但在适当粗粒化（coarse-graining）下可变为类流形的类别。采用图观测量（子图统计量与全局观测量）代替连续几何观测量进行分析。

Result: 链接度分布（link degree distribution）、对称化Hasse图的图拉普拉斯（graph Laplacian）特征值，以及最近提出的因果区间（causal intervals）丰度这三个观测量，能够区分所有九类因果集。这些观测量在大多数类别中涨落较小，从而使得区分成为可能。

Conclusion: 图观测量为刻画和区分不同类别的因果集提供了有效且计算可行的工具，有助于推进因果集构型空间的系统映射。

Abstract: The configuration space of causal sets is vast. It is a critical goal to map out this space. Here, we take a practical step towards this goal. We investigate nine classes of causal sets, most of them not studied before. These include manifoldlike causal sets with inhomogeneous Ricci curvature, both topologically trivial and nontrivial. We also study classes of non-manifoldlike causal sets, including lattices, layered orders as well as Lorentzian quasicrystals. Finally, we study classes of causal sets that are not manifoldlike, but are expected to become manifoldlike under a suitable coarse-graining process. We use this broad range of distinct classes of causal sets as a testbed for observables. Rather than focusing on continuum-geometry inspired observables, such as curvature invariants, which often exhibit large fluctuations and are computationally very expensive, we focus on graph observables, including some observables that constitute subgraph statistics and some that are global. We find that three observables, namely the link degree distribution, the eigenvalues of the graph Laplacian of the symmetrized Hasse diagram and the recently proposed abundance of causal intervals, can distinguish between the distinct classes of causal sets. This is made possible by the small fluctuations that these observables have in most classes.

</details>


### [4] [Stationary generalizations for the vacuum ring wormhole](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27600)
*Mikhail S. Volkov*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究环形虫洞（ring wormhole）——克尔度规（Kerr metric）的零质量极限——的稳态推广。通过求解真空Ernst方程，数值构造了非微扰解，发现慢速旋转时满足 M∼J² 的非相对论关系，快速旋转时过渡到 Regge 关系 J=M²，且在极端条件下可趋近并“模仿”极端克尔解（extremal Kerr solution）。通过标量化（scalarization）程序可消除环上的曲率奇点，得到含鬼标量场（phantom scalar field）的正则虫洞。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 环形虫洞作为Kerr度规的零质量极限，具有局域平坦但拓扑非平凡的几何结构，且环绕喉咙的环上存在分布性曲率奇点。此前仅构造了慢速旋转的微扰解，本文旨在通过数值方法获得非微扰的稳态推广解，系统地分析其旋转性质及与Kerr解的关联。

Method: 将静态环形虫洞推广至稳态情形，要求解在虫洞喉部两侧反射对称。问题归结为在相应对称性条件下求解真空Ernst方程（vacuum Ernst equations）。对于慢速旋转采用微扰方法，而对非微扰解则采用数值框架进行详细分析。

Result: 慢速旋转时，质量M与角动量J满足非相对论关系 M∼J²；快速旋转且J→∞时，环被离心力无限拉伸，关系过渡为Regge关系 J=M²；若同时将静态极限下的环尺寸趋于零，则M和J保持有界，喉部线速度趋近于1，虫洞几何趋近并“模仿”极端Kerr解。虫洞环上存在曲率奇点，但可通过标量化程序（引入鬼标量场）将其消除，得到正则虫洞。

Conclusion: 环形虫洞的稳态解在不同旋转速率下展现出从非相对论到相对论（Regge）的质量-角动量关系转变，并在特定极限下可模仿极端Kerr黑洞。尽管原始解带有曲率奇点，但通过标量化方法可构造无奇点的正则虫洞，这为虫洞物理与黑洞物理之间的关联提供了新视角。

Abstract: The ring wormhole is the zero-mass limit of the Kerr metric. Its geometry is locally flat, but the topology is nontrivial, with a throat connecting two asymptotic regions and a distributional curvature singularity on the ring encircling the throat. We construct stationary generalizations of this static wormhole that are different from Kerr and invariant under reflections across the wormhole throat. The problem reduces to solving the vacuum Ernst equations subject to the corresponding symmetry conditions. The slowly rotating perturbative solutions were constructed previously, while we now present a detailed analysis of non-perturbative solutions obtained within a numerical framework. For slow rotation, they exhibit the non-relativistic relation $M\sim J^2$ between the mass and angular momentum, which transforms into the Regge relation $J=M^2$ in the fast-rotation regime, when $J\to\infty$ and the ring is stretched without bound by the centrifugal force. However, if the ring size in the static limit is sent to zero at the same time, then $M$ and $J$ remain bounded as the throat linear velocity approaches unity. The wormhole geometry then approaches the extremal Kerr solution, thus ``mimicking'' it. The wormholes carry a curvature singularity at the ring, but this can be removed by via simple ``scalarization'' procedure that promotes the vacuum solutions to regular wormholes with a phantom scalar field.

</details>


### [5] [Lorentz-Violating (Regular) Black Holes in Einstein Gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27615)
*Zhi-Chao Li,H. Lu*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文基于非线性电动力学（nonlinear electrodynamics）构建一个最小耦合暗扇区（minimally coupled dark sector），通过该机制在爱因斯坦引力（Einstein gravity）中生成从规则核心过渡到渐近洛伦兹破缺锥形几何（asymptotic Lorentz-violating conical geometry）的时空结构，进而获得洛伦兹破缺的Schwarzschild、Reissner-Nordström、Bardeen、Hayward以及一类带电规则黑洞。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索一种简单机制，在最小耦合物质的爱因斯坦引力框架下，生成具有规则核心的洛伦兹破缺黑洞解，从而将规则黑洞与洛伦兹破缺几何统一描述。

Method: 引入一个基于非线性电动力学的最小耦合暗扇区，使得时空从规则核心平滑插值到渐近的洛伦兹破缺锥形几何。该构造不涉及额外的高阶引力修正，仅靠物质场耦合实现。

Result: 在爱因斯坦引力中获得了洛伦兹破缺的Schwarzschild和Reissner-Nordström黑洞解；进一步构造了洛伦兹破缺的规则黑洞，包括Bardeen黑洞、Hayward黑洞以及一类带电规则黑洞。

Conclusion: 该工作提供了一种在爱因斯坦引力中同时实现规则黑洞和洛伦兹破缺时空的统一构造方法，丰富了规则黑洞解的家族，并为暗扇区（dark sector）与引力相互作用的建模提供了新视角。

Abstract: We introduce a minimally coupled dark sector based on a nonlinear electrodynamics to generate regular spacetime textures that interpolate from a regular core to an asymptotic Lorentz-violating conical geometry. This construction provides a simple mechanism, in Einstein gravity with minimally coupled matter, for obtaining Lorentz-violating Schwarzschild and Reissner-Nordström black holes. The framework further allows us to construct Lorentz-violating regular black holes, including the Bardeen and Hayward black holes, as well as a class of electrically-charged regular black holes.

</details>


### [6] [Reconstructing ACT-compatible and GW170817-compatible Einstein-Gauss-Bonnet Inflation from the Observational Indices](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27727)
*V. K. Oikonomou*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文通过逆向重构技术，构建了同时符合宇宙微波背景辐射（cosmic microwave background, CMB）观测（ACT）和引力波事件GW170817约束的爱因斯坦-高斯-博内（Einstein-Gauss-Bonnet, EGB）暴胀理论。利用给定的张量-标量比（tensor-to-scalar ratio）重构出标量-高斯-博内耦合函数与标量势的具体形式，并给出了四个通过全部观测检验的可行暴胀模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有爱因斯坦-高斯-博内（EGB）暴胀理论中，标量扰动振幅的非平凡约束导致许多模型难以同时满足ACT实验和引力波事件GW170817的观测限制；亟需一种系统方法直接构建与这些观测兼容的理论。

Method: 采用逆向重构技术，从给定的张量-标量比（tensor-to-scalar ratio）出发，反推出标量-高斯-博内耦合函数（scalar Gauss-Bonnet coupling function）和标量势（scalar potential）的具体形式，使所得理论自动满足ACT与GW170817的约束。

Result: 给出了系统的形式化框架，并获得了四个不同的暴胀模型，这些模型均通过了标量扰动振幅、ACT观测和GW170817引力波约束在内的系列观测检验。

Conclusion: 逆向重构技术能够有效地构建同时与ACT和GW170817兼容的爱因斯坦-高斯-博内暴胀理论，为在高维引力修正框架下寻找可行的暴胀模型提供了可行途径。

Abstract: In this work we use an inverse reconstruction technique for constructing ACT-compatible and GW170817-compatible Einstein-Gauss-Bonnet inflationary theories. From a given tensor-to-scalar ratio using the reconstruction technique, we find which scalar Gauss-Bonnet coupling function and which scalar potential can yield the given tensor-to-scalar ratio. We present the formalism and the viable theories pass a series of observational tests, including the amplitude of the scalar perturbations, which is non-trivial for Einstein-Gauss-Bonnet theories. We present four viable models of inflation that pass all the observational tests.

</details>


### [7] [Shadow, acoustic redshift, and transfer observables of Lorentz-violating rotating acoustic black holes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27862)
*Fernando M. Belchior,Edilberto O. Silva*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文针对具有洛伦兹对称性破缺（Lorentz symmetry violation）的旋转声学黑洞，建立了冲击参数分辨的传递分析框架，推导了零射线方程、临界冲击参数条件、声阴影区间及红移传递因子，并构建了薄环与扩展盘的强度传递方案，揭示了阴影宽度、质心、红移不对称性和通量不对称性等可观测量的层级结构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在洛伦兹破缺的旋转声学黑洞背景中，现有研究缺乏系统的冲击参数分辨传递分析，无法全面刻画洛伦兹破缺参数α对声阴影、红移及强度分布的影响。

Method: 基于(2+1)维洛伦兹破缺排水浴缸几何（draining-bathtub geometry），推导零射线方程与临界冲击参数条件；利用声阴影区间和红移传递因子，构建考虑源发射率、发射体运动、有限源宽度及探测器卷积的薄环与扩展盘强度传递方案。

Result: 声阴影宽度探测洛伦兹破缺展宽效应，阴影质心追踪旋转参数B，左右声学红移不对称性检验分支依赖的多普勒效应和参考系拖曳效应，积分通量不对称性测量它们对观测强度的印记。合成二维声学屏幕图显示(2+1)维捕获区间自然表示为垂直条带，其位移和亮度不平衡编码了B与α的联合效果。

Conclusion: 该传递分析框架将洛伦兹破缺参数α与旋转参数B的影响映射为可观测的阴影和红移结构，为声学模拟黑洞中的洛伦兹对称性检验提供了定量诊断工具。

Abstract: We develop an impact-parameter-resolved transfer analysis for the rotating acoustic black hole with Lorentz symmetry violation. The background is the $(2+1)$-dimensional Lorentz-violating draining-bathtub geometry, where the draining parameter $A$ fixes the sonic horizon, the circulation parameter $B$ controls rotation, and the Lorentz-breaking parameter $α$ deforms the effective acoustic metric. We derive the null-ray equations, the critical-impact-parameter conditions, the acoustic shadow interval, and the redshift transfer factor. We then formulate an intensity-transfer prescription for thin rings and extended disks that accounts for source emissivity, emitter motion, finite source width, and detector convolution. The resulting observables form a hierarchy: the shadow width probes Lorentz-violating broadening, the shadow centroid traces rotation, the left-right acoustic-redshift asymmetry tests branch-dependent Doppler and frame-dragging effects, and the integrated flux asymmetry measures their imprint on the observed intensity. We also construct synthetic two-dimensional acoustic screen maps, showing that the $(2+1)$-dimensional capture interval is naturally represented as a vertical strip whose displacement and brightness imbalance encode the combined effects of $B$ and $α$. We focus on the exterior-regular regime $α\geq0$, with $α=0$ retained as the Lorentz-symmetric benchmark.

</details>


### [8] [Probing Effective Field Theory Corrections with Quasinormal Modes and Gravitational Lensing in Reissner-Nordström Black Holes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27953)
*Takamasa Kanai*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文在有效场论（EFT）框架下，系统研究了弱场和强场引力透镜效应对EFT修正的Reissner-Nordström黑洞时空的影响，推导了高导数曲率-电磁相互作用对偏转角、光子球半径、临界碰撞参数及强透镜系数的修正，并指出强引力透镜观测可为超越广义相对论的高曲率EFT耦合提供约束。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 有效场论（effective field theory, EFT）为参数化广义相对论之外的高能修正提供了系统性框架，但高曲率相互作用对引力透镜效应的影响尚待系统研究，尤其是在带电黑洞背景下的强场透镜区域。

Method: 采用强偏转极限形式论（strong deflection limit formalism），针对弱荷和近极端两种构型，推导了EFT修正的Reissner-Nordström黑洞时空中偏转角、光子球半径、临界碰撞参数以及强透镜系数的解析修正表达式。分析限于背景时空几何修正，未包含光子传播定律的极化依赖修正。

Result: 高导数曲率-电磁相互作用对强引力透镜可观测量产生可解析计算的修正；带电黑洞背景下的强透镜观测可作为引力和电磁场之间有效相互作用的互补探针。

Conclusion: 未来高精度强透镜现象观测可能对超越广义相对论的高曲率EFT耦合常数施加约束。

Abstract: Effective field theory (EFT) provides a systematic framework for parametrizing possible higher-energy corrections to general relativity through higher-curvature interactions. In this work, we investigate gravitational lensing in both weak- and strong-field regimes for EFT-corrected Reissner-Nordström black hole spacetimes, focusing on both weakly charged and near-extremal configurations. Using the strong deflection limit formalism, we derive the corresponding corrections to the deflection angle, photon sphere radius, critical impact parameter, and strong lensing coefficients induced by higher-derivative curvature-electromagnetic interactions.
  Our analysis is restricted to purely geometrical corrections associated with modifications of the background spacetime geometry, without including polarization-dependent corrections to the photon propagation law. We show that strong gravitational lensing observables in charged black hole backgrounds can provide complementary probes of effective interactions between gravity and electromagnetic fields. These results suggest that future high-precision observations of strong lensing phenomena may place constraints on higher-curvature EFT couplings beyond general relativity.

</details>


### [9] [Dynamical Resolution of the Cosmic Coincidence Problem in Non-Interacting Holographic Dark Energy via Einstein-Cartan Torsion](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27973)
*Yongjun Yun,Kyungduk Kim,Jungjai Lee*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文提出在爱因斯坦-卡坦引力（Einstein-Cartan gravity）框架下，利用宇宙学原理兼容的挠率标量（torsion scalar）Φ的自洽标度行为Φ～a⁻³，使得非相互作用的全息暗能量模型（holographic dark energy）中的密度比r≡ρ_m/ρ_X成为动力学变量，无需引入唯象相互作用项即可解决宇宙巧合问题（cosmic coincidence problem）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准广义相对论中，以哈勃半径为红外截断（infrared cutoff）的非相互作用全息暗能量呈现出类似尘埃的状态方程（equation of state），无法解释宇宙加速膨胀，且密度比为常数，因而存在宇宙巧合问题。作者旨在寻找一种几何机制替代唯象的暗区耦合（dark sector coupling），在无需精细调节参数的前提下实现动力学密度比与加速膨胀。

Method: 作者将爱因斯坦-卡坦引力中满足宇宙学原理（cosmological principle）的挠率标量Φ引入非相互作用全息暗能量模型，并采用自洽的标度行为Φ～a⁻³进行分析。挠率贡献无需额外的唯象相互作用项Q=0，即可使暗能量状态方程向负值偏移，并使物质与暗能量密度比r成为动力学变量。

Result: 挠率标量的存在使得密度比r从常数变为动态演化；暗能量状态方程被推向负值区域，从而能够驱动宇宙加速膨胀。在弱挠率（weak torsion）区域，无需调节全息自由参数即可实现观测上要求的量级为1的密度比。

Conclusion: 爱因斯坦-卡坦引力中的挠率提供了一种几何机制，能够取代唯象的暗区相互作用，实现宇宙巧合问题的动力学解决。

Abstract: We investigate the cosmic coincidence problem in non-interacting holographic dark energy with the Hubble radius as the infrared cutoff in Einstein-Cartan gravity. In general relativity, this cutoff gives a dust-like equation of state in the non-interacting case, whereas interacting models require a phenomenological dark sector coupling and yield a constant density ratio. We show that the Einstein-Cartan torsion scalar $Φ$, compatible with the cosmological principle, with the self-consistent scaling behavior $Φ\sim a^{-3}$, makes the density ratio $r\equiv ρ_m/ρ_X$ dynamical even when the phenomenological interaction term is absent, $Q=0$. The same torsion contribution shifts the equation of state for holographic dark energy toward negative values, allowing cosmic acceleration, and realizes the observed order-unity density ratio within the weak torsion regime without tuning the holographic free parameter. Thus, Einstein-Cartan torsion provides a geometric mechanism that replaces the phenomenological dark sector interaction and offers a dynamical resolution of the cosmic coincidence problem.

### [10] [Scalar absorption beyond geometric optics in Klein-Gordon-separable Johannsen black hole spacetimes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28094)
*Jining Tang,Yang Huang,Hongsheng Zhang*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文在Johannsen度规（Kerr度规的广义化）中构建了无质量标量平面波的吸收理论框架，通过Klein-Gordon可分离子类推导了角向与径向方程，分析了不同变形扇区对低频面积律、高频零限俘获截面及有限频率吸收谱的影响，并提出有限频率吸收可作为强场检验黑洞几何的新诊断工具。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Johannsen度规是最一般的稳态轴对称时空，能保留Carter守恒量，为强场检验无毛定理（no-hair theorem）及Kerr黑洞几何偏差提供系统框架。本文旨在构建该框架下的波吸收理论，以探索传统几何光学手段无法触及的径向传播扇区。

Method: 在渐近平坦的Johannsen度规中施加Klein-Gordon可分离条件，推导分离后的角向方程与径向方程；针对主导变形扇区$A_1(r)$、$A_2(r)$和$A_5(r)$构建分波（partial wave）框架，并区分改变径向尺度函数$X(r)$的变形与仅进入径向动能项的变形。

Result: 改变$X(r)$的变形会修改低频面积律、高频零限俘获截面及有限频率吸收谱；纯$A_5$变形不改变主导零限俘获可观测量，但在波传播中仍可探测。在非正入射、共/反旋转贡献及超辐射（superradiance）模式中，$X(r_+)$的变化会移动视界角速度及超辐射阈值。

Conclusion: 有限频率吸收可作为波光学（wave-optics）诊断工具，探测面积律和零限测地线俘获可观测量无法触及的径向传播扇区，为强场检验黑洞几何提供新手段。

Abstract: Johannsen metric is a natural and significant generalization of the Kerr metric, representing the most general stationary, axisymmetric spacetime that preserves the Carter constant of motion. The theoretical status furnishes a powerful, systematic framework for strong-field tests of the no-hair theorem and for investigations of deviations from Kerr black-hole geometries. We formulate massless scalar plane-wave absorption in a Klein-Gordon-separable subclass of Johannsen spacetimes. In the asymptotically flat Johannsen metric, we impose Klein-Gordon separability, derive the separated angular and radial equations, and build a partial wave framework for the leading deformation sectors $A_1(r)$, $A_2(r)$, and $A_5(r)$. The resulting description separates deformations that change the radial size function $X(r)$ from those that enter only the radial kinetic term. The former modify the low-frequency area law, the high-frequency null-capture cross section, and the finite-frequency absorption spectra, whereas a pure $A_5$ deformation leaves the leading null-capture observable unchanged while remaining detectable in wave propagation. We further examine off-axis incidence, co-/counter-rotating contributions, and superradiant modes, where changes in $X(r_+)$ shift the horizon angular velocity and hence the superradiant threshold. Our results identify finite-frequency absorption as a wave-optics diagnostic that can probe radial propagation sectors inaccessible to both the area law and null geodesic capture observables, offering a new tool for strong-field tests of black hole geometry.

### [11] [Conformal Symmetry and Non-Singular Scalar field Collapse](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28246)
*Mohamed Aarif A,Soumya Chakrabarti*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文在广义相对论框架下，研究共形平坦球对称时空中大规模标量场的引力坍缩。通过精确解析解，发现坍缩在有限本征时间内不会形成壳聚焦奇点；自相似解在包含耗散效应时才成立，且坍缩过程中Misner-Sharp质量因能量向外输运而单调递减。标量场满足零能量条件，而有效流体部分则违背零能量条件和强能量条件，表现出有效奇异物质行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解引力坍缩过程中奇点的形成条件，特别是壳聚焦奇点（shell-focusing singularity）的可避免性，以及在共形平坦对称性约束下寻找精确解。

Method: 采用共形平坦、球对称时空几何，通过Weyl张量（Weyl tensor）为零的条件约束时空；利用最小耦合的均匀标量场（scalar field）结合理想流体（perfect fluid）和耗散物质（dissipative matter）作为坍缩物质模型；求解场方程得到可分共形因子形式的精确解析解，并分析自相似解（self-similar solution）与同宿对称性（homothetic symmetry）的兼容性。

Result: 非耗散情况下存在连续坍缩的精确解，可光滑匹配到外部Schwarzschild时空，坍缩渐进进行，有限本征时间内不出现壳聚焦奇点。自相似解在仅有理想流体时不存在，加入径向热流（radial heat flux）形式的耗散效应后得以实现，并需匹配外部Vaidya时空；该过程中Misner-Sharp质量单调递减。两类解的固有半径始终有限，避免壳聚焦奇点。标量场满足零能量条件（null energy condition），有效流体部分违背零能量条件和强能量条件（strong energy condition）。

Conclusion: 在共形平坦对称性下，标量场引力坍缩可以在不形成壳聚焦奇点的情况下进行；自相似坍缩依赖于耗散机制；有效流体成分表现出奇异物质（exotic matter）行为，可能对奇点避免机制有重要启示。

Abstract: We investigate the gravitational collapse of a massive scalar field in a conformally flat, spherically symmetric spacetime within general relativity. The collapsing matter distribution is modeled using a minimally coupled homogeneous scalar field together with both perfect fluid and dissipative matter sectors. Imposing conformal flatness through the vanishing of the Weyl tensor considerably constrains the geometry and enables the construction of exact analytical solutions. In the non-dissipative case, the field equations admit a separable conformal factor leading to a continuously collapsing configuration smoothly matched to an exterior Schwarzschild spacetime. The collapse proceeds asymptotically and does not develop a shell-focusing singularity within finite proper time. We further examine the possibility of self-similar evolution associated with homothetic symmetry. It is shown that self-similar solutions are incompatible with a perfect-fluid configuration alone, but become consistent when dissipative effects in the form of a radial heat flux are included. The resulting self-similar collapse must be matched to an exterior Vaidya spacetime and exhibits a monotonically decreasing Misner-Sharp mass due to outward energy transport. For both classes of solutions, the proper radius remains finite throughout the evolution, preventing the formation of shell-focusing singularities within the considered domain. The scalar field sector satisfies the null energy condition for the potentials studied, while the effective fluid sector exhibits violations of the null and strong energy conditions, indicating the emergence of effective exotic matter behavior.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 基于后反应（backreacted）的复标量场（complex scalar field）模型，该标量场与爱因斯坦引力（Einstein gravity）最小耦合（minimally coupled），并处于反演宇称激发态。通过薄盘成像（thin-disk imaging）方法，分析不同毛发强度和观测角度下的透镜结构。

Result: 在弱毛发区（weak-hair regime），黑洞行为接近标准Kerr黑洞。随着毛发强度增大，光子环（photon ring）和阴影（shadow）区域收缩且畸变加剧。在强毛发区（strong-hair regime）出现多重不连续阴影分量、新月形结构和混沌透镜（chaotic lensing）信号；近边缘观测角度下，赤道多次穿越产生嵌套环状图案（nested ring-like patterns）。

Conclusion: 激发态标量毛发的存在会在黑洞成像中产生可辨识的几何特征，强毛发区的新透镜结构可作为此类黑洞的潜在观测信号。

Abstract: We investigate thin-disk imaging of Kerr black holes with synchronized scalar hair, focusing on backreacted parity-odd excited states of a complex scalar field minimally coupled to Einstein gravity. The spacetime displays a core-double-torus lensing structure, with a central black hole surrounded by two scalar clouds. We study the dependence of the images on hair strength and viewing angle, identifying a weak-hair regime close to Kerr. With increasing hair, the photon ring and shadow region shrink and become more distorted. In the strong-hair regime, gravitational lensing produces new features, including multiple disconnected shadow components, crescent-shaped structures, and signatures of chaotic lensing. For nearly edge-on viewing angles, repeated equatorial crossings generate nested ring-like patterns. These results highlight possible geometric signatures of black holes with excited scalar hair.

### [13] [Universal thermodynamic topological classes of the charged dRGT black string](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28523)

TL;DR: 本文通过正则系综（canonical ensemble）和巨正则系综（grand canonical ensemble）研究了带电dRGT黑洞弦（charged dRGT black string）的普适热力学拓扑分类（universal thermodynamic topological classes），发现最外分支在两种系综下均稳定，最内分支在正则系综中稳定（W^{1+}）但在巨正则系综中不稳定（W^{0-}），并指出引力效应被忽略时电荷不改变拓扑分类，而dRGT有质量引力与电磁场的耦合是产生非平凡热力学拓扑的关键。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 分别在正则系综和巨正则系综框架下分析带电dRGT黑洞弦的热力学拓扑分类，并考察其在极限参数区间下的渐近行为，通过对不同分支的拓扑类别（W^{1+}与W^{0-}）进行对比来确定系综依赖性和耦合效应。

Result: 最外层大黑洞弦分支在两种系综下均保持热力学稳定；最内层小黑洞弦分支在正则系综中稳定（W^{1+}），在巨正则系综中不稳定（W^{0-}）；在引力效应被忽略的极限下，电荷贡献不改变拓扑分类。

Conclusion: 系综选择对带电dRGT黑洞弦的热力学构型有显著影响；dRGT有质量引力与电磁场的耦合是产生非平凡热力学拓扑的必要条件，研究结果有助于深入理解黑洞弦热力学并为量子引力探索提供新理论依据。

Abstract: In this study, we explore universal thermodynamic topological classes of charged dRGT black string within both the canonical ensemble and grand canonical ensemble frameworks, and further analyze its asymptotic behavior under limiting parameter regimes. We demonstrate that, while the outermost large black string branch remains thermodynamically stable in both ensembles, the innermost small black string branch exhibits distinctly different stability properties: it is stable in the canonical ensemble but becomes thermodynamically unstable in the grand canonical ensemble, corresponding to the $W^{1+}$ and $W^{0-}$ topological categories,respectively.These findings demonstrate that the selection of thermodynamic ensemble has a significant influence on the thermodynamic configuration of the charged dRGT black string. In the limit where gravitational effects are neglected, the charge contribution does not modify the underlying topological classification. This implies that the coupling between dRGT massive gravity and the electromagnetic sector is essential for the emergence of nontrivial thermodynamic topology.These results contribute to a deeper understanding of the black string thermodynamics and provide a novel theoretical basis for exploring the basic properties of quantum gravity.

### [14] [New asymptotically flat gravitational instanton](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28542)
*Edward Teo*

TL;DR: 本文通过对称性和正则性条件，从欧几里得双Kerr-NUT解中识别出一个新的双参数渐近平直环面引力瞬子，它是Li和Sun证明存在的无穷序列中的第三个，也是首个非厄米特（non-Hermitian）的里奇平坦（Ricci-flat）引力瞬子。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 将欧几里得双Kerr-NUT解作为起点，对其杆结构（rod structure）施加对称性和正则性条件，除一个化为五次多项式（fifth-order polynomial）的条件外，其余条件均显式求解。

Result: 该引力瞬子是双参数的（two-parameter），具有欧拉数（Euler number）χ=4和赫兹布鲁赫符号（Hirzebruch signature）τ=0，其全局拓扑（global topology）为$\mathbb{C}P^2\#\overline{\mathbb{C}P^2}$并适当移除一个圆$S^1$。该解是Li和Sun序列中的第三个，前两个分别为Kerr瞬子和Chen–Teo瞬子。

Conclusion: 该引力瞬子是首个已知的非厄米特里奇平坦引力瞬子（Ricci-flat gravitational instanton that is not Hermitian），填补了该序列中的一个重要空白。

Abstract: A new two-parameter asymptotically flat (AF) toric gravitational instanton is identified as a special case of the Euclidean double Kerr-NUT solution, by imposing certain symmetry and regularity conditions on its rod structure. These conditions are solved explicitly, except for one which takes the form of a fifth-order polynomial. This gravitational instanton has Euler number $χ=4$ and Hirzebruch signature $τ=0$, and its global topology is $\mathbb{C}P^2\#\overline{\mathbb{C}P^2}$ with a circle $S^1$ removed appropriately. It is the third of an infinite sequence of AF toric gravitational instantons that was proved to exist by Li and Sun, the first two being the Kerr and Chen--Teo instantons. It is also the first known example of a Ricci-flat gravitational instanton that is not Hermitian.

### [15] [Perturbative dynamics and relativistic effects of a dyonic Kalb-Ramond black hole](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28580)
*A. A. Araújo Filho*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究了在洛伦兹破坏（Lorentz-violating）反对称张量背景下的双荷Kalb-Ramond黑洞的微扰动力学、潮汐效应和相对论频移，发现洛伦兹破坏参数主导了准正则频率的修正，而双荷电荷产生较温和的影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究洛伦兹破坏背景与双荷（dyonic）结构共同作用下黑洞的微扰动力学、潮汐效应和相对论频移，以理解这类非标准黑洞的观测特征。

Method: 通过分析径向信号交换的引力多普勒效应（gravitational Doppler effect）、自由落体参照系中的径向和角向潮汐力（tidal forces）、零测地线（null geodesics）的引力时间延迟（gravitational time delay），以及利用六阶WKB方法（WKB method）计算标量、矢量、张量和旋量有效势（effective potentials）的准正则频率（quasinormal frequencies）。

Result: 双荷电荷使红移减弱，频率比趋近于1；潮汐力拉伸与压缩模式反转的特征半径被确定；电磁荷相对于参考构型减小了时间延迟；洛伦兹破坏参数主导准正则频率修正，增大振荡频率并改变阻尼率，双荷电荷产生较温和的偏移；时域剖面（time-domain profiles）证实了阻尼准正则振荡（quasinormal ringing）及其后的晚期幂律拖尾（power-law tails）。

Conclusion: 洛伦兹破坏背景下的双荷Kalb-Ramond黑洞展现了区别于标准黑洞的引力频移和潮汐特征，且其准正则模谱主要由洛伦兹破坏参数控制，双荷电荷仅引起次级修正，为探测洛伦兹对称性破缺提供了潜在的引力波观测窗口。

Abstract: We investigate perturbative dynamics, tidal effects, and relativistic frequency shifts in a dyonic Kalb-Ramond black hole generated by a Lorentz-violating antisymmetric tensor background. The geometry is controlled by the mass $M$, the electric charge $Q$, the magnetic charge $p$, and the Lorentz-violating parameter $\ell$, with the dyonic sector entering through the effective combination $P_{\ell}^{2}=Q^{2}/(1-\ell)^{2}+p^{2}/(1-2\ell)$. First, we analyze the gravitational Doppler effect for radial signal exchange between freely falling and static observers, showing how the dyonic charges weaken the redshift by shifting the frequency ratio toward unity. We then compute the radial and angular tidal forces in a freely falling frame and determine the characteristic radii at which the usual stretching and compression patterns are reversed. The gravitational time delay is also evaluated for null trajectories, showing that the electric and magnetic sectors reduce the delay relative to the reference configuration. In the perturbative sector, we derive the scalar, vector, tensor, and spinor effective potentials and compute the corresponding quasinormal frequencies through the sixth-order WKB method. The numerical spectra indicate that the Lorentz-violating parameter gives the dominant correction, increasing the oscillation frequencies and modifying the damping rates, while the dyonic charges produce milder shifts. Finally, the time-domain profiles confirm the presence of damped quasinormal ringing followed by late-time power-law tails.

### [16] [Geometric Aharonov-Bohm phase effect around a black hole](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28582)
*Kaushlendra Kumar,Shahn Majid*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文在广义相对论（GR）框架下，将时空密度流（spacetime density flow）的测地线（geodesic）提升为一个具有密度|ψ|²的振幅ψ，通过一般协变量子力学（generally-covariant quantum mechanics）和Klein-Gordon算子在半经典分析中推导其来源，并展示其与Raychaudhuri方程的联系。进一步，该研究证明了在靠近黑洞的运动中，ψ的相位存在Aharonov-Bohm型效应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索广义相对论中时空密度流的测地线能否被推广为量子振幅ψ，并建立其与一般协变量子力学及半经典分析的关联，以揭示引力与量子理论之间的新联系。

Method: 采用半经典分析方法（semiclassical analysis），借助一般协变量子力学（generally-covariant quantum mechanics）和Klein-Gordon算子（Klein-Gordon operator），将时空密度流测地线提升为振幅ψ，并推导其与Raychaudhuri方程（Raychaudhuri equations）的联系。

Result: 成功将时空密度流的测地线升级为振幅ψ（密度为|ψ|²），建立了其与一般协变量子力学和Klein-Gordon算子的联系，并发现了在趋近黑洞的运动中存在Aharonov-Bohm型效应（Aharonov-Bohm type effect），即ψ的相位受到非平凡影响。

Conclusion: 广义相对论中的时空密度流测地线可以在量子框架下被自然升级为振幅ψ，且这一构造与半经典分析兼容；靠近黑洞时ψ的相位会出现Aharonov-Bohm型效应，为引力系统中的量子现象提供了新的理论可能性。

Abstract: In recent work, we have explored the novel possibility that the geodesic of a spacetime density flow in GR could be upgraded to an amplitude $ψ$ with density $|ψ|^2$. We show how this arises from generally-covariant quantum mechanics and the Klein-Gordon operator in a semiclassical analysis, and how it connects to the Raychaudhuri equations. In this setting, we demonstrate an Aharonov-Bohm type effect for the phase of $ψ$ in motion approaching a black hole.

</details>


### [17] [First-Order Perturbations of Covariant Maxwell Equations in Gravitational Waves](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28663)
*Lingyue Lou,Haorong Wu,Xi-Long Fan*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该论文构建了一个系统的理论框架，用于研究引力波（gravitational waves, GWs）诱导的一阶电磁（electromagnetic, EM）扰动，从协变麦克斯韦方程出发，推导了完整的扰动方程及电磁场与能动张量的一阶表达式，并定量分析了平面电磁波与引力波相互作用的强度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为引力波与电磁场之间的相互作用提供一个系统性的理论描述框架，填补现有研究中缺乏完整一阶扰动方程系统性推导的空白。

Method: 从协变形式的麦克斯韦方程（covariant Maxwell equations）出发，分别基于电磁场张量（EM field tensor）和四势（four-potential）推导完整的一阶扰动方程，并证明二者等价性及洛伦兹规范（Lorenz gauge）下的剩余规范不变性（residual gauge invariance）。随后在横向无迹规范（transverse-traceless gauge）下，以平面电磁波与引力波的相互作用作为显式算例进行解析评估。

Result: 一阶诱导电场和磁场及电磁能动张量（EM energy-momentum tensor）的显式表达式被给出；耦合系数（coupling coefficient）的最大模量级约为 $10^2$；对于典型天体物理引力波（无量纲应变量 $h_0 \sim 10^{-21}$），其一阶电磁响应相对于入射场振幅的量级约为 $10^{-19}$。

Conclusion: 论文定量地建立了引力波强度与一阶电磁响应之间的对应关系，表明引力波诱导的电磁扰动尽管极其微弱，但在理论上可以通过所构建的框架进行精确描述与评估。

Abstract: We present a systematic theoretical framework for investigating first-order electromagnetic (EM) perturbations induced by gravitational waves (GWs). Beginning with the covariant Maxwell equations, we derive the complete first-order perturbation equations in terms of both the EM field tensor and the four-potential, demonstrating their equivalence alongside the residual gauge invariance under the Lorenz gauge condition. Furthermore, explicit first-order expressions for the induced electric and magnetic fields, as well as the associated EM energy-momentum tensor, are obtained. As an explicit illustration, we analytically evaluate the interaction between a plane EM wave and a GW within the transverse-traceless gauge. By demonstrating that the maximum modulus of the coupling coefficient is on the order of $10^2$, we quantitatively establish that a typical astrophysical GW with a dimensionless strain of $h_0 \sim 10^{-21}$ generates a first-order EM response on the order of $10^{-19}$ relative to the incident field amplitude.

</details>


### [18] [Accurate waveforms for generic planar-orbit binary black holes: The multipolar effective-one-body model SEOBNRv6EHM](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28715)
*Aldo Gamboa,Alessandra Buonanno,Lorenzo Pompili,Raffi Enficiaud,Michael Boyle,Lawrence E. Kidder,Oliver Long,Peter James Nee,Harald P. Pfeiffer,Antoni Ramos-Buades,Mark A. Scheel*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文提出了SEOBNRv6EHM，一个基于有效单体（effective-one-body）框架的时域多极子引力波波形模型，适用于一般平面轨道上的致密双星系统，包含准圆轨道、偏心轨道、动力学俘获及散射过程。该模型通过新型重求和（resummation）技术提升了辐射反作用力与波形模式的精度，在高偏心率系统（偏心率高达约0.9）上实现了前所未有的精度（波形不匹配度低于或接近2%），且生成速度比现有最先进EOB偏心模型快2–6倍。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 从引力波（gravitational wave, GW）信号中精确推断致密双星参数需要高精度且计算高效的波形模型。轨道偏心率（orbital eccentricity）是识别致密双星动力学形成通道的关键指标，忽略偏心率会导致引力波分析中的系统性误差。因此，开发一个能准确描述偏心轨道且计算效率高的波形模型是当前引力波天文学中亟待解决的问题。

Method: 该模型基于有效单体（effective-one-body, EOB）框架构建，采用新型重求和（resummation）技术处理辐射反作用力（radiation-reaction force）与波形模式。模型提供(2,2)、(2,1)、(3,3)、(3,2)、(4,4)和(4,3)等多极子（multipole）波形，覆盖完整旋进–合并–铃宕（inspiral-merger-ringdown）过程以及动力学俘获（dynamical capture）和散射（scattering）过程。模型经过592个准圆（quasi-circular）、319个偏心、1个动力学俘获和2个散射的SXS数值相对论（numerical-relativity, NR）波形数据的校准与验证。

Result: 对于准圆和小偏心率双星系统，SEOBNRv6EHM的精度与上一代SEOBNRv5模型相当。对于高偏心率系统（偏心率高达约0.9），该模型实现了前所未有的精度，在20–200 M⊙总质量范围内，合并前14个近星点通过时刻的波形不匹配度（waveform mismatch）低于或接近2%。此外，波形生成耗时（walltime）比现有最先进EOB偏心模型快2–6倍。

Conclusion: SEOBNRv6EHM在保持与先前型号相当精度的同时，极大地扩展了对高偏心率系统的建模能力，并在计算效率上显著优于同类模型。该模型为引力波天文学中偏心率相关参数的高效、精确推断提供了有力工具。

Abstract: Accurate and computationally efficient waveform models are required to infer the parameters of compact binaries from their gravitational wave (GW) emission. Among these parameters, orbital eccentricity serves as a smoking gun for dynamical formation channels and must be accounted for to avoid systematic errors in GW analyses. Here, we present SEOBNRv6EHM, a time-domain, multipolar waveform model for binaries on generic planar orbits, calibrated to quasi-circular (QC) numerical-relativity (NR) simulations from the SXS collaboration. In addition to the dominant $(2,2)$ mode, the model provides the $(2,1)$, $(3,3)$, $(3,2)$, $(4,4)$, and $(4,3)$ multipoles for the full inspiral-merger-ringdown process of coalescing binaries, as well as for dynamical captures and scattering encounters. The model is built within the effective-one-body (EOB) framework, and it employs novel resummations of the radiation-reaction force and waveform modes. We validate its accuracy through comparisons against 592 QC, 319 eccentric, one dynamical-capture, and two scattering SXS NR waveforms, and through scattering-angle comparisons against 61 SXS NR simulations. For QC and small-eccentricity binaries, its accuracy is comparable to previous-generation SEOBNRv5 models. For highly eccentric systems, however, SEOBNRv6EHM attains unprecedented accuracy, with waveform mismatches remaining below or close to $ 2\% $ across the total mass range $ 20-200\, \mathrm{M}_\odot $ for eccentricities up to $\sim 0.9$ at 14 periastron passages before merger. Additionally, SEOBNRv6EHM achieves waveform-generation walltimes that are $ 2 - 6 $ times faster than other state-of-the-art EOB eccentric models, enabling efficient and accurate applications in GW astronomy.

</details>


### [19] [Eccentric and unbound compact binaries in the LIGO-Virgo-KAGRA catalog: parameter estimation and waveform systematics with SEOBNRv6EHM](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28716)
*Lorenzo Pompili,Aldo Gamboa,Alessandra Buonanno*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文使用SEOBNRv6EHM波形模型对致密双星系统的引力波数据进行参数估计（parameter estimation）分析，发现其在偏心度（eccentricity）、质量（masses）和自旋（spins）的估计上优于前代模型，并在LIGO–Virgo–KAGRA的26个引力波事件中识别出5个事件存在偏心度的弱支持证据，但对GW190521等高质量事件的直接捕获（direct-capture）解释虽不排除，但结果缺乏天体物理合理性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 轨道偏心率（orbital eccentricity）编码了致密双星形成通道和天体物理环境的关键信息，是引力波（gravitational-wave, GW）推断的重要目标，因此需要更精确的偏心波形模型进行参数估计。

Method: 使用SEOBNRv6EHM波形模型对偏心致密双星进行参数估计分析；采用高偏心率数值相对论波形（numerical-relativity waveforms）作为合成信号，比较当前最先进的偏心模型之间的参数恢复效果；并将该模型应用于LIGO–Virgo–KAGRA O1–O4运行期的26个引力波事件。

Result: SEOBNRv5EHM和TEOBResumS-Dalí在最困难的构型下会产生偏心度、质量和自旋的有偏估计（biased estimates），而SEOBNRv6EHM显著降低了这些偏差。在26个引力波事件中，有5个事件在偏心度上对准圆形进动自旋假说（quasi-circular precessing-spin hypothesis）表现出弱支持（Bayes因子$\log_{10} \mathcal{B}^{\text{EAS}}_{\text{QCP}} > 0.5$）。对三个高质事件如GW190521，直接捕获构型与偏心对齐自旋和准圆形进动自旋假说相当或略受偏好（$\log_{10}\mathcal{B}^{\rm unbound}_{\rm QCP} \approx 0.2$–$0.6$），但恢复的构型在天体物理上不现实，无法与高偏心束缚轨道区分。

Conclusion: SEOBNRv6EHM在参数估计分析中比SEOBNRv5EHM快约三倍，同时提高了波形精度，能够支持高效、大规模的使用偏心波形进行引力波推断；但关于GW190521等事件的非束缚起源（unbound origin），当前结果尚不能提供明确支持。

Abstract: Orbital eccentricity encodes key information about compact-binary formation channels and astrophysical environments, making it a critical target for gravitational-wave (GW) inference. We present parameter-estimation (PE) analyses of GWs from eccentric compact binaries with the SEOBNRv6EHM waveform model. Using long, highly eccentric numerical-relativity waveforms as synthetic signals, we compare parameter recovery across state-of-the-art eccentric models. We find that SEOBNRv5EHM and TEOBResumS-Dalí can yield biased estimates of eccentricity, masses, and spins in the most challenging configurations, while SEOBNRv6EHM significantly reduces these biases. Applying SEOBNRv6EHM to 26 GW events from the O1--O4 LIGO--Virgo--KAGRA observing runs -- including binary black hole, neutron-star--black-hole, and binary neutron-star mergers -- we identify five events with mild support for eccentricity over the quasi-circular precessing-spin hypothesis, with Bayes factors $\log_{10} \mathcal{B}^{\text{EAS}}_{\text{QCP}} > 0.5$. Since SEOBNRv6EHM is applicable to generic planar binaries, we reanalyze five high-mass events allowing for unbound initial conditions. For three of them -- including GW190521, previously claimed to originate from a dynamical capture -- a direct-capture configuration is comparable to, or marginally favored over, both the eccentric aligned-spin and quasi-circular precessing-spin hypotheses ($\log_{10}\mathcal{B}^{\rm unbound}_{\rm QCP} \approx 0.2$--$0.6$ for GW190521). The recovered configurations are, however, astrophysically unrealistic and cannot be confidently discriminated from highly eccentric bound orbits, so these results do not, by themselves, support an unbound origin for these events. SEOBNRv6EHM is approximately three times faster in PE analyses than SEOBNRv5EHM, while improving waveform accuracy, enabling efficient, large-scale GW inference with eccentric waveforms.

</details>


### [20] [Jacobson's thermodynamic approach to classical gravity applied to non-Riemannian geometries: remarks on the simplicity of Nature](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.00422)
*Jhan N. Martinez,Jose F. Rodriguez-Ruiz,Yeinzon Rodriguez*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文探讨了Jacobson的热力学-引力对应方法从黎曼几何（Riemannian geometry）向非黎曼几何（non-Riemannian geometry）的推广。研究发现，除黎曼情形外，仅由爱因斯坦-希尔伯特作用量导出的引力理论并非自然选择的候选理论；结合Lanczos-Lovelock引力理论假设，非黎曼无非度量性情形下，包含挠率矢量平方项的爱因斯坦-希尔伯特作用量理论被识别为自然选择的理论；但在完整非黎曼情形下两种方法互不兼容。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Jacobson（1993）提出了一个引人入胜的方法，将经典引力场方程视为Rindler观测者所经历的热力学第一定律的推论。该方法原初针对黎曼几何（Riemannian geometry）表述，本文旨在探究其在非黎曼几何（non-Riemannian geometry）中的推广后果。

Method: 将Jacobson的热力学推导方法从黎曼几何推广至非黎曼几何；同时引入Lanczos-Lovelock引力理论（Lanczos-Lovelock theories of gravity）的假设条件，共同约束可能的引力理论形式。区分了非度量性（non metricity）为零与完整非黎曼几何两种情形，并分别考察了能量-动量张量（energy-momentum tensor）采用度规版本（metric version）与规范版本（canonical version）时的结论。

Result: 从爱因斯坦-希尔伯特作用量（Einstein-Hilbert action）导出的理论——“最简单的理论”——除黎曼情形外，不属于自然界可供选择的引力理论集合。在无非度量性的非黎曼情形下，当能量-动量张量采用度规版本时，爱因斯-希尔伯特作用量加上一个挠率矢量（torsion vector）平方项的理论被两种方法共同指向为自然选择的理论。但当能量-动量张量采用规范版本时，或在完整非黎曼情形下，两种方法互不兼容。

Conclusion: Jacobson的热力学方法在黎曼几何与非黎曼几何中指向不同的引力理论。仅在无挠率时退化为黎曼情形的条件下，标准广义相对论才被恢复。更广泛的非黎曼情形下，热力学方法与Lanczos-Lovelock假设之间的不一致性表明，需要进一步探索完整的非黎曼引力理论的选择机制。

Abstract: Three decades ago, Ted Jacobson surprised us with a very appealing approach to classical gravity. According to him, the gravitational field equations are the consequence of the first law of thermodynamics applied to a Rindler observer. Jacobson's approach being formulated for Riemannian geometries, we have wondered what its consequences would be for non-Riemannian geometries. The results of our quest have been particularly appealing: we have found that the theory that derives from the Einstein-Hilbert action, arguably ``the simplest one'', does not belong to the pool of gravitational theories available for Nature's selection (except in the Riemannian case). In the search of a unique alternative, we have considered the hypotheses employed in the formulation of the Lanczos-Lovelock theories of gravity. Together, the two approaches point towards the theory that derives from the Einstein-Hilbert action plus a term quadratic in the torsion vector as the one that would be selected by Nature in the non-Riemannian case without non metricity (when the energy-momentum tensor is identified as its metric version). The same strategy cannot be followed in the full non-Riemannian case (and in the previous case when the energy-momentum tensor is identified as its canonical version) as the two approaches are mutually inconsistent.

</details>

### [21] [Existence of nonrelativistic $\ell$- and multi-$\ell$-boson stars and their radial stability](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27529)
*Emmanuel Chávez Nambo,Olivier Sarbach*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文通过变分法（calculus of variations）的直接方法，证明了多场薛定谔-泊松系统（multi-field Schrödinger-Poisson system）中存在无穷多类球对称解，并进一步证明了这些解在特定函数集内具有轨道稳定性（orbital stability）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多场薛定谔-泊松系统是描述自引力背景下多个量子波函数相互作用的数学模型，其解的存在性与稳定性是量子力学与引力交叉领域的重要问题。现有方法在构造高阶或无穷类球对称解方面存在局限，因此需要发展新的变分框架来证明此类解的存在性。

Method: 采用变分法的直接方法，将能量泛函（energy functional）限制在Sobolev空间$H^1$中具有旋转群（rotation group）表示不变性的向量值波函数（vector-valued wave functions）集合上，并约束各分量的$L^2$范数固定，进而证明该泛函在该约束集上存在全局最小值（global minimum）。

Result: 成功证明存在无穷多类球对称解（spherically-symmetric solutions）；这些由全局最小值对应的解在所述函数集内对波函数的扰动具有轨道稳定性；此外，文中还讨论了包含外势（external potential）的推广情形及最小值的一些重要性质。

Conclusion: 本文建立的变分框架为多场薛定谔-泊松系统提供了一类新的球对称解及其稳定性保证，拓展了该系统的可解结构，并为后续研究含外势情形下的解性质奠定了理论基础。

Abstract: Using direct methods of the calculus of variations we establish the existence of an infinite class of spherically-symmetric solutions to the multi-field Schrödinger-Poisson system. This is achieved by proving that the energy functional admits a global minimum when restricted to the set of vector-valued wave functions in the Sobolev space $H^1$ which are invariant with respect to a suitable representation of the rotation group and whose components have fixed $L^2$-norms. Additionally, we show that these minima correspond to solutions which are orbital stable with respect to perturbations of the wave function within this set. The generalization to include an external potential and some important properties of the minima are also discussed.

</details>


### [22] [WKB Spectral Asymptotics for a One-Dimensional Dirac Operator with a Slowly Varying Mass Profile](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27592)
*Owen Sutton,Alexander B. Watson*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究了一维狄拉克算符（Dirac operator）在半经典框架下的谱理论，通过修正的玻尔-索末菲量子化条件（Bohr-Sommerfeld quantization condition）揭示了赝自旋指数（pseudo-spin index）导致的半整数偏移，从而恢复拓扑保护的零模（topologically protected zero mode），并通过精确可解势和数值计算验证了理论结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在拓扑不同介质界面处的波传播问题中，狄拉克算符的谱理论对于理解拓扑保护态至关重要；现有标准WKB量子化条件未能正确描述赝自旋自由度的影响，因此需要发展修正的半经典理论以恢复拓扑零模。

Method: 对一维狄拉克算符的平方算符（squared operator）进行系统性的形式化WKB（Wentzel–Kramers–Brillouin）构造，推导出修正的玻尔-索末菲量子化条件；通过精确可解的Pöschl–Teller势验证解析结果，并结合数值计算确认特征值与特征函数向WKB近似的收敛性。

Result: 推导出的修正量子化条件与标准结果的区别在于一个依赖于赝自旋指数的半整数偏移（half-integer shift），该偏移能够恢复拓扑保护的零模；在Pöschl–Teller势下的精确解和数值计算均验证了该WKB近似的正确性与收敛性。

Conclusion: 修正的Bohr-Sommerfeld量子化条件成功将赝自旋自由度纳入半经典框架，为拓扑界面态提供了统一的半经典描述，数值结果支持该方法的有效性。

Abstract: We study the semiclassical spectral theory of a one-dimensional Dirac operator describing waves at the interface between topologically distinct media. We derive a modified Bohr-Sommerfeld quantization condition for the squared operator via a systematic formal WKB construction producing approximate eigenpairs. Our result differs from the standard result by the half-integer shift depending on the pseudo-spin index which allows for recovering the topologically protected zero mode. We verify our result for the solvable Pöschl--Teller potential and provide numerical computations confirming the convergence of eigenvalues and eigenfunctions to their WKB approximations.

</details>


### [23] [Exact solution for a periodically driven magnetic multilayer system](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27638)
*P. I. Naumkin,A. V. Nikolaev,L. L. Tao,M. Ye. Zhuravlev*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文针对具有时间相关势（尤其旋转磁化）的量子系统，以双层磁多层结构为例，构建了含任意有限项的解，并指出旋转磁化情况下无法直接推广稳态边界条件。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管Floquet工程（Floquet engineering）为周期性驱动下控制物理系统性质提供了通用理论框架，但在具体问题（如含时间相关势的磁多层结构）中，由于双分量波函数和界面匹配条件的存在，分析面临显著困难。

Method: 以包含旋转磁化层的双层磁系统为例，构造了一类含有任意有限项数的解，并对解的结构进行了分析。

Result: 得到了含任意有限项的解析解结构；证明了在旋转磁化情况下，那些看似自然的稳态边界条件（boundary conditions）推广形式无法施加。

Conclusion: 周期性驱动下磁多层结构的边界条件问题比稳态情形更为复杂，标准边界条件不能直接推广至旋转磁化情形。

Abstract: Periodic driving serves as an effective method for controlling the properties of physical systems. Called "Floquet engineering," it is a broad field of theoretical and experimental activity. Whereas original Floquet theory was proposed to a system of ordinary differential equations, the quantum systems with time-dependent potential require using partial differential equations. Among different methods of analysis of such systems, time series is a most common one. Though general scheme was developed in a number of works, its application to specific problems often faces significant difficulties. In particular, the class of the problems describing magnetic multilayers with time-dependent potential (e.g., rotating magnetization of some of the layers) leads to significant complication of the problem due to two-component wave function and matching conditions at the interfaces. Taking as an example a two-layer system containing magnetic layer with rotating magnetization, we construct a class of solution containing arbitrary but finite number of the terms. The structure of the solution is analyzed. In particular, we show that boundary conditions, which seem a natural generalization of that for a stationary problem, cannot be imposed in the case of rotating magnetizations.

</details>


### [24] [Existence and Uniqueness of Irregular Vectors of Integer and Half-Integer Ranks for the Virasoro Algebra](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28002)
*Hajime Nagoya*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文基于Virasoro微分算子（Virasoro differential operators）建立了一个代数框架，首次严格证明了任意整数和半整数阶（rank）的Virasoro代数不规则向量（irregular vectors）的存在性与唯一性定理，为构造高阶不规则共形块（irregular conformal blocks）提供了代数基础。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管Virasoro代数的不规则向量在现代数学物理中被广泛使用，但文献中一直缺乏任意阶下的严格存在性与唯一性定理。本文旨在填补这一理论空白。

Method: 基于参数空间上的Virasoro微分算子建立代数框架；从截断Virasoro实现（truncated Virasoro realization）的矢量场部分的系数矩阵构造规范算子\(L_*\)；该算子通过分离对最高不规则参数（highest irregular parameter）的导数来封闭递归系统，从而证明存在唯一性。

Result: 证明了任意整数阶形式不规则向量（formal irregular vectors）的存在性与唯一性；构造了半整数阶设定所需的截断Virasoro矢量场，并证明了相应半整数阶形式不规则向量的存在性与唯一性。

Conclusion: 这些结果为从高阶不规则向量构造不规则共形块提供了严格的代数基础。

Abstract: Although irregular vectors for the Virasoro algebra are widely used in modern mathematical physics, a rigorous existence and uniqueness theorem in arbitrary rank has not been available in the literature. In this paper, we develop an algebraic framework, based on Virasoro differential operators on the parameter space, which gives such a theorem for arbitrary integer and half-integer ranks. A key ingredient is the construction of a canonical operator \(L_*\) from the coefficient matrix of the vector-field part of a truncated Virasoro realization. This operator closes the recursive system by isolating the derivative with respect to the highest irregular parameter. Using this mechanism, we prove the existence and uniqueness of formal irregular vectors of arbitrary integer rank. We then construct the truncated Virasoro vector fields required in the half-integer rank setting and prove the existence and uniqueness of the corresponding half-integer rank formal irregular vectors. These results provide an algebraic foundation for the rigorous construction of irregular conformal blocks built from higher-rank irregular vectors.

</details>

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究具有多个守恒量的随机五邻居元胞自动机（stochastic 5-neighbor cellular automaton）的稳态分布与平均流特性，并从随机系统出发恢复确定性极限下的已知结果。

Method: 通过分析关联转移矩阵（transition matrix）的特征值问题（eigenvalue problem），推导各不可约分量（irreducible component）上稳态分布（stationary distribution）的显式公式，其中构型权重由两种局部模式出现次数表示，并利用该表达式理论推导平均流对守恒量的依赖关系。

Result: 获得了稳态分布的显式解析表达式，建立了平均流与守恒量之间的理论依赖关系，并在零噪声极限（zero-noise limit）下成功恢复了确定性情形下的平均流公式。

Conclusion: 该分析为具有多个守恒量的随机元胞自动机提供了精确的稳态分布解析解，并揭示了随机系统与确定性系统之间的极限对应关系。

Abstract: We analyze a stochastic 5-neighbor cellular automaton with several conserved quantities, including the particle density. By examining the eigenvalue problem of the associated transition matrix, we derive an explicit formula for the stationary distribution on each irreducible component, in which the weight of each configuration is expressed in terms of the numbers of occurrences of two specific local patterns. This analysis further allows us to theoretically derive the dependence of the mean flux on the conserved quantities. In particular, we recover the mean flux formula in the deterministic case by taking the zero-noise limit of the system.

### [26] [Dissipative Spectral Form Factor of the Complex Elliptic Ginibre Ensemble across Various Non-Hermiticity Regimes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28319)
*Gernot Akemann,Sung-Soo Byun,Seungjoon Oh*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本研究分析了复杂椭圆Ginibre系综中耗散谱形状因子（DSFF）在复时间下的渐近行为，推导了其非连通与连通分量的精确表达式，刻画了dip-ramp-plateau结构及相图，并识别出从非厄米到厄米随机矩阵行为过渡的介观标度区间。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 耗散谱形状因子（dissipative spectral form factor, DSFF）是理解非厄米随机矩阵谱关联的重要量，但其在不同标度参数下的渐近行为尚未被完整刻画，尤其是从非厄米到厄米体系过渡的介观标度区域缺乏系统分析。

Method: 考虑复椭圆Ginibre系综（complex elliptic Ginibre ensemble），其非厄米参数（non-Hermiticity parameter）τ∈[0,1)。在矩阵维度N→∞下，对时间变量T和非厄米参数1-τ分别引入标度T=O(N^γ)和1-τ=O(N^{-α})，在全部γ≥0、α≥0的标度区间内推导DSFF的断开分量（disconnected component）与连通分量（connected component）的渐近行为。

Result: 精确刻画了dip-ramp-plateau结构，包括dip time和Heisenberg time；识别出介观标度区间（mesoscopic regime）α∈(0,1)，该区间插值了非厄米随机矩阵DSFF与厄米系综谱形状因子（spectral form factor, SFF）之间的行为；给出了完整的相图（phase diagram），其中ramp部分依据标度参数呈现二次、线性或中间行为。

Conclusion: 本研究完整刻画了复杂椭圆Ginibre系综DSFF在所有标度参数下的渐近行为，揭示了非厄米随机矩阵谱关联中从非厄米到厄米过渡的介观标度机制，为理解耗散量子系统的谱统计提供了系统理论框架。

Abstract: We study the dissipative spectral form factor (DSFF) at complex time $T e^{iθ}$ for the complex elliptic Ginibre ensemble with non-Hermiticity parameter $τ\in [0,1)$. As the matrix dimension $N \to \infty$, we consider the natural scalings in both the time variable and the non-Hermiticity parameter, namely $T = O(N^γ)$ and $1 - τ= O(N^{-α})$. For all regimes $γ\ge 0$ and $α\ge 0$, we derive the precise asymptotic behaviour of both the disconnected and connected components of the DSFF. In particular, we explicitly characterise the dip--ramp--plateau structure, including the dip time and the Heisenberg time. In addition, we identify the mesoscopic regime $α\in (0,1)$, which interpolates between the behaviour of the DSFF of non-Hermitian random matrices and the spectral form factor (SFF) of Hermitian ensembles. We further provide an explicit description of the phase diagram, in which the ramp exhibits quadratic, linear, or intermediate behaviour depending on the scaling parameters.

### [28] [Purified Projection Method and Uhlmann Fidelity for Mixed Hartree Dynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28685)
*Hao Liang,Zhenfu Wang*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文针对混合哈特里（Hartree）数据，提出了投影方法的纯化与保真度（fidelity）表述，证明了在平方乌尔曼保真度（squared Uhlmann fidelity）和迹范数（trace norm）下所有固定边缘的定量传播混沌（quantitative propagation of chaos），论证适用于满足投影平方有界条件的奇异相互作用（包括L^{2r}相互作用和库仑势）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 对于混合哈特里（Hartree）数据的平均场演化，需要一种严格的投影方法来量化传播混沌（propagation of chaos）的速率，尤其是对奇异相互作用（如库仑势）的情形。

Method: 采用纯化和保真度（fidelity）重新表述投影方法；在纯化单粒子空间中使用秩为1的皮克尔型计数估计（rank-one Pickl-type counting estimate）；利用部分迹下保真度的单调性回到物理变量；通过福克斯–范德格拉夫不等式（Fuchs--van de Graaf inequality）从保真度结果导出迹范数界。

Result: 对所有固定边缘（fixed marginals）证明了定量的传播混沌（quantitative propagation of chaos），保真度结果适用于满足投影平方有界条件（projected-square bound）的奇异相互作用，包括L^{2r}相互作用和库仑势（Coulomb potential）。

Conclusion: 本文建立的纯化-保真度框架将投影方法的适用范围从正则相互作用推广到奇异相互作用，为平均场极限的定量分析提供了新工具。

Abstract: We give a purification and fidelity formulation of the projection method for mixed Hartree data. For the mean-field evolution of $N$-particle density matrices, we prove quantitative propagation of chaos for all fixed marginals, first in squared Uhlmann fidelity and then in trace norm via the Fuchs--van de Graaf inequality. The argument applies a rank-one Pickl-type counting estimate in a purified one-particle space and uses monotonicity of fidelity under partial trace to return to the physical variables. The result allows singular interactions satisfying a projected-square bound, including $L^{2r}$ interactions and the Coulomb potential.

</details>

### [29] [Exceptional points in diamond optomechanics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27536)
*Waleed El-Sayed,Elham Zohari,Joe Itoi,Peyman Parsa,Gustavo de Oliveira Luiz,Joseph E. Losby,Misa Hayashida,Marek Malac,Paul E. Barclay*

Main category: physics.optics

TL;DR: 本文在金刚石光机晶体（diamond optomechanical crystal）中实现了一个奇异点（exceptional point），该奇异点位于声子激射阈值（phonon-lasing threshold）之下的稳定工作窗口内，并观测到杂化模间光机械阻尼与反阻尼的不对称重新分布。这项工作确立了金刚石光机晶体作为非厄米光力学（non-Hermitian optomechanics）平台的地位，为混合自旋-声子界面（hybrid spin-phonon interface）中的拓扑力学动力学（topological mechanical dynamics）开辟了道路。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多模腔光机系统（multimode cavity optomechanical systems）能使光耦合原本无相互作用的力学谐振子，从而实现奇异点等非厄米现象，而奇异点的获取是迈向手性模式动力学（chiral mode dynamics）与拓扑态转移（topological state transfer）的第一步。金刚石光机器件虽具备实现奇异点所需的强相干光机械耦合以及对自旋缺陷的应变耦合能力，但此前尚未被用于多模非厄米物理学研究。

Method: 利用金刚石光机晶体中的结构对称性破缺（structural symmetry breaking），产生两个高频力学共振模（high-frequency mechanical resonances），使其与一个光学腔（optical cavity）耦合，从而调谐至奇异点。

Result: 奇异点在声子激射阈值之下的稳定工作窗口内达到；实验观察到杂化模之间光机械阻尼（optomechanical damping）与反阻尼（anti-damping）的不对称重新分布。

Conclusion: 本研究确立了金刚石光机晶体作为非厄米光力学平台的有效性，为在混合自旋-声子界面中实现拓扑力学动力学提供了新途径。

Abstract: Multimode cavity optomechanical systems allow light to couple otherwise non-interacting mechanical resonators, enabling non-Hermitian phenomena such as exceptional points, where eigenfrequencies and eigenvectors of coupled modes coalesce. Accessing an exceptional point and its nearby parameter space is a first step towards chiral mode dynamics and topological state transfer. Diamond optomechanical devices support strong coherent optomechanical coupling required to tune resonances to an exceptional point, as well as strain-coupling to spin-defects for hybrid quantum technologies, but have not yet been used for multimode non-Hermitian physics. Here we tune to an exceptional point in a diamond optomechanical crystal, which uses structural symmetry breaking to produce two high-frequency mechanical resonances coupled to an optical cavity. The exceptional point is reached within a stable operating window below the phonon-lasing threshold, and we observe asymmetric redistribution of optomechanical damping and anti-damping between hybridized modes. These results establish diamond optomechanical crystals as a platform for non-Hermitian optomechanics, opening routes to topological mechanical dynamics in hybrid spin-phonon interfaces.

</details>


### [30] [Orbital Altermagnetic Photonic Crystal](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28656)
*Sichang Qiu,Huichang Li,Yan Meng,Xiang Xi,Zebin Zhu,Ce Shang,Zhen Gao,Tie Jun Cui,Shuo Liu*

Main category: physics.optics

TL;DR: 本文首次实验实现了一种轨道交变磁性（orbital altermagnetic）光子晶体，基于反幺正 $C_{4z}\mathcal{T}$ 对称性，展示了动量依赖的自旋劈裂和赝自旋选择性电磁波输运，将交变磁性（altermagnetism）拓展至光子学领域。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 交变磁性（altermagnetism）在电子系统中展现出动量依赖的自旋劈裂（momentum-dependent spin splitting）且无净磁化，有望扩展自旋电子学（spintronics）的应用。然而，由于费米子电子与玻色子光子之间的根本差异，交变磁性的光子学实现一直是一个严峻挑战。

Method: 作者基于反幺正（antiunitary）$C_{4z}\mathcal{T}$ 对称性所强制对应的局域 $p$ 轨道 $σ/π$ 双重态与晶体动量（crystal momentum）之间的关系，设计并制备了一种轨道交变磁性（orbital altermagnetic）光子晶体。

Result: 实验测得的能带结构（band structure）和等频轮廓（iso-frequency contour）证实该系统具有动量依赖的自旋劈裂、交替的赝自旋极化（pseudospin polarization）以及 $d_{xy}$-波形式因子（$d_{xy}$-wave form factor）。此外，该光子晶体支持独特的赝自旋选择性电磁波输运，包括光子赝自旋劈裂（photonic pseudospin splitting）和赝自旋滤波（pseudospin filtering）。

Conclusion: 该工作将交变磁性拓展至光子学系统，为设计自旋光子学（spinphotonics）器件开辟了新途径。

Abstract: Altermagnetism features momentum-dependent spin splitting without net magnetization, extending spintronics beyond conventional ferromagnetism and antiferromagnetism. However, the photonic realization of altermagnetism has remained a formidable challenge due to the fundamental differences between fermionic electrons and bosonic photons. Here, we report the first experimental realization of an orbital altermagnetic photonic crystal, based on an antiunitary $C_{4z}\mathcal{T}$ symmetry enforced correspondence between a local $p$-orbital $σ/π$ doublet and crystal momentum. We experimentally demonstrate that the resulting system exhibits momentum-dependent spin splitting with alternating pseudospin polarization and a $d_{xy}$-wave form factor, as confirmed by measured band structures and iso-frequency contours. Moreover, we show that the orbital altermagnetic photonic crystal supports unique pseudospin-selective transport of electromagnetic waves, including photonic pseudospin splitting and pseudospin filtering. Our results extend the field of alternagnetism to photonic systems, opening a new avenue for designing spinphotonic devices.

### [31] [Search for light scalar particles produced in Higgs boson decays in exclusive final states with two muons and two hadrons in proton-proton collisions at $\sqrt{s}$ = 13 TeV](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27875)
*CMS Collaboration*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 该论文报告了利用CMS探测器在大型强子对撞机（LHC）上收集的质子-质子对撞数据，对希格斯玻色子（Higgs boson）衰变至一对轻标量粒子（scalar particle）的搜索。标量粒子质量在0.4–2.0 GeV范围，衰变长度（cτ）可达100 mm，最终态包含一对缪子（muon）和一对带电强子（charged kaon或pion）。基于138 fb⁻¹的13 TeV数据，对希格斯玻色子衰变至标量粒子的分支比上限达到了∼10⁻⁴量级。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有理论中，许多超出标准模型（Standard Model, SM）的新物理模型预测存在质量在GeV量级的轻标量粒子，希格斯玻色子可能衰变至这些粒子。此前实验对该质量区域（0.4–2.0 GeV）的覆盖有限，尤其是对涉及强子衰变（hadronic decay）的通道灵敏度不足。

Method: 利用CMS实验在2016–2018年收集的质子-质子对撞数据（质心能量13 TeV，积分亮度138 fb⁻¹），搜索希格斯玻色子衰变至一对相同标量粒子（prompt或long-lived）。标量粒子质量范围为0.4–2.0 GeV，其衰变产物为两个缪子或一对带电强子（kaon或pion），这些粒子可能产生于对撞顶点或偏离顶点（displaced）。实验终态特征为紧致的双缪子对和双带电强子对。

Result: 对希格斯玻色子衰变至轻标量粒子的分支比（branching fraction）给出了上限，量级为∼10⁻⁴。该上限覆盖多个标量粒子质量（0.4–2.0 GeV），对衰变长度（proper decay length）在∼1 mm以内的信号尤为敏感。

Conclusion: 该分析显著提升了对极轻标量玻色子质量的探测灵敏度，并展示了一种探测轻标量粒子强子衰变的新方法。所得分支比上限为相关新物理模型提供了重要约束。

Abstract: A search for new scalar particles of $\mathcal{O}$(GeV) mass in exclusive final states with muons and light hadrons is presented. The analysis uses proton-proton collision data produced at a center-of-mass energy of 13 TeV collected by the CMS experiment at the CERN LHC in 201$-$2018, corresponding to an integrated luminosity of 138 fb$^{-1}$. The search targets exotic decays of the Higgs boson to a pair of prompt or long-lived identical scalar particles with proper decay lengths $cτ$ up to 100 mm and masses within the range of 0.4$-$2.0 GeV. This mass window corresponds to a unique parameter space where hadronic decays of these particles mostly result in a pair of light hadrons. The considered experimental signature is a collimated pair of muons and another pair of charged kaons or pions, each of which may be prompt or displaced. The analysis improves the sensitivity to very light scalar boson masses and demonstrates a novel approach to probe hadronic decays of light scalar bosons. Upper limits on the branching fraction of the Higgs boson to scalar bosons at the level of $\mathcal{O}$(10$^{-4}$) are obtained for several scalar boson masses between 0.4 and 2.0 GeV, with proper decay lengths of up to $\sim$1 mm.

</details>


### [32] [Search for pair-produced vector-like $T$-quarks decaying into $Ht$ final states in the lepton-plus-jets channel in $pp$ collisions at $\sqrt{s}$=13 TeV with the ATLAS detector](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28538)
*The ATLAS Collaboration*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 本文基于ATLAS探测器在13 TeV质心能量下收集的139 fb⁻¹质子-质子对撞数据，搜索成对产生的矢量类T夸克（vector-like T-quark）。在T→Ht衰变通道中，通过可变半径重聚簇射流（variable-radius reclustered jets）和神经网络区分信号与标准模型本底，未发现显著超出，并在95%置信水平下给出了T夸克的质量下限（1.40–1.66 TeV）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 矢量类夸克（vector-like quark）是许多超越标准模型（Beyond Standard Model, BSM）理论预言的粒子，其电弱相互作用不同于手征性夸克，可能解释希格斯玻色子质量和层级问题（hierarchy problem）。该研究旨在通过高能质子对撞实验直接搜索成对产生的T夸克，检验相关BSM理论模型。

Method: 利用ATLAS探测器在13 TeV质心能量下记录的139 fb⁻¹质子-质子对撞数据，筛选至少一个T夸克衰变为希格斯玻色子（Higgs boson）和顶夸克（top quark）的末态（T→Ht, H→bb̅, t→ℓ⁺νℓb）。采用可变半径重聚簇射流（variable-radius reclustered jets）重建 boosted 重共振态的衰变产物，并训练神经网络（neural network）以区分信号与标准模型本底过程。

Result: 对有效质量分布（effective mass distribution）进行轮廓似然拟合（profile-likelihood fit），未观察到超出标准模型预言的显著信号。在95%置信水平（confidence level）下，对T夸克对产生截面设定排除限，对应的质量下限分别为：SU(2)单态表示（singlet representation）下1.40 TeV，SU(2)二重态表示（doublet representation）下1.56 TeV，分支比BR(T→Ht)=100%假设下1.66 TeV。

Conclusion: 搜索未发现矢量类T夸克的证据，实验结果对T夸克质量设定了迄今为止最严格的排除限之一，排除了质量低于1.40–1.66 TeV（依赖所选的SU(2)表示）的T夸克对产生信号。该结果对矢量类夸克模型的空间给出了新的约束。

Abstract: A search for pair-produced vector-like $T$-quarks in 139 fb$^{-1}$ of $pp$ collisions recorded by the ATLAS detector at a centre-of-mass energy $\sqrt{s}$=13 TeV is presented. The search targets signal events where at least one $T$-quark decays into a Higgs boson and a top quark, $T\rightarrow Ht$, with subsequent decays of the Higgs boson into a bottom quark-antiquark pair, $H\rightarrow b\bar{b}$, and the top quark into a light charged lepton, a neutrino and a bottom quark, $t\rightarrow\ell^+ν_\ell b$, where $\ell=e/μ$. The decay products of boosted heavy resonances are reconstructed using variable-radius, reclustered jets, and a neural network is employed to discriminate signal from Standard Model background processes. A profile-likelihood fit to the effective mass distribution is performed, and no excess above the Standard Model prediction is observed. Exclusion limits at 95% confidence level are set on the $T$-quark pair-production cross-section, corresponding to lower mass limits of 1.40 TeV in the SU(2) singlet representation, 1.56 TeV in the SU(2) doublet representation, and 1.66 TeV assuming the branching fraction of $T$-quarks to $Ht$ to be 100%.

</details>


### [33] [CP-violation or Nuclear Excitation: Reviewing the Role of Neutrino Interaction Model Uncertainties on Accelerator-Based Neutrino Oscillation Measurements](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28671)
*Stephen Dolan,Luke Pickering,Patrick Stowell,Callum Wilkinson,Clarence Wret*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 本文综述了中微子相互作用系统不确定性（neutrino interaction systematic uncertainties）对当前及未来加速器中微子振荡实验的影响，分析了这些不确定性在电荷宇称破坏测量、中微子质量排序判定及超出三味混合新物理探索中带来的挑战，并讨论了通过改进理论模型和近探测器精确测量来降低不确定性的实验与理论前景。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 加速器中微子振荡实验在理解基本物理——如轻子扇区电荷宇称破坏（charge-parity violation）、中微子质量排序（neutrino mass ordering）及超出三味混合的新物理——方面潜力巨大。然而，随着数据积累，对分析中系统不确定性（systematic uncertainties）的精细控制需求日益迫切，其中最难克服的正是来自中微子-原子核相互作用（neutrino--nucleus interactions）建模的不确定性。

Method: 本文采用综述（review）的研究方式，系统梳理了中微子相互作用系统不确定性对当前及未来振荡测量的影响，并评估了实验与理论层面降低这些不确定性的前景，包括改进前沿理论模型（state-of-the-art theoretical modelling）和利用近探测器（near detectors）对中微子相互作用事件率进行精确测量。

Result: 指出了中微子相互作用系统不确定性是当前及下一代振荡实验中最难克服的挑战之一，其来源与核物理（nuclear physics）的细微细节密切相关，极难实现足够精度的控制。现有方法需要结合前沿理论建模与近探测器精确测量来应对这些不确定性。

Conclusion: 应对中微子相互作用系统不确定性需要同时推进理论建模精度和近探测器测量精度。本文的综述为下一代实验如何将此类不确定性降低至可接受水平提供了实验与理论上的前景展望。

Abstract: Accelerator-based neutrino oscillation experiments have the potential to revolutionise our understanding of fundamental physics, offering an opportunity to characterise charge-parity violation in the lepton sector; to determine the neutrino mass ordering; and to explore the possibility of physics beyond three-flavour neutrino mixing. However, as more data is collected, the current and next-generation of experiments will require increasingly precise control over the systematic uncertainties within their analyses. It is well known that some of the most challenging uncertainties to overcome stem from our uncertain modelling of neutrino--nucleus interactions, which also affect the event rates used to infer the oscillation probability. The sources of these uncertainties are often related to subtle details of the pertinent nuclear physics which are extremely difficult to control with sufficient precision. Confronting such uncertainties requires both state-of-the-art theoretical modelling and precise measurements of neutrino interaction event rates at experiment's near detectors, before oscillations occur. In this work, we review the role of neutrino interaction systematic uncertainties in current and future measurements of neutrino oscillation as well as the experimental and theoretical prospects for reducing them to an acceptable level for the next generation of experiments.

</details>


### [34] [Characterising the role of final state interactions on neutrino energy estimation in the DUNE and Hyper-K era](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28696)
*Stephen Dolan,Jake McKean,Laura Munteanu*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 本研究使用最先进的微中子事件生成器，评估了末态相互作用（FSI）建模对Hyper-Kamiokande和DUNE实验所使用的两类微中子能量估计器的影响，发现FSI模型的可信变化引入的能量估计不确定性已达到或超过两个实验对能量刻度控制精度的要求，且两个实验对FSI模型不同方面敏感度不同。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: DUNE和Hyper-K实验需要将微中子能量估计控制在几MeV级别，而实现这一目标的核心挑战在于对微中子-原子核散射中产生的强子在残余核介质中再相互作用（即末态相互作用，final-state interactions, FSI）的精确建模。

Method: 使用最先进的微中子相互作用事件生成器（neutrino interaction event generators），对比分析了当前模拟中主流的半经典核内级联模型（semi-classical intranuclear cascades, INCs）和基于相对论平均场（relativistic mean field）计算的微观处理方法对能量估计的影响。

Result: FSI模型的可信变化在Hyper-K和DUNE所需的能量估计代理量（estimators）上引入了达到或超过能量刻度控制精度要求的不确定性；Hyper-K的能量估计受π介子吸收和超越半经典范式的核效应影响最大，而DUNE的能量估计更多受强子能量在可见与不可见探测信号之间分配方式建模的影响。

Conclusion: 强调了精细的FSI建模对于实现稳健的近探测器（near detector）约束的重要性，并指出需要进一步的理论和实验发展以控制FSI建模不确定性对微中子振荡分析的影响。

Abstract: The Deep Underground Neutrino Experiment (DUNE) and Hyper-Kamiokande (Hyper-K) will measure neutrino oscillation parameters with an unprecedented precision that requires neutrino energy estimation to be controlled at the few-MeV level. A central challenge in achieving this is the modelling of the reinteractions of hadrons produced in neutrino-nucleus scatters with the residual nuclear medium, or final-state interactions (FSI). In this work we use state-of-the-art neutrino interaction event generators to review the impact of FSI modelling on the kinematic and calorimetric neutrino energy estimators used by Hyper-K and DUNE respectively, considering both the semi-classical intranuclear cascades (INCs) that dominate current simulations and a microscopic treatment based on a relativistic mean field calculation. We find that plausible variations of the FSI model introduce uncertainties on the neutrino energy estimation proxies that are at or above the precision on the energy scale control required for Hyper-K and DUNE projected neutrino oscillation sensitivities, highlighting the importance of careful FSI modelling to allow robust near detector constraints. We further demonstrate that the two experiments are sensitive to different aspects of the FSI models. Neutrino energy estimation at Hyper-K is most impacted by pion absorption and nuclear effects beyond the semi-classical paradigm, whilst the DUNE energy estimation is more affected by the modelling of how hadronic energy is shared between sources of visible and invisible energy in the detector. We discuss the implications of these findings for neutrino oscillation analyses and outline some of the key experimental and theoretical developments needed to bring FSI modelling uncertainties under control.

### [35] [The dynamical structure of the Earth co-orbital region and implications for the near-Earth asteroid population](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27683)
*Marco Fenucci,Óscar Rodríguez,Melaine Saillenfest,Laura Faggioli*

Main category: astro-ph.EP

TL;DR: 本文利用1:1平均运动共振的半解析模型，系统研究了低偏心率和低倾角下地球共轨区域的结构，对轨道进行分类并量化各共轨态的相空间占比，发现马蹄形轨道占据主导地位，并分析了共轨态分布的非均匀性、短时间稳定性及其对地球共轨小天体种群预测和行星防御的意义。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解低偏心率和低倾角下地球共轨区域（co-orbital region）的结构，对地球共轨小天体的轨道动力学进行分类与定量刻画，为未发现种群估算和行星防御（planetary defence）提供动力学依据。

Method: 采用1:1平均运动共振（1:1 mean-motion resonance）的半解析模型，构建共振半长期哈密顿量（resonant semi-secular Hamiltonian），在轨道要素空间系统探索相空间，计算各类运动类型的占比；并利用MEGNO指标（MEGNO indicator）研究相空间的短期稳定性及混沌水平。

Result: 马蹄形轨道（horseshoe orbits）占据相空间超过一半的体积，其次是特洛伊型（Trojan）和循环型（circulating）轨道，准卫星（quasi-satellite）仅占很小比例。共轨态分布存在显著的非均匀性，尤其在近心点经度（argument of perihelion）方向上，马蹄形轨道的集中区域与节点交叉几何（node-crossing geometries）相关。不同共轨态的混沌程度存在差异。

Conclusion: 地球共轨区域中马蹄形轨道占主导，共轨态分布高度不均匀；这些结果对预测地球共轨小天体种群有重要启示，并表明仍有大量共轨体尚未被发现，对行星防御具有实际意义。

Abstract: We investigate the structure of the Earth co-orbital region at low eccentricity and low inclination using a semi-analytical model of the 1:1 mean-motion resonance. The dynamics of asteroids in co-orbital motion with the Earth is described through a resonant semi-secular Hamiltonian, allowing the classification of orbits into circulation, Trojan, horseshoe, and quasi-satellite states. By systematically exploring the phase space in the space of the orbital elements, we compute the fraction of each type of motion and quantify how different co-orbital states fill the Earth co-orbital region. We find that horseshoe orbits dominate the phase space, occupying more than half of the volume, followed by Trojan and circulating orbits, while quasi-satellites represent only a small fraction. The distribution of co-orbital states exhibits strong inhomogeneities, particularly as a function of the argument of perihelion, with clear concentration regions of horseshoe orbits associated with node-crossing geometries. We also study the short-term stability of this portion of phase space by means of the MEGNO indicator, and how the level of chaos differs between different co-orbital states. Finally, we discuss the implications of these results for the expected population of Earth co-orbitals and for planetary defence, showing that a large fraction of co-orbitals remains undiscovered.

</details>

### [36] [Quantum criticality of the ferromagnetic Dicke-Ising model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27484)
*Jan Alexander Koziol*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文利用朗道理论方法描述铁磁Dicke-Ising模型中的量子相变，定量捕捉了从正常相到超辐射相的二阶到一阶转变通过三临界点的变化，识别出虚关联最近邻双自旋翻转过程为关键机制，并讨论了修正有限尺寸标度以正确解释三临界点数值数据的方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究铁磁Dicke-Ising模型中的量子相变（quantum phase transition）行为，特别是在全连接相互作用系统中超出上临界维度（upper critical dimension）的相变特性，以及三临界点（tricritical point）附近有限尺寸标度（finite-size scaling）的修正需求。

Method: 采用朗道理论（Landau theory）方法对铁磁Dicke-Ising模型进行解析分析，识别虚拟关联最近邻双自旋翻转（virtual correlated nearest-neighbor double spin-flip）过程作为关键微观机制，并讨论适用于三临界点的有限尺寸标度修正形式。

Result: 朗道理论定量捕捉了正常相与超辐射相之间从二阶（second-order）到一阶（first-order）转变的演化，该转变通过三临界点发生；三临界点构成了一个位于上临界维度之上的量子相变；研究指出全连接相互作用量子系统需要采用经过修正的有限尺寸标度形式。

Conclusion: 铁磁Dicke-Ising模型可作为一个范例平台（paradigmatic platform），用于研究上临界维度之上的量子相变，涵盖标准的φ⁴临界性（criticality）及其超越行为。

Abstract: We describe the quantum phase transitions in the ferromagnetic Dicke-Ising model using a Landau theory approach. The theory quantitatively captures the change from a second- to a first-order transition between the normal and superradiant phases through a tricritical point. We identify virtual correlated nearest-neighbor double spin-flip processes as the crucial mechanism responsible for this behavior. The tricritical point constitutes a quantum phase transition above the upper critical dimension. We discuss the modifications to finite-size scaling required for the correct interpretation of numerical data at the tricritical point. Our results emphasize the need for adapted finite-size scaling forms in all-to-all interacting quantum systems and establish the ferromagnetic Dicke-Ising model as a paradigmatic platform for quantum phase transitions above the upper critical dimension, encompassing both standard $φ^4$ criticality and beyond.

### [37] [Inelastic Neutron Scattering of the layered Kitaev ferromagnet Li$_3$Co$_2$SbO$_6$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27518)
*Abdul Basit,Richard A. Mole,Alex J. Brown,Jiatu Liu,Chris D. Ling,Stephan Rachel*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本研究报告了Li₃Co₂SbO₆量子磁体的非弹性中子散射实验。通过与线性自旋波理论（linear spin wave theory）对比，表明其磁性质可由扩展的Kitaev–Heisenberg模型（extended Kitaev–Heisenberg model）很好地描述，从而将Li₃Co₂SbO₆确立为Kitaev铁磁体（Kitaev-ferromagnet），更具体地说是Kitaev A型反铁磁体（Kitaev A-type antiferromagnet）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 钴基蜂窝状层状量子磁体被认为是实现奇异Kitaev自旋交换（Kitaev spin exchange）的潜在平台，其中Na₃Co₂SbO₆和Na₂Co₂TeO₆等候选材料已在低温下展现出磁性的zigzag有序态。本研究旨在探索Li₃Co₂SbO₆这一新兴材料的磁性质，并验证其是否也能用Kitaev类模型描述。

Method: 采用非弹性中子散射（inelastic neutron scattering）实验对Li₃Co₂SbO₆量子磁体进行测量，并结合线性自旋波理论（linear spin wave theory）进行对比分析。此外还进行了磁场测量与模拟以补充验证。

Result: Li₃Co₂SbO₆的特征是铁磁性蜂窝状平面（ferromagnetic honeycomb planes）且相邻平面磁化方向相反。通过理论与实验对比，其磁性质可由扩展的Kitaev–Heisenberg模型良好拟合，从而被确定为Kitaev铁磁体，具体为Kitaev A型反铁磁体。

Conclusion: Li₃Co₂SbO₆可被归类为Kitaev A型反铁磁体，为研究Kitaev自旋交换物理提供了新的材料平台。

Abstract: Cobalt-based quantum magnets forming layered honeycomb arrangements have attracted much attention recently, as they are considered as a potential platform for materials with exotic Kitaev spin exchange. Amongst the discussed candidate materials are Na$_3$Co$_2$SbO$_6$ and Na$_2$Co$_2$TeO$_6$, both possessing a low-temperature ground state with magnetic zigzag ordering, similar to Na$_2$IrO$_3$ and $α$-RuCl$_3$. Here we report inelastic neutron scattering experiments on the quantum magnet Li$_3$Co$_2$SbO$_6$, which features ferromagnetic honeycomb planes with opposite magnetizations in neighboring planes. By comparing with linear spin wave theory, we show that the magnetic properties of Li$_3$Co$_2$SbO$_6$ can be well-modelled by an extended Kitaev--Heisenberg model, establishing it as a Kitaev-ferromagnet, or more specifically, as a Kitaev A-type antiferromagnet. Our analysis is complemented by magnetic field measurements and simulations.
