### [38] [Zero modes of non-abelian Dirac operator in topologically non-trivial band insulator](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27608)
*Neha Kumari,Sankalpa Ghosh*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文证明，布洛赫动量空间中量子几何张量（QGT）的局域规范不变性蕴含非阿贝尔狄拉克算子零模的存在，这些零模解通过雅可比Theta函数给出基态概率幅，并自然导出了陈能带涡旋性判据的非阿贝尔推广及其与动量空间最低朗道能级代数的联系。论文还提出了一个欧几里得作用量框架，并应用该框架分析了晶格狄拉克（QZW）模型和菱面体N层石墨烯的两带模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索量子几何张量（quantum geometric tensor）的局域规范不变性如何导致非阿贝尔狄拉克算子（non-abelian Dirac operator）在动量空间中产生零模，并在此基础上统一理解分数量子陈绝缘体（fractional Chern insulator, FCI）相关相的非相互作用部分。

Method: 通过分析N能带绝缘体布洛赫动量空间中量子几何张量的局域规范不变性，推导非阿贝尔狄拉克算子零模方程；利用二维布里渊区环面上的雅可比Theta函数（Jacobi Theta function）求解零模，得到N分量基态波函数的概率幅；引入归一化条件后，在存在色散简并点时构建复数射影空间（complex projective space, CP^{N-1}空间）。

Result: 证明了陈能带涡旋性判据（vortexability criterion）的非阿贝尔推广自动从零模方程中得出，并展示了这些方程与动量空间版本的最低朗道能级代数（Lowest Landau level algebra）之间的联系。推导出一个欧几里得作用量（Euclidean action），零模方程可从该作用量导出。

Conclusion: 所提出的框架可用于理解多种二维材料中分数量子陈绝缘体类似相的非相互作用部分；应用该框架分析晶格狄拉克（QZW）模型和菱面体N层石墨烯（rhombohedral N-layer graphene）的两带模型，获得了重要结论。

Abstract: We show that the local gauge-invariance of the quantum geometric tensor (QGT) defined in the Block-momentum space of a generic $N$-level (sublattice degrees of freedom) band insulator implies the existence of zero modes of non-abelian Dirac operator in such momentum space. Solutions of these zero modes equations in the two-dimensional Brillouin zone torus, in terms of Jacobi Theta function determine the probability amplitudes associated with the $N$-component ground state wave-function under adiabatic approximation in this Hilbert space. These solutions subjected to normalization, defines a complex projective ($CP$) space of $N-1$ dimension ($CP^{N-1}$ space) when one or more degeneracy points exist in the dispersion spectrum of such band-isulator. We show how the non-abelian generalization of the vortexability criterion of Chern bands automatically follows from these zero-mode equations, and also demonstrate their connection with momentum space-version of Lowest landau level algebra. Subsequently we write an Euclidean action from which these zero mode equations follow. We point out that the non-interacting part of different paradigms used to understand fractional Chern insulator(FCI) like phases in a host of two-dimensional material can be understood within this approach. We analyse two effective hamiltonian : lattice Dirac (QZW) model and two-band model for rhombohedral $N$-layer graphene in our propsoed framework and obtain important conclusions.

</details>


### [39] [Spontaneous breaking of non-invertible symmetries and duality to beyond-Landau transitions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27672)
*Xie Chen,Shang Liu,Da-chuan Lu,Nathanan Tantivasadakarn*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文以Rep(H₈)对称性为例，研究非可逆对称性（non-invertible symmetries）破缺相的特征，发现其序参量满足更一般的代数结构，并通过广义规范变换（generalized gauging）与非可逆对称性破缺相变和退禁闭量子临界点（deconfined quantum critical points）之间的对偶关系，为超越朗道（beyond-Landau）相变研究提供了系统路径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自发对称性破缺（spontaneous symmetry breaking）是理解物质相变的重要机制。近年来对称性概念被扩展到包含无逆元操作，即非可逆对称性（non-invertible symmetries）。论文旨在回答：与非可逆对称性相关的对称性破缺相，与传统可逆对称性（invertible symmetries）导致的对称性破缺相有何不同？

Method: 作者使用具有非可逆Rep(H₈)对称性的具体晶格模型（lattice models）对有能隙相（gapped phases）进行分析，通过广义规范变换（generalized gauging）建立非可逆对称性破缺相变与可逆对称性的退禁闭量子临界点（deconfined quantum critical points）之间的对偶关系，并给出该对偶成立的精确条件。

Result: 非可逆对称性破缺相仍可通过局域序参量（local order parameters）的长程关联（long-range correlation）来刻画，但其序参量满足比可逆情形更一般的代数结构。通过广义规范变换，某些非可逆对称性破缺相变与可逆对称性中的退禁闭量子临界点之间存在对偶关系。

Conclusion: 研究建立了非可逆对称性破缺相与可逆对称性退禁闭量子临界点之间对偶成立的条件，并通过多个例族加以说明，为研究超越朗道（beyond-Landau）相变提供了系统途径。

Abstract: Spontaneous symmetry breaking is a well-understood mechanism for generating distinct phases of matter. Recently, the notion of symmetry has been broadened to include operations without inverses, leading to the concept of non-invertible symmetries. How do symmetry-breaking phases associated with non-invertible symmetries differ from those arising from conventional invertible symmetries? We address this question using concrete lattice models of the gapped phases with non-invertible Rep($H_8$) symmetry as an example. We find that, despite the symmetry being non-invertible, the symmetry-breaking phases can still be characterized by the long-range correlation of local order parameters, which obey a more general algebraic structure than in the invertible setting. Furthermore, via generalized gauging, certain non-invertible symmetry-breaking transitions can be mapped to deconfined quantum critical points of invertible symmetries, and vice versa. We establish precise conditions under which this duality holds and illustrate them with several families of examples, providing a systematic route to studying beyond-Landau phase transitions.

### [40] [Chirality in Structural Phase Transitions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27812)
*Keita Matsubara,Kazumasa Hattori*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文基于群论方法，将电极化环形多极矩（electric toroidal multipoles）$G_{0,u}$ 构造为原子位移序参量 $\eta$ 的显式函数，用于描述非手性到手性（achiral-to-chiral, AtC）结构相变。研究发现，$G_{0,u}(\eta)$ 的领头阶行为由母相结构和位移模对称性决定，并可直接关联电流诱导磁化（CIM）和手性声子分裂（CPS）等可观测物理量，从而为 AtC 相变提供超越二元区分的对称性分类框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 手性（chirality）体系中的非手性到手性（AtC）结构相变缺乏统一的对称性分类方法，现有研究多停留在手性与非手性的二元区分层面。本文旨在建立基于电极化环形（ET）多极矩的解析框架，以更精细地表征此类相变。

Method: 采用群论（group-theoretical）方法，将立方体系中的 ET 单极子 $G_0$ 与非立方体系中的 ET 四极子 $G_u$ 构造为原子位移序参量 $\eta$ 的显式函数 $G_{0,u}(\eta)$；通过对称性分析确定其领头阶依赖关系，并建立与 CIM 和 CPS 等可观测物理量的比例关系。

Result: $G_{0,u}(\eta)$ 的领头阶行为完全由母相（parent structure）的对称性和位移模（displacive mode）的对称性特征决定；CIM 和 CPS 均与 $G_{0,u}(\eta)$ 呈现一致的标度行为；揭示了 AtC 相变通过 $G_{0,u}(\eta)$ 与声子自由度的耦合产生手性声子（chiral phonons）和手性声子分裂（CPS）的微观机制。

Conclusion: 该工作为 AtC 结构相变提供了一种基于对称性的分类方案，超越了简单的手性/非手性二元区分，并建立了 ET 多极矩与实验中可观测的电-磁交叉响应及手性声子效应之间的直接联系。

Abstract: Chirality, defined by the absence of mirror and inversion symmetries, has attracted considerable attention owing to its unique physical phenomena, including cross-correlated responses such as current-induced magnetization (CIM) and chiral phonons. Recently, it has been established that chirality is characterized by electric toroidal (ET) multipoles: the ET monopole $G_0$ in cubic systems and the ET quadrupole $G_u$ in noncubic systems. In this paper, we investigate achiral-to-chiral (AtC) structural phase transitions driven by atomic displacements and construct $G_{0,u}$ as explicit functions of the displacement order parameter $η$ based on a group-theoretical approach. We show that the leading-order dependence of $G_{0,u}(η)$ is determined by the symmetry of the parent structure and the character of the displacive mode, providing a symmetry-based classification of AtC transitions beyond a binary distinction between achiral and chiral phases. We also demonstrate that $G_{0,u}(η)$ is directly reflected in observable quantities such as CIM and CPS, both of which scale consistently with $G_{0,u}(η)$. We further clarify the microscopic mechanism by which AtC transitions give rise to chiral phonons and chiral phonon splitting (CPS) through the coupling between $G_{0,u}(η)$ and phonon degrees of freedom.

Abstract: We propose a definition of a non-invertible symmetry enriched topological order (NI-SETO), and we implement our definition for string net models. All NI-SETOs can be realized in either model, where we can use enriched UFCs to get chiral examples on the boundary of a 3D Walker-Wang model representing the anomaly. Abstract: The complex interplay of charge, spin, orbital, and lattice degrees of freedom governs emergent phases in quantum materials, making strain a powerful control parameter. Recent advances in free-standing layer techniques have enabled extreme strains of nearly 8%, opening access to novel and often unexpected electronic and magnetic phases. Here, using a density functional theory approach, we investigate the effect of direction-selective uniaxial strain on the prototypical Jahn-Teller system La1-xCaxMnO3 (x = 0.25). Method: 对Na₃Ni₂BiO₆体系进行了热力学量（thermodynamic quantities）的综合测量，包括比热（specific heat）等。

Abstract: Quantum fluctuations endow spin systems with surprisingly enriched magnetic phase diagrams. In frustrated magnets, strong quantum fluctuations boosted by either geometrical incompatibility or competitive exchange interactions stabilize cascades of unusual phases of matter. Here we reveal the presence of multiple quantum phases in the honeycomb antiferromagnet Na$_{3}$Ni$_{2}$BiO$_{6}$, both inside and beyond its field-induced one-third magnetization plateau. Comprehensive measurements of thermodynamic quantities demonstrate that the one-third plateau comprises at least three distinct spin states with nearly-degenerate net magnetization, separated by first-order transitions that likely involve sequential spin reconfiguration. Upon further increasing the magnetic field, the system evolves across a myriad of peculiar phases before reaching full polarization; these intermediate phases possess copious low-energy excitations, manifested by anomalous upturns of specific heat at ultralow temperatures -- probably hinting at the development of "hidden" ordered ground states. Method: 在反铁磁绝缘体（antiferromagnetic insulator）中测量零场条件下的热流偏转行为，并与典型外磁场响应进行比较。

Abstract: Fourier's law dictates that heat flow is usually parallel to the applied temperature gradient. Intriguingly, we observe at zero field a spontaneous thermal Hall effect in an antiferromagnetic insulator. Despite a vanishingly small uncompensated magnetization, the magnitude of this effect is surprisingly large, comparable to typical responses induced by several teslas of external field. This zero-field behavior indicates that charge-neutral heat carriers can be governed by an intrinsic effective field arising from the unique spin arrangement. Our discovery challenges the centuries-old preconception of heat conduction and open up new avenues for exploring non-trivial topological responses in quantum materials.

### [46] [Topological lattice gauge theory enriched by non-invertible symmetry](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28688)
*Lea E. Bottini,Clement Delcamp,Edmund Heng,Campbell K. McLauchlan,Dominic J. Williamson*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文以有限群拓扑格点规范理论（量子双模型）为切入点，探索由非可逆对称性（non-invertible symmetry） enriched 的拓扑序（topological order），通过凝聚任意电荷代数，证明局域激发范畴形成超群分次扩张，并用Hopf单子（Hopf monad）编码该范畴作用，最后将框架推广至一般弦网模型（string-net model）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前对于可逆对称性增殖的拓扑序（symmetry enriched topological order）已有成熟的公理化表述（G-交叉辫子融合范畴），但对于非可逆对称性增殖的拓扑序，尚缺乏系统的一般化理论框架。本文旨在建立这一推广的基础。

Method: 在量子双模型（quantum double model）中凝聚任意电荷代数（algebra of charges），分析所得理论中局域激发（localised excitations）的范畴结构，证明其构成超群（hypergroup）分次扩张；进一步引入Hopf单子（Hopf monad）编码该范畴上的非可逆作用，并通过Hopf单子模范畴（category of modules）实现非可逆对称性的规范（gauging）。

Result: 1. 凝聚代数后，局域激发范畴形成超群分次扩张，且每一超群元素对应的畴壁（domain wall）对局域激发的作用通常是非可逆的。2. 该作用与幺半结构（monoidal structure）均与超群分次相容。3. 非可逆对称性的规范等价于计算该Hopf单子的模范畴。4. 该框架可自然推广至一般弦网模型中凝聚代数的情形。

Conclusion: 本文为非可逆对称性增殖的拓扑序建立了一个基于超群分次范畴与Hopf单子的推广框架，并展示了其在量子双模型及更一般的弦网模型中的适用性，为非可逆对称性的系统研究提供了新的范畴论工具。

Abstract: We use finite group topological lattice gauge theory, also known as the quantum double model, as a lens to explore a notion of topological order enriched by a non-invertible symmetry. For invertible symmetry enriched topological order, there is an established axiomatisation in terms of a G-crossed braided fusion category. We lay the foundations for a generalisation of this notion. By condensing an arbitrary algebra of charges in a quantum double model, we demonstrate that the category of localised excitations in the resulting theory forms a hypergroup-graded extension of the category of deconfined excitations. For every element in the hypergroup, the associated domain wall acts in a typically non-invertible way on these localised excitations. Both this action and the monoidal structure are compatible with the hypergroup grading. The actual categorical action is encoded in a Hopf monad on the category of localised excitations, and gauging the non-invertible symmetry amounts to computing the category of modules over this Hopf monad. Finally, we outline how this framework naturally extends to theories obtained by condensing algebras in a generic string-net model.

</details>


### [47] [Anisotropic magnetism and Kondo-lattice behavior in the frustrated antiferromagnet Ce3MgBi5](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28540)
*Karolina Gornicka,Brenden R. Ortiz,Matthew S. Cook,Heda Zhang,Andrew D. Christianson,Andrew F. May*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文报道了Ce3MgBi5单晶的合成与物性表征。该化合物属Ce3MPn5家族，六方P63/mcm结构，具有各向异性的Ce亚晶格（c轴之字链+基面畸变Kagome网络）。磁化测量显示TN≈4.2 K反铁磁序，强磁各向异性及垂直于[001]方向的多级场致亚稳磁转变，形成穹顶状H-T相图。电输运呈现Kondo晶格特征（宽电阻峰、磁阻和霍尔响应中的场致异常追踪磁相边界）。比热确认磁相变，20 K时恢复Ce3+ Kramers二重态的R ln 2熵，表明存在与Kondo关联一致的宽温区磁涨落。该体系为研究几何阻挫、磁各向异性和Kondo晶格物理的相互作用提供了平台。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索Ce3MPn5家族中此前未研究的成员Ce3MgBi5，并揭示其晶体结构中几何阻挫（geometric frustration）、磁各向异性（magnetic anisotropy）与Kondo晶格（Kondo lattice）物理之间的相互作用。

Method: 采用单晶合成方法制备样品，通过磁化测量、电输运测量和比热测量进行物理表征，并结合H-T相图分析。

Result: Ce3MgBi5在TN≈4.2 K处呈现反铁磁序（antiferromagnetic order），具有强磁各向异性，垂直于[001]方向出现多级场致亚稳磁转变（metamagnetic transitions），形成穹顶状H-T相图；电输运显示Kondo晶格特征，磁阻与霍尔响应异常追踪磁相边界；比热测量证实磁相变，并在20 K时恢复Ce3+ Kramers二重态的全熵R ln 2，表明宽温区磁涨落与Kondo关联一致。

Conclusion: Ce3MgBi5是Ce3MPn5家族中一个有效的实验平台，可用于在外加磁场下研究几何阻挫、磁各向异性和Kondo晶格物理三者之间的相互耦合。

Abstract: We report the synthesis and physical characterization of single-crystalline Ce3MgBi5, a previously unexplored member of the Ce3MPn5 family. This compound crystallizes in the hexagonal P63/mcm structure, featuring an anisotropic Ce sublattice composed of zig-zag chains along the c axis and a distorted kagome-like network in the basal plane. Magnetization measurements reveal antiferromagnetic order below TN approximately 4.2 K, accompanied by strong magnetic anisotropy and multiple field-induced metamagnetic transitions for fields applied perpendicular to [001], leading to a dome-shaped H-T phase diagram. Electrical transport exhibits characteristic signatures of a Ce-based Kondo lattice, including broad resistivity maxima and pronounced field-dependent anomalies in the magnetoresistance and Hall response that track the magnetic phase boundaries. Specific-heat measurements confirm the magnetic transition and show that the full R ln 2 entropy expected for a Ce3+ Kramers doublet is recovered by 20 K, indicating an extended temperature range of magnetic fluctuations consistent with Kondo correlations. Our results establish Ce3MgBi5 as a platform within the Ce3MPn5 family for exploring the interplay of geometric frustration, magnetic anisotropy, and Kondo-lattice physics under applied magnetic fields.

*Wolfgang Simeth,Connor A. Occhialini,Michael E. Ziebel,Nethmi W. Hewage,Sabrina J. Li,Daniel Pajerowski,Taehun Kim,Ben Zager,Jonathan Pelliciari,Kipton Barros,Daniel Rehn,Abhay N. Pasupathy,Valentina Bisogni,Xavier Roy,Allen Scheie*

Method: 采用中子散射（neutron scattering）、X射线吸收谱（X-ray absorption spectroscopy）和共振X射线光谱（resonant X-ray spectroscopy）等多种实验手段，对CeSiI中的磁激发进行测量与分析，并基于实验数据确定有效哈密顿量及基态。

Conclusion: 该工作为CeSI的第一性原理建模提供了关键依据，从而为深入理解重费米子物理、非常规超导电性及量子临界性奠定了微观基础。

Abstract: We report neutron, X-ray absorption, and resonant X-ray spectroscopy of magnetic excitations in the new heavy-fermion van-der-Waals superconductor CeSiI. We determined effective Hamiltonians and ground states of crystal electric fields and magnons. Isotropic Heisenberg interactions on a quasi two dimensional lattice, including ferromagnetic nearest-neighbor exchange as the dominant interaction, provide an excellent account to the low-energy measured dynamics and stabilize a co-rotating spin cycloid. Our study provides the basis to model CeSiI from first principles, thereby laying the ground for microscopic understanding of heavy-fermion physics, their unconventional superconductivity, and quantum criticality.

### [49] [Odd spin symmetry and anisotropy switching in p-wave magnet CeNiAsO](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28701)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管理论上已预测数百种奇宇称磁体（odd-parity magnet）及其优异特性，但实验研究极为稀缺；已有候选材料NiI2和Ga3Ru4Al12的磁结构与输运性质虽被报道，但其特征能带结构尤其是奇宇称自旋对称性（odd-parity spin symmetry）尚未明确，亟需实验确认。

Result: ARPES揭示两个不同解理终止面具有迥异的表面能带结构；补偿极性表面后获得的本征体态能带结构的自旋劈裂可由p波磁结构（p-wave magnetic structure）的第一性原理计算很好地描述；自旋分辨ARPES测得体态自旋极化呈现仅有一个简并面的对称性，这是p波磁性的特征指纹（fingerprint）；此外实现了通过弱场诱导畴选择获得的巨大电阻各向异性及高低阻态切换。

Conclusion: CeNiAsO被实验确认为具有确定性p波自旋对称性的原型奇宇称磁体，其巨大的电阻各向异性开关效应展示了在反铁磁自旋存储器件中的应用潜力；该材料与1111型铁基超导体（1111-type Fe-based superconductors）的结构相似性为探索p波磁性、超导与能带拓扑之间的相互作用开辟了新方向。

Abstract: Odd-parity magnets, complementary to altermagnets, exhibit unique properties such as high efficiency in charge-spin conversion and compatibility with conventional superconductivity, of critical importance in the pursuit of energy-efficient spintronics and topological superconductors for quantum computation. For even-parity d-wave and g-wave altermagnets, the magnetic structure, spin-split band structure and physical properties are currently under intensive study. On the contrary, while hundreds of odd-parity magnets and the promising properties have been predicted in theory, experimental studies are scarce. Specifically, the magnetic structure and transport properties of candidates NiI2 and Ga3Ru4Al12 have been reported, yet the characteristic band structure and particularly the odd-parity spin symmetry remain elusive. Here we demonstrate experimentally the deterministic p-wave spin symmetry and resistance anisotropy switching for the prototype odd-parity magnet, CeNiAsO. Angle-resolved photoemission spectroscopy (ARPES) reveals two cleaved terminations with distinct surface band structure. By compensating the polar surface, we achieve intrinsic bulk band structure, for which the spin splitting can be well described by the p-wave magnetic structure through first-principles calculation. The bulk spin polarization measured by spin-resolved ARPES exhibits symmetry with only one degenerate plane, fingerprint of p-wave magnetism. We further demonstrate giant resistance anisotropy and switching between high-resistance and low-resistance states through modest field-induced domain selection, highlighting its potential for antiferromagnetic spin memory devices. The structural similarity between CeNiAsO and 1111-type Fe-based superconductors stimulates further exploration on the interplay between p-wave magnetism, superconductivity and band topology.

### [50] [Avoided Stoner instability at a single ordinary Van Hove point](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28761)
*I. S. Tupitsyn,B. Currie,A. V. Chubukov,B. V. Svistunov,E. Kozik,N. V. Prokof'ev*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文通过数值精确的图解蒙特卡洛（diagrammatic Monte Carlo）方法研究二维哈伯德模型（Hubbard model），发现范霍夫奇点（Van Hove singularity）处铁磁斯特纳不稳定性（ferromagnetic Stoner instability）的抑制机制源于有效耦合的下向重整化（downward renormalization）和准粒子权重（quasiparticle residue）损失导致态密度（density of states）降低，从而使系统在远低于平均场（mean-field）预测温度 $T_{MF}$ 时仍能避免铁磁失稳。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 平均场（mean-field）分析预测在范霍夫点（Van Hove point）处任意耦合强度下均存在铁磁斯特纳不稳定性（ferromagnetic Stoner instability），但该效应从未被实验观测到。本文旨在通过数值精确方法揭示这一平均场预测失败背后的物理机制。

Method: 采用两种图解蒙特卡洛（diagrammatic Monte Carlo）方法分析具有普通范霍夫奇点（Van Hove singularity）的二维哈伯德模型（two-dimensional Hubbard model）：(i) 四通道自洽近似（four-channel self-consistent approximation）；(ii) 对截断展开进行可控重求和（controlled resummation）的图解组合求和的数值精确方法。

Result: 系统在远低于平均场预测温度 $T_{MF}$ 约一个数量级的温度下仍能避免斯特纳不稳定性（Stoner instability），这一抑制效应源于两个共同机制：有效耦合（effective coupling）的下向重整化（downward renormalization）以及准粒子权重（quasiparticle residue）损失导致的态密度（density of states）降低。

Conclusion: 图解蒙特卡洛数值精确结果解释了为何平均场理论在范霍夫奇点处预测的铁磁失稳在实验上未被观测到，并揭示了有效耦合重整化与态密度抑制在其中的关键作用。

Abstract: When the Fermi surface and the Brillouin zone boundary touch at a Van Hove point, mean-field analysis predicts a ferromagnetic (Stoner) instability at finite $T_{MF}$ for any coupling strength due to the divergent density of states. However, the predicted effect has not been observed experimentally. Several qualitative theoretical proposals have been put forward to explain why the mean-field prediction fails. Based on numerically exact results for the two-dimensional Hubbard model with an ordinary Van Hove singularity, we uncover the mechanisms behind the suppression of the ferromagnetic instability. We employ two diagrammatic Monte Carlo approaches: (i) the four-channel self-consistent approximation and (ii) numerically exact method of combinatorial summation of diagrams with controlled resummation of the truncated expansion. We find that the system avoids the Stoner instability down to temperatures an order of magnitude below $T_{MF}$ due to the combination of the downward renormalization of the effective coupling and the suppression of the density of states by the loss of the quasiparticle residue.

</details>


### [51] [Realization of the Ruby Lattice Antiferromagnet in Layered Transition-Metal Fluorides](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28821)
*Harald O. Jeschke,Daniel Guterding,Pratyay Ghosh*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文通过密度泛函理论（DFT）能量映射和经典蒙特卡罗（Monte Carlo）模拟，证实层状过渡金属氟化物CsBaFe₃F₁₂和CsBaCr₃F₁₂是实现红宝石晶格（ruby lattice）反铁磁体的候选材料，并揭示了其强阻挫（frustration）特性、磁有序倾向及与实验观测的一致性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 红宝石晶格上的反铁磁体预期能展现多种新奇涌现现象（emergent phenomena），但其实际材料实现（material realization）一直难以达成。本工作旨在寻找并表征可实验实现的红宝石晶格反铁磁材料。

Method: 采用基于DFT的能量映射（DFT energy mapping）计算微观哈密顿量（microscopic Hamiltonian），并通过经典蒙特卡罗（Classical Monte Carlo）模拟和Luttinger-Tisza分析研究磁序与阻挫行为。

Result: CsBaFe₃F₁₂（Fe³⁺, S=5/2）和CsBaCr₃F₁₂（Cr³⁺, S=3/2）具有轻微畸变的红宝石晶格几何。两种化合物的哈密顿量均由红宝石层内的短程反铁磁（antiferromagnetic）相互作用主导。模拟显示强阻挫，六角元胞（hexagonal plaquette）上存在局域奈尔关联（local Néel correlation），而长程有序倾向由较弱的三角键（triangular link）控制。CsBaFe₃F₁₂的热力学行为与实验报告的磁有序标度一致。CsBaCr₃F₁₂则表现出竞争的低能有序波矢、强有限尺寸敏感性（finite-size sensitivity）以及向非公度（incommensurate）有序的趋势。

Conclusion: 该研究确立了这两种氟化物为实验上可获取的红宝石晶格反铁磁体，并为未来的中子散射（neutron-scattering）研究提供了定量预测。

Abstract: The antiferromagnet on the ruby lattice is expected to host a range of exotic emergent phenomena, yet its material realization has remained elusive. Here we show that the layered transition metal fluorides CsBaFe$_3$F$_{12}$ and CsBaCr$_3$F$_{12}$ with Fe$^{3+}$ and Cr$^{3+}$ ions realize only slightly distorted ruby lattice geometries with spin moments $S=5/2$ and $S=3/2$, respectively. Their microscopic Hamiltonians, calculated with DFT energy mapping, are dominated by short-ranged antiferromagnetic interactions within the ruby layers. Classical Monte Carlo simulations reveal strong frustration in both compounds, with local Néel correlations on the hexagonal plaquettes and distinct long-range ordering tendencies governed by weaker triangular links. For CsBaFe$_3$F$_{12}$, the calculated thermodynamic behaviour is consistent with the experimentally reported magnetic ordering scale. For CsBaCr$_3$F$_{12}$, classical Monte Carlo and Luttinger-Tisza analysis reveal competing low-energy ordering wave vectors, strong finite-size sensitivity, and a tendency toward incommensurate order. Overall, our results establish these fluorides as experimentally accessible ruby-lattice antiferromagnets and provide quantitative predictions for future neutron-scattering studies.

</details>

# cond-mat.stat-mech [[Back]](#toc)

### [52] [Competition for Survival and the Maximum Entropy Production Principle in Self-Organized Silver Particle Chains](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27457)
*Albert Han,Jiri Kataman-Kustwan,Alexey Bezryadin*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文通过银颗粒悬浮液的电学实验，研究了远离平衡态复杂系统中最大熵产生（MEP）原理受资源竞争约束的问题。实验发现，两个并联样本之间存在竞争，导致无法同时达到最大熵产生率（EPR），只有一个样本能自组织，全局EPR也低于理论最大值。据此提出竞争效应是MEP原理的重要约束条件，并类比了自然系统中的资源竞争现象。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 验证最大熵产生（MEP）原理在复杂系统中的适用性，并探究资源竞争是否限制耗散结构（dissipative structure, DS）达到最大熵产生率（entropy production rate, EPR）的能力。

Method: 对电场下的银颗粒悬浮液进行高精度电学测量，将两个银悬浮样本并联连接，使其能够自组织、耗散能量、产生熵，并通过竞争获取电流这一资源。

Result: (1) 两个样本之间的竞争阻止了各自对全局熵产生率做出最大贡献；(2) 竞争导致仅一个样本能自组织，另一个样本退化并趋近于零EPR；(3) 子系统间的竞争使全局EPR（包括样本和供能电路产生的熵）也低于其可能的最大值。

Conclusion: 竞争效应是MEP原理必须纳入的关键约束条件；该原理与自然系统中物种和个体间的资源竞争现象具有平行性；MEP还可用作驱动文明沿卡尔达肖夫指数（Kardashev scale）上升的机制。

Abstract: The maximum entropy production (MEP) principle is a hypothetical law of physics which dictates that complex systems, far from equilibrium, evolve into an ordered dissipative structure (DS) which generates as much entropy per second as possible. An important problem is whether the natural competition for resources, limits the ability of DS to achieve the maximum of the entropy production rate (EPR). We investigate this competition between DS by performing high precision electrical measurements on suspensions of silver particles under electric fields. To establish the impact of competition on MEP principle, precise electrical measurements are performed on two Ag suspension samples connected in parallel. The samples are able to self-organize, dissipate energy, generate entropy, and compete with each other for resources, i.e., electrical current. Our findings are as follows: (1) There is a competition between the two samples, which prevents both systems from achieving their maximum possible contribution to the global entropy production rate. (2) Due to this competition, we find that only one out of two samples can self-organize, while the other deteriorates and approaches zero EPR. (3) The global EPR, i.e., the entropy produced by the samples and the energy supply circuit, is also reduced from its possible maximum due to the competition between the sub-systems. Based on these observations, we propose that the competition effect constitutes an essential constraint that must be incorporated into formulations of the MEP. This principle parallels real-world phenomena, reflecting the competition for resources observed among species and individual organisms in natural systems. We also examine the global implications of the MEP and propose that it serves as a driving mechanism propelling the hypothetical ascent of civilizations along the Kardashev scale.

</details>


### [53] [A method for calculating entropy production without knowing transition rates or dwell times](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27635)
*John W. Biddle*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种仅从马尔可夫系统状态序列（state sequence）及其总时长推断熵产生率（entropy production rate）的方法，无需知道停留时间、跃迁时刻或跃迁速率等动力学细节。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 熵产生率是量化非平衡系统（non-equilibrium system）远离热力学平衡程度的关键参数，但其标准公式依赖于对系统底层动力学的完整知识，而实践中这些知识往往难以获取。

Method: 通过分析马尔可夫（Markovian）系统在一条长轨迹或多条较短轨迹上依次占据的状态序列，结合轨迹的总时间，即可推断熵产生率。该方法不要求知道各状态的停留时间（dwell time）、跃迁发生的时刻或刻画马尔可夫过程的跃迁速率（transition rate）。

Result: 给出了一种仅利用状态序列和总时间信息就能计算熵产生率的推断方法。

Conclusion: 该方法为实践场景中缺乏动力学细节的非平衡系统提供了熵产生率的实用估算途径。

Abstract: The entropy production rate is central to the study of non-equilibrium systems. This parameter is closely connected to violation of time-reversal symmetry, energy consumption, efficiency, and other properties of interest; in short, it quantifies how far a system is from thermodynamic equilibrium. Standard formulas for the entropy production require knowledge of the system's underlying dynamics, but this knowledge may be hard to acquire in practice. Here, I present a method for inferring the entropy production rate of a Markovian system from the sequence of states that the system occupies on a single long trajectory or many shorter trajectories, and the total time of the trajectory or trajectories. The method does not require knowledge of the dwell times in the various states, the times at which transitions occur, or of the transition rates characterizing the Markov process.

</details>


### [54] [Finite-size occupancy scaling of apparent fractal dimensions in stochastic trajectories](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27925)
*Bon A. Koo,Edward Ju*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文提出一个基于“球入盒”（balls-in-boxes）占位模型的有限尺寸标度（finite-size scaling）框架，用于解决从有限随机轨迹估计分形维数（fractal dimension）时的系统性偏差问题，并给出了偏差校正方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 从有限随机轨迹（finite stochastic trajectory）中估计分形维数是一个有限尺寸标度问题：表观盒计数指数（apparent box-counting exponent）受到分辨尺度范围与有限采样点之间占位交叉（occupancy crossover）的影响，不一定等于极限过程的真实维数。现有方法难以消除这一偏差，局部斜率稳定性本身也不是可靠诊断指标。

Method: 提出balls-in-boxes占位模型来描述有限采样点的占位交叉，预测盒计数曲线（box-count curve）、有限尺寸饱和标度（finite-size saturation scale）以及归一化局部斜率的标度函数（scaling function）。通过逆推该占位模型，得到有限尺寸偏差校正方法。

Result: 在随机游走迹线（random-walk traces）、分数布朗运动图（fractional Brownian graphs）和莱维飞行（Levy flights）上，归一化局部斜率坍缩（collapse）到单一交叉曲线；窗口化盒计数偏差（windowed box-counting bias）在回归窗口相对于饱和标度定位后也发生坍缩。偏差校正方法能减少受控随机轨迹上的误差，并可迁移至留出模型类（held-out model classes）。与关联维数（correlation dimension）、去趋势波动分析（detrended fluctuation analysis）、变异函数（variogram）及Higuchi方法的比较表明，主导偏差是点采样盒计数在有限尺度窗口上的特有问题。

Conclusion: 通过逆推占位模型提出的有限尺寸偏差校正方法可有效降低盒计数维数估计的系统性误差，且该偏差是点采样盒计数方法在有限尺度窗口下的固有特性。局部斜率稳定性单独不足以作为可靠诊断标准。实验代码已开源，结果可完全复现。

Abstract: Estimating a fractal dimension from a finite stochastic trajectory is a finite-size scaling problem: the apparent box-counting exponent is shaped by an occupancy crossover between the resolved range of scales and the finite number of sampled points, and need not equal the dimension of the limiting process. We model this crossover with a balls-in-boxes occupancy law, which predicts the box-count curve, the finite-size saturation scale, and a scaling function for the normalized local slope. Across random-walk traces, fractional Brownian graphs, and Levy flights, the normalized local slope collapses onto a single crossover curve, while the windowed box-counting bias collapses when the regression window is positioned relative to the saturation scale. Inverting the occupancy model gives a finite-size bias correction that reduces error on controlled stochastic trajectories and transfers across held-out model classes. Comparisons with correlation dimension, detrended fluctuation analysis, the variogram, and Higuchi's method show that the dominant bias is specific to point-sampled box-counting over finite scale windows, and that local-slope stability alone is not a reliable diagnostic. A DNA-walk example illustrates the workflow on measured data, and all figures, tables, and in-text numbers are regenerated from released single-seed code.

</details>


### [55] [Barrier crossing in a two-state system: Effect of bias and stochastic fields](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28196)
*Sara Oliver-Bonafoux,Raúl Toral,Amitabha Chakrabarti*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本研究通过动力学伊辛模型（kinetic Ising model）探讨弱偏置场（bias field）与时空均匀但时间依赖的高斯随机场（Gaussian random fields）对两态系统势垒穿越（barrier crossing）的影响，发现偏置场控制磁化概率分布的主峰位置，噪声强度决定峰的尖锐性与分布稳定性，适度随机场可降低有效能垒并促进有序态间跃迁，而过强噪声则导致宽分布和显著回流，降低方向选择性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解弱偏置场与时间相关高斯随机噪声共同作用下两态系统（two-state system）的势垒穿越动力学，揭示随机驱动强度与偏置场之间的平衡条件如何影响系统的跃迁效率与方向选择性。

Method: 采用动力学伊辛模型（kinetic Ising model）作为两态系统，在其中引入弱偏置场和时空均匀但时间依赖的高斯随机场，通过分析磁化概率分布函数（probability distribution function of the magnetization）的主峰位置、尖锐程度及分布稳定性来刻画系统行为。

Result: 偏置场决定磁化概率分布函数主导极大值的位置；噪声强度控制分布的尖锐程度与稳定性；适度随机场可降低有效能垒并促进有序态间跃迁；强噪声引起宽分布和显著回流，削弱方向选择性。

Conclusion: 高效的势垒穿越需要适度随机驱动与受控偏置场之间达成平衡组合。

Abstract: We study barrier crossing in a two-state system, namely the kinetic Ising model, in the presence of a weak bias field and spatially homogeneous, but time-dependent, Gaussian random fields. We find that the bias field determines the location of the dominant maxima of the probability distribution function of the magnetization, whereas the noise intensity controls their sharpness and stability of the distribution. A moderate stochastic field lowers the effective energy barrier and facilitates transitions between ordered states, while strong noise induces broad distributions and significant backflow, which reduces directional selectivity. Our results suggest that efficient barrier crossing requires a balanced combination of moderate stochastic driving and controlled bias.

</details>


### [56] [The Resetting Heat Engine: A Thermodynamic Cycle of Thermal Expansion and Compression](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28445)
*Oded Farago*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文通过热力学循环与KL散度（Kullback-Leibler divergence）框架，分析了受随机重置（stochastic resetting）作用的布朗粒子（Brownian particle）的熵产（entropy production），发现谐波势（harmonic potential）下熵产可简化为态函数形式，且低重置率时熵产率与重置率线性相关，高重置率时趋于零。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随机重置动力学具有重复性特征，但其不可逆性（irreversibility）与热力学（thermodynamics）之间的定量联系尚不明确。本文旨在建立随机重置过程与热力学循环、信息论不可逆性度量之间的直接关联。

Method: 将布朗粒子的重置过程描述为一个热膨胀与收缩的热力学循环（thermodynamic cycle）；利用正向与反向轨迹系综（forward and reversed trajectory ensembles）之间的KL散度作为分析框架，推导谐波势下的精确解析结果，并通过朗之万模拟（Langevin simulations）验证非谐势（anharmonic quartic potential）下的行为。

Result: 谐波势下熵产可精确简化为仅由重置前后分布决定的态函数（state-function-like expression）；周期性重置与泊松重置（Poissonian resetting）下均获得了解析结果。低重置率r时熵产率与r线性相关，且正比于重置分布与平衡分布间的对称KL散度；极高重置率时重置过程近似永续（perpetual），熵产趋零。非谐势的模拟结果呈现相同定性行为。

Conclusion: 随机重置过程的熵产并非总能简化为热力学态变量，但在谐波势这一特例下可精确约化。该研究建立了随机重置、热力学循环与信息论不可逆性度量之间的直接联系，且结论具有一定的普遍性（不限于谐波约束）。

Abstract: We consider a Brownian particle confined by an external potential and subject to stochastic resetting to the origin. Motivated by the repetitive nature of the dynamics, we describe the process as a thermodynamic cycle of thermal expansion and collapse, analyzed via a framework based on the Kullback-Leibler (KL) divergence between forward and reversed trajectory ensembles. While the entropy production generally depends on the full trajectory ensemble and cannot be reduced to thermodynamic state variables alone, we show that the harmonic potential constitute a special case, where the entropy production reduces exactly to a state-function-like expression determined solely by the distributions before and after resetting. Explicit analytical results are derived for periodic and Poissonian resetting. At low resetting rates $r$, the entropy production rate grows linearly with $r$ and is proportional to the symmetric KL divergence between the reset and equilibrium distributions. At very high rates, the resetting process becomes effectively perpetual and the entropy production vanishes. Langevin simulations for an anharmonic quartic potential display the same generic behavior, indicating that these features are not restricted to harmonic confinement. Our results establish a direct connection between stochastic resetting, thermodynamic cycles, and information-theoretic measures of irreversibility.

</details>


### [57] [Thermodynamic properties of chemically disordered compounds via AI-driven estimation of partition function with the PULSE method](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28594)
*Baptiste Bernard,Luca Messina,Eiji Kawasaki,Emeric Bourasseau*

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 降低蒙特卡洛方法（Monte Carlo approaches）在化学无序化合物热力学性质计算中的计算成本，解决传统方法对此类材料效率低下的问题。

Method: 采用改进版PULSE方法，一种基于生成模型的非监督学习框架，通过对系统配分函数（partition function）进行采样和估计来获取热力学性质；使用2D伊辛模型作为基准测试来验证方法的有效性。

Result: 改进版PULSE方法能够以高精度和高效率准确复现平均性质，性能优于传统的蒙特卡洛采样方法。

Conclusion: PULSE方法具有高效性和适应性，是研究传统方法因化学无序（chemical disorder）而计算成本过高的材料体系的有力工具。

Abstract: In this article, we present an improved version of the PULSE method (Partition function Unsupervised Learning Sampling and Evaluation) for estimating the thermodynamic properties of chemically disordered compounds. The aim is to reduce the computational cost of Monte Carlo approaches for this type of material and to demonstrate that this generative tool can estimate thermodynamic properties by sampling and estimating the partition function of the system. To validate this innovative approach, we use the 2D Ising model as a benchmark. We demonstrate that our method accurately reproduces average properties with high precision and efficiency compared to traditional Monte Carlo sampling methods. Our results highlight the efficiency and adaptability of the PULSE method, making it a valuable tool for studying materials for which conventional methods are too inefficient to compute properties affected by chemical disorder at low cost.

### [58] [From geodesic flow to wave dynamics on hyperbolic surfaces](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28243)
*Frédéric Faure*

Main category: math.SP

TL;DR: 本文利用 $SL_{2}(\mathbb{R})$ 表示论，在闭双曲曲面的余切单位丛林 $M=S^{*}\mathcal{N}$ 上构造了显式的 $X$-适应希尔伯特空间（$X$-adapted Hilbert spaces），使得测地线生成元 $X$ 在该空间中成为具有离散谱（除阈值 $\mu=1/4$ 处可能出现二阶若尔当块（Jordan block）外）的正规算子（normal operator），并以此阐明了测地线动力学与拉普拉斯谱之间的经典联系，包括塞尔伯格迹公式（Selberg trace formula）的动力学形式以及球平均算子的大时间行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法对闭双曲曲面测地流（geodesic flow）的谱分析缺乏一个既能显式刻画生成元谱结构，又能统一联系测地线动力学与曲面拉普拉斯谱（Laplace spectrum）的希尔伯特空间框架。作者的目标是构造这样的显式适应空间，从而将经典动力学、鲁埃勒共振（Ruelle resonances）和曲面谱理论纳入一个统一的希尔伯特结构之中。

Method: 利用 $SL_{2}(\mathbb{R})$ 表示论，在 $L^{2}(M)$ 的传播稠密域（propagated dense domains）上完成化，构造出显式的 $X$-适应希尔伯特空间。在此模型中，传播子 $e^{tX}$ 被分解为一个阻尼谐振子部分（特征值 $e^{-t(n+1/2)}$）和一个横截部分（涉及 $\mathcal{N}$ 上的平移波群 $e^{\pm it\sqrt{\Delta-1/4}}$ 以及全纯和反全纯离散序列（discrete series））。

Result: 在 $X$-适应希尔伯特空间中，$X$ 除阈值 $\mu=1/4$ 处可能出现二阶若尔当块外，成为具有离散谱的正规算子。将传播子的谱迹（spectral trace）与阿蒂亚-博特-吉明平坦迹（Atiyah–Bott–Guillemin flat trace）比较，导出了塞尔伯格迹公式的动力学形式：闭测地线来自平坦迹，谱侧来自显式的 $SL_{2}(\mathbb{R})$ 分解。相同的分解还解释了 $\mathcal{N}$ 上球平均算子（spherical mean operators）的大时间结构：在自然的 $e^{t/2}$ 重正化（renormalization）并移除有限秩低能部分后，平移波方程成为主导的有效动力学。

Conclusion: 该构造建立了一个显式的希尔伯特空间结构，将经典测地线动力学、鲁埃勒共振与曲面的谱理论三者统一起来，揭示了测地流与拉普拉斯谱之间深层的代数对应关系。

Abstract: We study the geodesic flow on the unit cotangent bundle $M=S^{*}\mathcal{N}$ of a closed hyperbolic surface $\mathcal{N}$, using the representation theory of $SL_{2}(\mathbb{R})$. We construct explicit $X$-adapted Hilbert spaces, obtained by completing propagated dense domains of $L^{2}(M)$, which are tailored to the spectral analysis of the geodesic generator $X$. In these spaces, $X$ becomes a normal operator with discrete spectrum, except at the threshold $μ=1/4$, where Jordan blocks of size two may occur.
  In this Hilbert model, the propagator $e^{tX}$ factorizes into a damped harmonic oscillator with eigenvalues $e^{-t(n+1/2)}$, $n\in\mathbb{N}$, and a transverse part involving the shifted wave group $e^{\pm it\sqrt{Δ-1/4}}$ on $\mathcal{N}$, together with the holomorphic and anti-holomorphic discrete series.
  The model clarifies two classical links between geodesic dynamics and the Laplace spectrum. Comparing the spectral trace of the propagator in the $X$-adapted Hilbert model with the Atiyah--Bott--Guillemin flat trace gives a dynamical form of the Selberg trace formula: closed geodesics arise from the flat trace, while the spectral side comes from the explicit $SL_{2}(\mathbb{R})$-decomposition. The same factorization also explains the large-time structure of spherical mean operators on $\mathcal{N}$: after the natural $e^{t/2}$-renormalization and the removal of a finite-rank low-energy part, the shifted wave equation on $\mathcal{N}$ emerges as the leading effective dynamics. Thus the construction provides an explicit Hilbert-space structure relating classical geodesic dynamics, Ruelle resonances, and the spectral theory of the surface.

### [59] [Three-component superconductivity: the effect of second-order Josephson couplings](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28221)
*Shen-Yi Peng,Ling-Feng Zhang,Xiao Hu*

TL;DR: 本文基于与3Q配对密度波态兼容的三组分金茨堡-朗道模型，完整推导了基态解并构建了包含解析相界的相图，识别出五个不同基态，并在受阻区域发现独特的希格斯-莱格特（Higgs-Leggett）模式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 近期在钒基笼目（kagome）超导体中观察到周期为φ₀/3 = hc/6e的分数量子磁阻振荡，为此人们提出了一个三组分金茨堡-朗道（Ginzburg-Landau, GL）模型。本文旨在系统性地解析该模型的基态结构和集体激发行为。

Method: 通过理论推导获得基态解的完整集合；利用解析方法确定相边界，构建GL参数空间中的完整相图；采用数值分析手段研究集体模式（collective modes）的行为。

Result: 识别出五种不同的基态：一个8重简并的受阻态（frustrated state）和四个4重简并非受阻锁相态。其中四个态自发破缺时间反演对称性（time-reversal symmetry）。在受阻区域中出现一个独特的希格斯-莱格特（Higgs-Leggett）模式，并在相边界附近伴随模式软化（mode softening）。

Conclusion: 研究结果为理解多分量超导体（multicomponent superconductivity）的多方面物理提供了一个全面的理论框架。

Abstract: Recently, a three-component Ginzburg-Landau (GL) model compatible with the 3Q pair-density-wave state has been proposed to explain the fractional quantum magnetic resistance oscillations of period $φ_0/3 = hc/6e$ observed in vanadium-based kagome superconductors. The physics of this model is governed by second-order Josephson-type couplings, which break both time-reversal symmetry and discrete $π$-phase flip symmetry. In this work, we theoretically derive the complete set of ground-state solutions and construct a comprehensive phase diagram in the GL parameter space, characterized by analytically determined phase boundaries. We identify five distinct ground states: an 8-fold degenerate frustrated state and four 4-fold degenerate non-frustrated phase-locked states. Four of these states spontaneously break time-reversal symmetry. Numerical analysis of the collective modes reveals the emergence of a Higgs-Leggett mode unique to the frustrated region, accompanied by mode softening near the phase boundaries. Our findings provide a comprehensive theoretical framework for understanding the multifaceted physics of multicomponent superconductivity.

### [60] [Absolute measurement of penetration depth of superconducting thin films using microwave stripline resonators](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28759)
*Arghya Dutta,Ajeet Salunke,Mahesh Poojary,Vivas Bagwe,Sangita Bose,Pratap Raychaudhuri*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文提出一种混合方法，通过将超导微带谐振器（superconducting microstrip resonator）测量与COMSOL Multiphysics有限元电磁仿真相结合，在宽温度范围内确定超导穿透深度（penetration depth）的绝对值。该方法通过不同厚度NbN薄膜验证了有效性，并利用翻转薄膜（flip-film）几何结构将其推广至低临界温度材料，为非破坏性、高灵敏度的超导薄膜穿透深度表征提供了一种可靠平台。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 超导微带谐振器虽可基于动感电感（kinetic inductance）探测超导薄膜的微波电动力学特性，但从这些测量中提取绝对超导穿透深度（absolute superconducting penetration depth）仍然是一个难题。

Method: 本文提出一种混合方法（hybrid method），将谐振器测量结果与COMSOL Multiphysics中的有限元电磁仿真（finite-element electromagnetic simulations）相结合，以在宽温度范围内确定穿透深度的绝对值。针对低临界温度（critical temperature）材料，采用翻转薄膜（flip-film）几何结构：将待测样品置于NbN谐振器上方，并以薄Mylar介电层隔开，形成耦合结构，使样品穿透深度的变化反映在谐振频率的移动上。

Result: 通过制备不同厚度的NbN薄膜谐振器并提取其穿透深度，验证了该方法的有效性。翻转薄膜几何结构进一步将技术推广至临界温度较低的超导材料，实现了非破坏性（non-destructive）的穿透深度测量。

Conclusion: 该混合方法为表征多种超导薄膜的穿透深度提供了一种可靠、高灵敏度的非破坏性平台，可望在更广泛的超导材料研究中发挥作用。

Abstract: Superconducting microstrip resonators, which leverage kinetic inductance to probe electrodynamics, are sensitive tools for studying superconducting thin films at microwave frequencies. However, extracting the absolute superconducting penetration depth from these measurements remains challenging. In this work, we present a hybrid method to determine the absolute value of penetration depth over a wide temperature range by combining resonator measurements with finite-element electromagnetic simulations in COMSOL Multiphysics. We demonstrate this approach by extracting the penetration depth of NbN films by fabricating resonators from films of various thicknesses. Furthermore, we extend the technique to materials with lower critical temperatures by employing a flip-film geometry. By placing a sample above a NbN resonator, separated by a thin Mylar dielectric, we create a coupled structure where changes in the sample's penetration depth shift the resonant frequency. This non-destructive method provides a reliable, high-sensitivity platform for characterizing the penetration depth of diverse superconducting thin films.

</details>

### [61] [Heatomics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28720)
*F. Ritort*

Main category: physics.bio-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出“热组学（heatomics）”作为研究生命系统熵产生率（σ）的新科学领域，指出生命物质单位质量耗散功率约为1瓦特/千克，该值在多个尺度上高度保守，且与宇宙平均功率密度惊人一致。作者引入方差和规则（Variance Sum Rule）作为从动力学探针涨落中提取σ的实验-理论框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 生命系统通过持续耗散能量维持非平衡稳态（nonequilibrium steady state, NESS），熵产生率（σ）是表征细胞状态的普适生命信号。然而，如何从实验可测量中提取σ仍缺乏系统框架，且生命系统耗散功率的宇宙学意义尚未被充分揭示。

Method: 文中提出热组学（heatomics）作为研究细胞和分子尺度熵产生率σ的科学体系，并引入方差和规则（Variance Sum Rule），一种结合动力学探针涨落与非平衡稳态状态方程（equation of state for a NESS）的实验-理论混合方法，用于从可观测涨落中提取σ。

Result: 生命物质单位质量耗散功率Plife ≈ 1 W/kg，该值在从分子反应到整个生物体的多个尺度上高度保守；该功率密度是太阳的10⁴倍，且与宇宙平均功率密度PU = c²H₀ ≈ 1 W/kg惊人一致，这一巧合呼应了狄拉克大数假说（Dirac's large number hypothesis）。

Conclusion: 假设Plife设定了产生负熵（negentropy）的尺度，负熵对整体正向熵产生率σ起负贡献作用，是维持生物组织、区分生命与非生命物质的核心机制。热组学的目标在于阐明生命系统中热量产生、能量资源优化及负熵生成的基本原理。

Abstract: Living cells are energy- and information-processing systems that sustain a nonequilibrium steady state (NESS) by continuously consuming energy and dissipating heat, as required by the second law of thermodynamics. The rate of heat dissipation, or the entropy production rate $σ$, is the universal primal life signal and a unique descriptor of the cellular state. Living matter dissipates $P_{\mathrm{life}} \sim 1$ Watt/kilogram (W/kg), a remarkably conserved value across scales, from molecular reactions to entire organisms. Surprisingly, this high power density is $10^{4}$ times larger than that of the Sun and comparable to the universe's average, $P_U = c^2 H_0 \sim 1$ W/kg, where $c$ is the speed of light and $H_0$ the Hubble constant, a striking coincidence that aligns with Dirac's large number hypothesis. We hypothesize that this large $P_{\mathrm{life}}$ sets the scale for generating negentropy, the negative contribution to the overall positive $σ$ that sustains biological organization, distinguishing animate from inanimate matter. Here, I introduce heatomics, the science of studying $σ$ at the cellular and molecular scales, and the Variance Sum Rule, an experimental--theoretical framework that extracts $σ$ from fluctuations of a dynamical probe combined with the equation of state for a NESS. The emerging field of heatomics aims to elucidate the fundamental principles governing heat power generation, optimization of energy resources, and negentropy in living systems.

</details>

### [62] [Non Maxwellian long-time asymptotics for Homoenergetic Boltzmann flows under strong shear](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27695)
*Alessia Nota,Juan J. L. Velázquez*

Main category: math.AP

TL;DR: 该论文通过匹配渐近展开（matched asymptotic expansions）方法，计算了在双曲主导 regime 下、具有剪切项的非线性玻尔兹曼方程（nonlinear Boltzmann equation）的同能解（homoenergetic solutions）的长时渐近行为，研究对象为均匀碰撞核（homogeneous collision kernels）。研究发现，解的质量集中在不断增大的二进尺度（dyadic scales）族上，这与经典麦克斯韦分布（Maxwellian distributions）的行为截然不同。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解非线性玻尔兹曼方程在剪切流与双曲主导条件下的长时渐近行为，尤其是当碰撞次数趋于无穷时，解的动力学演化规律。该问题在统计力学（statistical mechanics）和流体动力学中具有重要理论意义。

Method: 采用匹配渐近展开（matched asymptotic expansions）方法进行渐近分析，求解包含剪切项的非线性玻尔兹曼方程，并考虑均匀碰撞核且碰撞次数随τ→∞趋于无穷的极限情形。

Result: 解的质（mass）量分布在一个不断增大的二进尺度（dyadic scales）族上，而非如经典麦克斯韦分布（Maxwellian distributions）那样趋于平衡态。这一结果表明，在该参数 regime 下，解的渐近行为表现出多尺度（multi-scale）特征，与传统热力学平衡图像有本质差异。

Conclusion: 在双曲主导 regime 下，同能解的动力学行为显著偏离经典麦克斯韦分布，其质量在二进尺度上的集中意味着可能存在非传统的高能尾部（high-energy tail）或非平衡稳态（non-equilibrium steady state）结构。

Abstract: We compute, using matched asymptotic expansions, the long-time asymptotics of homoenergetic solutions to the nonlinear Boltzmann equation, in presence of a shear term, in the hyperbolic dominated regime, for homogeneous collision kernels for which there are infinitely many collisions as $τ\to \infty$. The mass of the resulting solutions is concentrated in an increasing family of dyadic scales, something that makes the behaviour of these solutions very different from classical Maxwellian distributions.

### [63] [Efficient dispersal of submicron solid particles for stratospheric aerosol injection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27414)
*Yair Segev,Eitan Y. Levine,Yair Bar-Yoseph,Ori Amsallem,Yuval Dagan,Elad Laor,Shai Rahamim,Alon Luski,Eran Daniel,Eshani Hettiarachchi,Amyad Spector*

Main category: physics.app-ph

TL;DR: 本文通过实验证明，对固体颗粒进行疏水表面处理并结合气动分散技术，能够有效克服平流层气溶胶注入（SAI）中固体颗粒的团聚问题，使50-85%的颗粒质量达到亚微米尺寸，且理论模型成功预测了不同颗粒的相对分散性，缩放分析表明可部署实际规模的机群来产生有意义的干预气溶胶层。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 提出使用固体颗粒替代硫酸盐气溶胶进行平流层气溶胶注入（Stratospheric Aerosol Injection, SAI）的太阳辐射修正方案，但实际部署面临如何高效解团聚和分散亚微米级粉末的挑战。

Method: 实验采用球形无定形二氧化硅颗粒，通过疏水表面处理改善分散性；利用气动分散系统实现颗粒输送；结合原子力显微镜（atomic force microscopy）提取表面粗糙度参数，并建立颗粒间粘附力（adhesion forces）的理论模型来预测相对分散性。

Result: 疏水处理后50-85%的颗粒质量达到亚微米级，而未处理颗粒仅为10%；300 nm颗粒比500 nm颗粒在相同空气消耗下解团聚效果更优；气动分散系统在气粉质量比约10:1时达到最佳性能；缩放分析表明可通过合理规模的分散飞机机群提供足够的气溶胶层以实现有意义的干预。

Conclusion: 疏水表面处理与气动分散技术能够解决固体颗粒在SAI中的团聚难题，为固体颗粒替代硫酸盐气溶胶进行太阳辐射修正提供了可行的技术路径。

Abstract: Stratospheric aerosol injection (SAI) using solid particles has been proposed as an alternative to sulfate aerosols for solar radiation modification, but practical deployment faces challenges in efficiently deagglomerating and dispersing powders as submicron particles. Here we experimentally demonstrate pneumatic dispersal of particles in optically optimal size ranges for SAI. Using spherical amorphous silica particles, we find that applying a hydrophobic surface treatment substantially improves dispersibility, with 50-85% of treated particle mass achieving submicron sizes compared to 10% for untreated particles. We compare the dispersal of treated particles of different sizes and find that 300 nm particles provide superior deagglomeration than 500 nm particles for the same air consumption. Theoretical modeling of the adhesion forces between particles, combined with surface roughness parameters extracted from atomic force microscopy, successfully predicted the relative dispersibility across different particle types. The pneumatic dispersal system achieved optimal performance at air-to-powder mass ratios of about 10:1. Using the measured dispersed particle sizes, we provide a scaling analysis suggesting that a feasibly sized fleet of dispersal aircraft could provide an aerosol layer sufficient for meaningful climate intervention. These results demonstrate that hydrophobic surface treatment and pneumatic dispersal can overcome the agglomeration challenge for SAI with solid particles.

### [64] [Dirac-Line Criticality and Emergent Horizons in Weyl Lifshitz Transitions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27453)
*Iftekher S. Chowdhury,Hom Nath Dhungana,Shah Haque,Hind Adawi,Eric Howard*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索黑洞事件视界与拓扑半金属中第一类到第二类Weyl费米子转变之间的物理类比关系，并揭示其中可能涌现的霍金辐射等引力现象。

Method: 采用Painlevé-Gullstrand度规描述视界附近的时空几何，将黑洞视界映射为半金属中第一类与第二类Weyl态之间的界面，并通过Lifshitz转变和狄拉克线进行分析。

Result: 发现第一类到第二类狄拉克费米子的转变态可类比为黑洞事件视界，该转变态具有狄拉克线费米面（Dirac-line Fermi surface）、非平凡拓扑不变量以及临界手征反常效应等独特特征。

Conclusion: 黑洞视界与Weyl半金属中的拓扑相变之间存在深刻类比，为在凝聚态体系中模拟黑洞物理（如霍金辐射）提供了理论依据。

Abstract: Type-II Weyl fermions may emerge behind the event horizon of black holes. We employ the Painlevé-Gullstrand metric to study the surface of the Lifshitz transition at the horizon, equivalent to the interface separating the type-I and type-II Weyl states. We find several analogies between the black hole horizon and the transformation of type-I to type-II Weyl fermions through the Dirac line. We analyze the symmetry-protected topological order at the Lifshitz transition originating in semimetals. The emergence of Hawking radiation in Weyl semimetals is discussed. We show that the transition state from type-I to type-II Dirac fermions can be viewed as a black-hole horizon, which exhibits unique characteristics, including a Dirac-line Fermi surface with a nontrivial topological invariant and a critical chiral anomaly effect.

### [65] [Emergence of an antiferromagnetic topological Anderson insulator in the interacting Haldane model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27524)
*Alejandro J. Uría-Álvarez,Roser Valentí*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文通过有限尺寸精确对角化（finite-size exact diagonalization）研究自旋哈德纳模型（spinful Haldane model）中拓扑、相互作用与无序的耦合，发现除标准 $C=2$ 拓扑安德森相外，还存在反铁磁 $C=1$ 拓扑安德森相（topological Anderson phase），并用神经网络对其进行分析，结果表明该 $C=1$ 相由安德森无序（Anderson disorder）而非交错质量（staggered mass）诱导的显式电荷不平衡所驱动。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索拓扑（topology）、相互作用（interactions）与无序（disorder）三者协同作用下，自旋哈德纳模型中拓扑安德森绝缘体相（topological Anderson insulating phases）的涌现机制及其物理图像。

Method: 采用有限尺寸精确对角化（finite-size exact diagonalization）计算，并引入神经网络（neural network）对精确对角化数据进行辅助分析与表征。

Result: 在标准 $C=2$ 拓扑安德森相之外，观测到一个反铁磁（antiferromagnetic）$C=1$ 拓扑安德森相，该相与清洁模型中有限交错质量（staggered mass）下的反铁磁量子反常霍尔绝缘体（quantum anomalous Hall insulator）一致。

Conclusion: 支持以下假设：$C=1$ 拓扑安德森相的涌现需要一个显式的电荷不平衡（explicit charge imbalance），该不平衡在本系统中由安德森无序（Anderson disorder）而非交错质量（staggered mass）诱导产生。

Abstract: We examine the emergence of topological Anderson insulating phases in the spinful Haldane model with Hubbard and next-neighbor density-density interactions, subject to Anderson disorder. Using finite-size exact diagonalization, we characterize the phases that arise from the interplay between topology, interactions, and disorder. In addition to standard $C=2$ topological Anderson phases, we observe an antiferromagnetic $C=1$ topological Anderson phase, consistent with the antiferromagnetic quantum anomalous Hall insulator previously identified in the clean model at finite staggered mass. We further analyze these phases using a neural network trained on the exact diagonalization data. Our results support the hypothesis that an explicit charge imbalance is required to induce the $C=1$ phase, generated by Anderson disorder rather than by a staggered mass.

### [66] [MATBG Josephson diode as an universal thermal machine](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27560)
*Hadi Mohammed Soufy,Colin Benjamin*

TL;DR: 本文提出基于魔角扭曲双层石墨烯约瑟夫森结（MATBG-JJ）的量子热机，利用其门可调的谷极化弱链接内禀约瑟夫森二极管效应，构建了量子斯特林、奥托和卡诺循环，以谷极化势Δ_v替代传统超导相位偏置作为控制参数；相比AA堆叠双层石墨烯系统，MATBG平台因平带增强态密度和可调非互易输运，在大范围工作区间内显著提升输出功和效率，并避免了磁通控制带来的噪声问题。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统约瑟夫森热机依赖超导相位偏置（superconducting phase bias）驱动，存在磁通控制和磁通噪声（flux-noise）的限制。本研究旨在利用魔角扭曲双层石墨烯中门可调的谷极化（valley polarization）与非互易超导输运特性，开发一种无磁通（flux-free）的全电调控量子热机新架构。

Method: 构建MATBG约瑟夫森二极管热机，以谷极化势Δ_v作为主要控制参数，分别实现量子斯特林、奥托和卡诺热力学循环。将MATBG二极管热机（MATBG-JDTM）与非二极管型MATBG约瑟夫森结热机（MATBG-JJTM）以及AA堆叠双层石墨烯约瑟夫森结热机（AABLG-JJTM）进行系统性能对比。

Result: MATBG-JDTM与MATBG-JJTM均能在较宽工作区间内，相比AABLG-JJTM显著提升输出功（work output）和热效率（efficiency）。MATBG-JDTM实现了无磁通的全电调控，规避了磁通控制和磁通噪声的固有缺陷。

Conclusion: MATBG约瑟夫森二极管平台被证明是实现电调控量子热机（electrically tunable quantum thermal machines）和非互易超导热电子学（nonreciprocal superconducting caloritronics）的有前景途径。

Abstract: Magic-angle twisted bilayer graphene Josephson junctions (MATBG-JJ) with a gate-tunable valley-polarized weak link exhibit an intrinsic Josephson diode effect originating from broken symmetries associated with valley polarization and band-structure anisotropy. Exploiting this nonreciprocal superconducting platform, we construct quantum Stirling (QSC), Otto (QOC), and Carnot (QCC) thermodynamic cycles, where the valley-polarization potential $Δ_v$ acts as the principal control parameter, in contrast to conventional Josephson thermal machines driven by superconducting phase bias. We systematically compare the performance of MATBG-based Josephson diode thermal machines (MATBG-JDTM) with MATBG-based Josephson junction thermal machines (MATBG-JJTM) and AA-stacked bilayer graphene Josephson junction thermal machines (AABLG-JJTM). Owing to the flat-band-enhanced density of states and electrically tunable nonreciprocal transport in MATBG, both MATBG-JDTM and MATBG-JJTM exhibit significantly enhanced work output and efficiency over a broad operating regime compared to AABLG-JJTM. In particular, the gate-controlled MATBG-JDTM provides a flux-free alternative to conventional phase-driven architectures, mitigating limitations associated with magnetic-flux control and flux-noise effects. Our results establish MATBG Josephson diode platforms as a promising route toward electrically tunable quantum thermal machines and nonreciprocal superconducting caloritronics.

### [67] [A supersymmetric study of charge and spin transport in Weyl semimetals under axionic electrodynamic response](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27657)
*J. C. Pérez-Pedraza,A. Martín-Ruiz,L. F. Urrutia*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文利用低能有效理论，通过手征变换和轴子电动力学，研究外磁场下外尔半金属（Weyl semimetal）的电荷与自旋输运性质，揭示轴子响应与超对称性对输运现象的调控机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索外磁场下外尔半金属中电荷与自旋输运的物理机制，尤其是轴子电动力学（axionic electrodynamics）与超对称性（supersymmetry）如何共同影响输运行为，为外尔半金属的有效场论描述提供新见解。

Method: 采用低能有效理论框架；通过手征变换（chiral transformation）移除费米子拉格朗日量中的轴矢项，将其物理效应保留在电磁响应中；对费米子自由度积分后得到轴子电动力学形式，并通过最小耦合（minimal coupling）引入狄拉克方程（Dirac equation）；对旋量施加罗宾边界条件（Robin boundary conditions）以确定能谱和精确旋量解。

Result: 动力学自然地分解为磁性和电性两部分：磁部门具有超对称因式分解（supersymmetric factorization），电部门呈现PT-超对称（PT-supersymmetric）结构；获得了概率密度和电流密度的手征投影，显示出材料中的手征不平衡；在x方向上仅有一种手征性对手征电流有贡献（j^x_l = 0）；同时计算了自旋密度和自旋电流。

Conclusion: 轴子响应与超对称性之间的相互作用调控了所设系统下的输运现象，为外尔半金属的有效场论描述提供了新见解。

Abstract: We investigate the charge and spin transport properties of a Weyl semimetal under an external magnetic field using a low-energy effective theory. By performing a chiral transformation, we remove the axial term from the fermionic Lagrangian, while its physical effects are retained through the system's electromagnetic response. This response, derived from integrating out the fermionic degrees of freedom, takes the form of axionic electrodynamics and enters the Dirac equation via minimal coupling. The resulting dynamics separate naturally into magnetic and electric components: the magnetic sector admits a supersymmetric factorization, while the electric part exhibits a PT-supersymmetric structure. Robin boundary conditions are applied to the spinor, setting the energy spectrum and defining exact spinor solutions. We obtain the chiral projections of probability and current densities, exhibiting a chiral imbalance in the material. We show that in the x-direction, only one chirality contributes to the chiral current ($j^x_l = 0$). Spin density and currents where also computed. Our results demonstrate how the interplay between axionic response and supersymmetry governs transport phenomena in our specific setup, offering novel insights into the effective field theory description of Weyl semimetals.

### [68] [Spin-Hall-Like Magnon Transport in a Synthetic Antiferromagnetic Skyrmion Lattice](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27822)
*Xingen Zheng,Xuejuan Liu,Zhenyu Wang,Jiyong Kang,Zhixiong Li,Hao Wu*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文研究由两个磁纹理相反的反铁磁耦合斯格明子晶格层构成的合成反铁磁斯格明子晶格中类似自旋霍尔效应的磁子边缘输运，发现层极化的反向传播边缘模式源于两层斯格明子晶格相反的霍尔趋势，而非真正的Z₂拓扑保护螺旋边缘态。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索合成反铁磁斯格明子晶格（synthetic antiferromagnetic skyrmion lattice）中的磁子边缘输运（magnon edge transport）行为，并检验其是否具有受Z₂拓扑保护的螺旋边缘态。

Method: 基于微磁模拟（micromagnetic simulation）获得弛豫的双层磁纹理，在线性自旋波理论（linear spin-wave theory）框架下构建玻色型Bogoliubov-de Gennes哈密顿量（bosonic Bogoliubov-de Gennes Hamiltonian），计算体态和条带磁子谱，并进行动力学微磁模拟和对称性分析。

Result: 发现了具有相反层极化的反向传播能隙内边缘模式（counterpropagating in-gap edge modes），其层分辨传播特性得到动力学微磁模拟的确认。对称性分析表明完全耦合的系统缺乏真正的玻色型Z₂拓扑相所需的赝时间反演对称性（pseudo-time-reversal symmetry）。

Conclusion: 所观察到的边缘模式并非Z₂保护的螺旋磁子边缘态，而是起源于两层斯格明子晶格相反霍尔趋势的层极化自旋霍尔类模式（spin-Hall-like modes）。合成反铁磁斯格明子晶格可作为一个超越严格玻色型Z₂分类的自旋霍尔类磁子输运平台。

Abstract: We investigate spin-Hall-like magnon edge transport in a synthetic antiferromagnetic skyrmion lattice composed of two antiferromagnetically coupled skyrmion lattice layers with opposite magnetic textures. Based on a relaxed bilayer texture from micromagnetic simulations, we construct the bosonic Bogoliubov-de Gennes Hamiltonian within linear spin-wave theory and calculate the bulk and strip magnon spectrum. We find counterpropagating in-gap edge modes with opposite layer polarization, whose layer-resolved propagation is further confirmed by dynamical micromagnetic simulations. A symmetry analysis shows that the fully coupled system lacks the pseudo-time-reversal symmetry required for a genuine bosonic Z2 topological phase. Thus, the observed edge modes are not Z2-protected helical magnon edge states, but layer-polarized, spin-Hall-like modes originating from the opposite Hall tendencies of the two skyrmion lattice layers. These results establish synthetic antiferromagnetic skyrmion lattices as a platform for spin-Hall-like magnon transport beyond a strict bosonic Z2 classification.

### [69] [Quantum anomalous Hall effect in chiral semimetals](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27826)
*Peng-Yi Liu,Yu-Hao Wan,Qing-Feng Sun*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文通过理论论证和输运计算，证明量子反常霍尔（QAH）效应不仅存在于陈绝缘体（Chern insulator）和铁磁金属中，还可以存在于手性半金属（chiral semimetal）中，并揭示了其独特的半金属性量子化输运特征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子反常霍尔效应传统上被认为仅存在于陈绝缘体中，近期研究表明铁磁金属也可承载该效应。本文旨在探索介于绝缘体和金属之间的手性半金属是否也能实现QAH效应，从而扩展QAH效应的概念范畴。

Method: 通过输运计算（transport calculations）分析手性半金属体系的霍尔电导率和纵向电导率行为，并研究体系在退相干（dephasing）存在下的量子化响应。

Result: 手性半金属在导带和价带于零能处接触的情况下，仍可维持QAH效应；其霍尔电导率在退相干存在下可被量子化，同时纵向电导率保持有限且呈现半金属行为；该体系可向陈绝缘体转变，伴随纵向电导率消失和霍尔响应内在长度尺度减小。

Conclusion: QAH效应可以存在于手性半金属中，其异常输运行为源于占据态贝里曲率积分（Berry curvature integral）的量子化与半金属能带结构的共同作用；该发现拓展了QAH效应的概念，并揭示了半金属性QAH的独特输运特征。

Abstract: The quantum anomalous Hall (QAH) effect is conventionally understood to exist only in Chern insulators, while a recent study has shown that ferromagnetic metals can also host the QAH effect. Between insulators and metals, we demonstrate that QAH can persist even in a chiral semimetal, where conduction and valence bands touch at zero energy. Transport calculations demonstrate that the Hall conductivity of such a system can be quantized in the presence of dephasing. Interestingly, its longitudinal conductivity remains finite and exhibits semimetallic behavior, in contrast to Chern insulators. This unusual transport behavior originates from the quantization of the Berry curvature integral over occupied states and the semimetallic band structure. This chiral semimetal can transition into a Chern insulator, accompanied by the vanishing of longitudinal conductivity and a reduction of the intrinsic length scale of the Hall response. Our results extend the concept of QAH and uncover the semimetallic QAH transport signatures.

### [70] [Taming quantum interference: a route to high electrical conductance in carbon nanotube assemblies](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28250)
*Teresa Kulka,Agnieszka E. Lekawa-Raus,John S. Bulmer,Krzysztof Koziol,Fedor F. Balakirev,Irina V. Lebedeva,Jacek A. Majewski,Magdalena Marganska,Karolina Z. Milowska*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本研究通过原子尺度紧束缚非平衡格林函数计算，系统探索了从单壁碳纳米管（SWCNT）到多壁碳纳米管（MWCNT）结中的相干电子输运，揭示了结结构对量子干涉的调控机制，并将微观干涉机制转化为高电导、场稳定的碳纳米管导体设计原则。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 小型化电子器件需要轻量化且在苛刻条件下保持高电导的导体。碳纳米管网络是候选材料，但其输运受制于管间结（inter-nanotube junctions）中的电子波干涉。控制这一干涉需要理解结结构（junction architecture）如何影响透射。

Method: 采用原子尺度紧束缚非平衡格林函数（tight-binding non-equilibrium Green's-function, NEGF）方法，在垂直磁场下计算了从单壁碳纳米管（SWCNT）到双壁碳纳米管（DWCNT）和三壁碳纳米管（TWCNT）结的相干输运。同时使用可解析求解的最小模型和电子波导图景（electron-waveguide picture）进行解释。

Result: 对于单SWCNT-SWCNT结，高透射窗口主要由重叠长度（overlap length）、掺杂和磁场决定。当某些子带（subbands）存在能隙时，网关态（gateway states）可增强电导；某些情况下磁场可通过解除干涉阻塞恢复透射。多结产生共振滤波效应，附加壁层作为选择性路径而非独立通道。DWCNT结仍以管壁为主，类似SWCNT，而TWCNT结呈现真正的多通道行为并对磁场更敏感。

Conclusion: 这解释了多壁碳纳米管（MWCNT）纤维电导较低且对磁场更敏感的现象，与在SWCNT和MWCNT纤维上的超高场测量结果一致。本研究将微观干涉机制转化为高电导、场稳定碳纳米管导体的设计原则。

Abstract: Miniaturized electronics require lightweight conductors that maintain high conductance under demanding conditions. CNT networks are promising candidates, but their transport is governed by inter-nanotube junctions where electron waves interfere. Controlling this interference requires understanding how junction architecture shapes transmission. We explore coherent transport through experimentally relevant junctions, from single and multiple single-walled CNT (SWCNT) contacts to double-walled CNT (DWCNT) and triple-walled CNT (TWCNT) junctions, with atomistic tight-binding non-equilibrium Green's-function calculations, also under a perpendicular magnetic field. We use analytically solvable minimal models to identify transport regimes expected for quasi-1D nanoscale junctions, and an electron-waveguide picture to interpret their CNT-specific manifestations. For single SWCNT--SWCNT junctions, high-transmission windows are set mainly by overlap length, doping and magnetic field. Gateway states can enhance conductance when some CNT subbands are gapped, and in some cases a magnetic field can restore transmission by lifting an interference blockade. In more complex architectures, added paths become selective: multi-junctions generate resonant filtering, while additional walls redistribute transmission instead of acting as independent channels. DWCNT junctions remain outer-wall dominated and SWCNT-like, whereas TWCNT junctions become genuinely multi-channel and more field-sensitive. This explains the lower, more field-sensitive conductance of multi-walled CNT (MWCNT) fibres, in accord with our ultrahigh-field measurements on SWCNT and MWCNT fibres. Ultimately, this work turns microscopic interference mechanisms into design principles for high-conductance, field-stable CNT conductors.

</details>

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 利用单分子电子发射器，通过调节激发光子能量，选择性地激发不同空间对称性（spatial symmetry）的分子态，从而在同一个局域场热点内实现电子出生位点在分子不同位置之间的可逆切换，并通过远场发射图案（far-field emission pattern）直接读取切换结果。

Abstract: Optical control of electron-generation sites has broadly enabled ultrafast nanoscale imaging, spectroscopy, and functional control. Existing approaches achieve nanoscale site selectivity by shaping localised optical fields around nanostructures, thereby limiting independent site selectivity within the same local-field hotspot. Here, using a single-molecule electron emitter, we show that site selectivity can instead be encoded in the electronic excitation pathway, enabling subnanometric control of electron birth sites within the same local-field hotspot. By tuning the photon energy, we selectively access molecular states of different spatial symmetry and reversibly switch the electron birth site between distinct locations in the same emitter, with the change read out directly in the far-field emission pattern. The switching depends on photon energy alone and is absent under variations in intensity or polarisation. Our results establish optical birth-site selectivity that is not dictated by the local-field distribution, opening a route to electron birth-site control through the electronic excitation pathway.

Method: 在保持激发条件不变的前提下，逐步增加Fe层的限域程度；结合对自旋、载流子和声子敏感的超快实验，辅以第一性原理（ab initio）计算和原子自旋动力学（atomistic spin dynamics）模拟进行验证。

Result: 厚度低于10 nm的Fe层表现出增大的退磁幅度，2 nm厚的Fe层退磁幅度增加了约75%。该有限尺寸效应（finite-size effect）源于磁性本身，而非声子驱动；其增强机制是Fe界面处自旋有序（spin order）的局部削弱，在高度限域条件下变得显著。

Conclusion: 研究表明，尺寸限域可以显著增强Fe薄膜的飞秒退磁幅度，且该效应在磁性起源上成立。这一发现为在纳米尺度器件中利用超快自旋动力学（ultrafast spin dynamics）提供了物理基础，有望推动自旋电子学器件速度的进一步突破。

Abstract: Nanoscale miniaturization has revolutionized the field of spintronics by enabling exponential growth in areal bit density. A similar leap is also expected in device speeds through successfully harnessing femtosecond magnetization dynamics. However, combining this with the miniaturization of realistic devices is challenging. To address this, we studied the effect of dimensional confinement on the femtosecond demagnetization of Fe. By gradually increasing the level of confinement while keeping excitation conditions constant, we found that Fe layers thinner than 10 nm exhibit enlarged demagnetization amplitudes, reaching a $\sim75\%$ increase at 2 nm. By combining ultrafast experiments sensitive to the spins, the charge carriers, and the phonons, we establish that this finite$\text{-}$size effect is magnetic in origin and is not phonon$\text{-}$driven. With the support of ab$\text{-}$initio calculations and atomistic spin dynamics simulations, we identify the enhancement effect as due to local weakening of spin order at the Fe$\text{'}$s interface, which becomes significant upon increased confinement.

### [73] [Unity-order coupling between free electrons and multiphoton waveguided Fock states](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28383)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 理论论证：采用一个偏置矩形硅波导（silicon waveguide），利用排斥性静电场使掠射电子发生偏转，通过电子入射角度和施加偏压动态调控电子转向点，进而控制耦合强度与模式选择性。

Result: 电子转向点同时决定耦合强度与模式选择性，可动态调控；逃逸电子-波导相互作用（aloof interaction）抑制了高能损耗通道（如硅带隙以上），同时保持对目标波导模式的有效激发。在实用偏置构型与100 keV电子条件下，预测平均产额超过每电子十个光子，且可通过电压调谐控制相互作用。

Conclusion: 静电场偏转为工程化并增强自由电子与波导光子模式的耦合提供了一条实用路径。

Abstract: Electron beams enable highly localized near-field excitation of waveguided optical modes, yet their coupling is typically limited by short interaction times along straight-line trajectories with fixed impact parameters. Here, we theoretically demonstrate that electrostatic steering overcomes this limitation by introducing a tunable turning point in grazing electron trajectories, thus controlling the minimum electron--waveguide separation and producing strong coupling to waveguided modes. Specifically, we consider a biased rectangular silicon waveguide, where a repulsive static field deflects a grazing electron. In this configuration, the electron turning point governs both the coupling strength and the modal selectivity, which can be dynamically tuned through the electron incidence angle and the applied bias. In addition, the aloof electron--waveguide interaction suppresses lossy high-energy channels (e.g., above the silicon band gap) while preserving substantial excitation of the targeted waveguided modes. Using a practical biasing configuration and 100~keV electrons, we predict an average yield exceeding ten photons per electron, with voltage-tunable control of the interaction. Our results establish electrostatic steering as a practical route for engineering and enhancing free-electron coupling to waveguided photonic modes.

### [74] [Symmetry-Selective Topological Magnon Engineering by Phonon Angular Momentum](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28425)
*Markus Weißenhofer,Philipp Rieger,Chandan K. Singh,M. S. Mrudul,Sergiy Mankovsky,Peter M. Oppeneer*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文基于第一性原理自旋-晶格耦合与Floquet理论，证明通过相干驱动声子可以对称性选择性地控制磁振子能带结构：线偏振声子不改变能谱，而携带有限声子角动量（PAM）的圆/椭圆偏振声子能打开并调控狄拉克点处的能隙，进而产生和翻转拓扑磁振子相。以单层CrI₃为例，研究建立了驱动晶格动力学作为工程化拓扑玻色子激发的通用路径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 贝里曲率（Berry curvature）的动力操控一直是拓扑相工程中的关键挑战，现有方法难以实现对磁振子能带的灵活调控。

Method: 采用第一性原理（\textit{ab initio}）自旋-晶格耦合计算结合Floquet理论（Floquet theory），分析不同偏振（线偏振、圆偏振、椭圆偏振）相干声子驱动对磁振子能带结构的影响，并以单层CrI₃为模型体系进行验证。

Result: 线偏振声子不改变磁振子能谱；圆/椭圆偏振声子因携带有限声子角动量（phonon angular momentum, PAM）而诱导手性相互作用，在狄拉克点（Dirac points）处打开并调控能隙，实现拓扑磁振子相的产生与翻转；能隙大小和陈数（Chern numbers）直接由PAM控制，从而实现手性选择性拓扑操控。

Conclusion: 该结果证明了驱动晶格动力学是工程化拓扑玻色子激发（topological bosonic excitations）的通用途径，并为Floquet控制磁性（Floquet control of magnetism）提供了多功能平台。

Abstract: Dynamical control of Berry curvature remains an outstanding challenge in the engineering of topological phases. Here, we demonstrate control of magnon band structures via coherently driven phonons, based on \textit{ab initio} spin-lattice coupling and Floquet theory. We show that this control is symmetry selective: linearly polarized phonons leave the spectrum unchanged, whereas circular and elliptical phonons carrying finite phonon angular momentum (PAM) induce chiral interactions that open and tune gaps at Dirac points, generating and reversing topological magnon phases. The gap magnitude and Chern numbers are directly governed by the PAM, enabling handedness-selective topology control. Applied to monolayer CrI$_3$, and supported by symmetry analysis, our results establish driven lattice dynamics as a general route to engineering topological bosonic excitations and a versatile platform for Floquet control of magnetism.

### [75] [Substrate-driven topological engineering in plasmonic Su-Schrieffer-Heeger chains](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28463)

Abstract: We demonstrate the possibility of engineering the topological band structure of a plasmonic Su-Schrieffer-Heeger (SSH) chain through the interaction with its electromagnetic environment. On the other hand, the short-range interaction with the substrate introduces a band touching, again with a change in the Zak phase. Surprisingly, this second mechanism enables the emergence of topologically protected edge modes for parameters which correspond to the topologically trivial phase for an isolated plasmonic SSH chain. We study these mechanisms by changing the chain-substrate distance and the dimerization parameter. An in-plane magnetic field opens a gap in the one-dimensional edge spectrum, while changes in the edge orientation generate localized in-gap states at the kinks. We show that, for suitable geometry and magnetic-field direction, two such states form an effective lithographically defined two-level subsystem. Using an edge-state model that includes both the localized levels and the continuum states outside the magnetic-field-induced gap, we calculate the electric-dipole matrix elements and solve the time-dependent problem under resonant driving. The resulting dynamics exhibits Rabi oscillations with linear frequencies of $20$--$40$~GHz for realistic parameters. We find that the continuum states provide a leakage channel whose strength is strongly controlled by the driving amplitude: reducing the electric field suppresses leakage below the percent level while preserving GHz-scale coherent oscillations. These results establish a route from magnetic-field-induced corner-state physics to electrically driven two-level dynamics in a realistic two-dimensional topological-insulator edge geometry.

</details>


### [77] [Photon correlation microscopy of quantum matter](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28623)
*Elie Vandoolaeghe,Iñigo Lasheras,Chirag Vaswani,Sampriti Saha,Purbasha Ray,Takashi Taniguchi,Kenji Watanabe,Prasana Sahoo,Nicolò Defenu,Thibault Chervy,Puneet A. Murthy*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文提出光子关联显微镜（PCM），通过探测发射光的关联来研究介观尺度量子物质中的多体关联，并在单层MoSe₂-WSe₂异质结的一维偶极激子体系中验证了该方法，观测到从可压缩相到不可压缩相的转变以及光子统计从聚束到反聚束的演化，标志着多体阻塞效应的出现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子光学与多体物理虽共享基本统计特性，但各自的实验探测手段长期沿不同轨迹发展：多体物理探索涌现集体现象，而量子光学则精于测量单个光子间的关联。本文旨在弥合这两个领域，建立一种通过发射光关联来探测量子物质中多体关联的实验方法。

Method: 本文引入光子关联显微镜（photon correlation microscopy, PCM），利用发射光的关联来探测介观（mesoscopic）尺度量子物质中的关联。实验上采用单层MoSe₂-WSe₂横向异质结中的一维（1D）偶极激子（dipolar exciton）系综，通过栅极定义势垒将一维激子限制在介观尺度，以增强物质关联在发射光子场中的可见性。

Result: 功率依赖光谱显示从可压缩相到不可压缩相的转变，表现为发射强度饱和与能量蓝移的同步出现，数值模拟支持该结果。光子关联测量在这一交叉过程中展现出从低密度下的聚束（bunching）到高密度下的反聚束（antibunching）的显著演化，这构成了由集体偶极排斥驱动、直接源于数稳定化态的光子发射多体阻塞（many-body blockade）效应。

Conclusion: PCM可作为通过量子光学视角探测多体物理的有力工具，可推广至广泛的关联电子相，同时为通过多体关联产生非经典光指明了方向。

Abstract: Light and matter share fundamental statistical properties, yet the experimental probes of quantum optics and many-body physics have largely evolved along separate trajectories. While many-body physics explores emergent collective phenomena, quantum optics has refined the measurement of correlations between individual photons. Here, we introduce photon correlation microscopy (PCM) - which bridges the two domains by leveraging correlations of emitted light to probe the correlations in quantum matter at mesoscopic scales. We demonstrate this approach using a one-dimensional (1D) ensemble of dipolar excitons confined at a lateral monolayer MoSe$_2$-WSe$_2$ heterojunction. We use gate-defined potentials to confine the 1D excitons to a mesoscopic lengthscale to enhance the visibility of matter correlations in the emitted photon field. Power-dependent spectroscopy reveals a transition from a compressible to an incompressible phase, signaled by the simultaneous saturation of the emission intensity and energy blueshift, which is supported by numerical simulations. Through this crossover, photon correlation measurements show a striking evolution from bunching at low densities to antibunching at high densities. This constitutes a many-body blockade of photon emission emerging directly from a number-stabilized state, driven by collective dipolar repulsion. Our results establish PCM as a powerful probe of many-body physics through the lens of quantum optics, extensible to a broad class of correlated electronic phases, while pointing toward a route to generating non-classical light through many-body correlations.

### [78] [Multiscale Vectorial Determination of Magnetic Order Parameters using Electron Magnetic Linear Dichroism](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28790)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有电子二色性技术主要针对标量磁序参数，缺乏对矢量磁序参数（如奈尔矢量Néel vector或磁化方向）具有纳米分辨率的定量探测手段，尤其难以区分磁信号与非磁各向异性信号。

Method: 将矢量芯能级交换分裂明确纳入混合动态形状因子模拟中，并考虑动力学衍射（dynamical diffraction）效应，从而基于动量分辨电子能量损失谱实现磁自旋轴（magnetic spin axis）的直接重建。

Result: 该二色性信号本质上可与非磁各向异性分离，对奈尔矢量或磁化取向具有明确的依赖关系，并在原子尺度下保持稳健。在立方FeRh（cubic FeRh）的共线反铁磁（collinear antiferromagnetic）和铁磁（ferromagnetic）相中成功实现了磁矢量的定量实空间映射。

Conclusion: 该方法为反铁磁体（antiferromagnets）和交变磁体（altermagnets）的纳米级光谱学与成像开辟了新途径，其中广义的电子二色性方法可直接访问不同的磁序参数。

Abstract: We demonstrate electron magnetic linear dichroism as a quantitative probe of vectorial magnetic order parameters with nanometer resolution in transmission electron microscopy. Explicit inclusion of vectorial core-level exchange splitting into mixed dynamic form factor simulations accounting for dynamical diffraction enables direct reconstruction of the magnetic spin axis from momentum-resolved electron energy-loss spectra. The resulting dichroic signal is intrinsically separable from nonmagnetic anisotropy, exhibits a well-defined dependence on the Néel vector or magnetization orientation, and remains robust down to the atomic scale. Applied to the collinear antiferromagnetic and ferromagnetic phase of cubic FeRh, this approach allows quantitative real-space mapping of the magnetic vector. These results open a pathway to nanoscale spectroscopy and imaging of antiferromagnets and altermagnets where the generalized approach to electron dichroism provides direct access to different magnetic order parameters.

### [79] [Gauge Geometry of Hodge Zero-Mode Transport in Parameter-Dependent Topological Data Analysis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28326)
*Satoshi Kanno,Rei Nishimura,Hiroshi Yamauchi,Yoshi-aki Shimada*

Main category: math.AT

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于组合霍奇拉普拉斯算子（combinatorial Hodge Laplacian）零模（zero modes）追踪同调特征（homological features）的计算框架，通过曲率（curvature）和和乐（holonomy）描述演化拓扑结构中的局部重组与累积记忆，实现了对参数依赖拓扑数据中结构变化的检测。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 持久性图（persistence diagrams）虽能描述拓扑特征的生灭，但无法充分捕捉特征随时间或参数变化的组织结构演化。为克服这一局限，需要一种能追踪同调特征在共同链空间中重组的计算方法。

Method: 将同调特征表示为普通组合霍奇拉普拉斯算子的零模，在公共环境链空间中追踪对应的特征空间；并据此计算曲率和和乐，分别作为局部重组和累积记忆的描述子。

Result: 在受控时间依赖点云数据上的数值实验表明，该方法能够检测跟踪不稳定性、区分具有几乎相同持久性图的系统，并捕捉点态特征匹配无法察觉的循环级记忆。

Conclusion: 零模输运几何（zero-mode transport geometry）可作为分析动态拓扑数据的有效计算工具；文中还给出了稳定性估计，证明这些描述子在正则区域上对霍奇拉普拉斯算子的扰动具有鲁棒性。

Abstract: We propose a practical computational framework for detecting structural changes in parameter-dependent topological data. In many applications, such as time-series data analysis, anomaly detection, and monitoring of systems under changing control parameters, persistence diagrams describe the birth and death of topological features at each parameter value, but they do not fully capture how these features are reorganized over time. To address this limitation, we represent homological features by zero modes of the ordinary combinatorial Hodge Laplacian and track the corresponding feature spaces in a common ambient chain space. This allows us to compute curvature and holonomy as descriptors of local reorganization and accumulated memory in evolving topological structures. Curvature highlights parameter regions where homological features mix or change rapidly, while holonomy summarizes the net effect of such changes after a closed cycle. We also establish stability estimates showing that these descriptors are robust under perturbations of the Hodge Laplacian on regular regions. Numerical experiments on controlled time-dependent point-cloud data show that the proposed method detects tracking instability, distinguishes systems with nearly identical persistence diagrams, and captures cycle-level memory invisible to pointwise feature matching. These results suggest that zero-mode transport geometry can serve as a useful computational tool for analyzing dynamic topological data.
