### [80] [On the Equivariant Learning of the $Q$-tensor Order Parameter](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27679)
*Julia Navarro,Mark Wilkinson*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文构建并评估了七种不同阶数的循环群等变神经网络（group-equivariant neural networks），用于从合成生成的微观纹理图像预测二维向列相液晶的Q张量序参量。实验表明，所有等变模型均满足Q张量等变约束达到单精度浮点精度，相比非等变基准模型，等变模型在误差和泛化鲁棒性上表现更优，且性能随群阶数增加而提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 从微观纹理图像预测向列相液晶的Q张量序参量是一个具有挑战性的任务，现有非等变模型无法充分利用图像中存在的旋转对称性，导致误差偏高且泛化能力有限。因此，本文旨在引入群等变神经网络以系统利用旋转对称性，提升预测精度和鲁棒性。

Method: 利用权重共享约束（weight-sharing constraints）、等变激活函数（equivariant activations）和正则化技术（regularization techniques），构建七种分别等变于循环群（cyclic group）$C_k$（$k=4,8,16,32,64,128,256$）的神经网络架构。具体构造了作用于行向量化图像的旋转类置换矩阵群元素$\varrho_{C_k}(g)$，以近似实现方形图像上圆形子域的$\frac{2π}{k}$旋转。

Result: 所有七个等变模型均满足Q张量等变约束，误差达到单精度浮点精度（single-precision floating point accuracy）。与采用数据增强（data augmentation）或不采用数据增强的参数匹配非等变基准模型相比，等变模型在误差上持续更低，并对未见缺陷构型（unseen defect configurations）具有更鲁棒的泛化能力。性能随群阶数增加而提升。

Conclusion: 纳入更精细的旋转对称性有助于降低预测误差，循环群等变神经网络在液晶Q张量预测任务中优于非等变方法。这为利用群等变性提升物理系统序参量预测的精度和泛化性提供了有效方案。

Abstract: We construct and evaluate group-equivariant neural networks for the prediction of the two-dimensional $Q$-tensor order parameter of nematic liquid crystals from synthetically generated microscopic textures. Seven architectures, equivariant to cyclic groups $C_k$ of order $k$ for $k=4,\,8,\,16,\,32,\,64,\,128,\, 256$, are built using a combination of weight-sharing constraints, equivariant activations and regularization techniques. To do this, we construct rotation-like permutation matrix groups with elements $\varrho_{C_k}(g)$ that act on row-wise vectorized images, thereby approximating a $\frac{2π}{k}$ rotation of the circular subdomain on square images. We show that all seven equivariant models satisfy the $Q$-tensor equivariance constraint to within single-precision floating point accuracy. Comparing against approximate parameter-matched non-equivariant benchmarks, with and without data augmentation, we find that the equivariant models consistently achieve lower errors and generalize more robustly to unseen defect configurations. Performance increases with group order, suggesting that the incorporation of finer rotational symmetry leads to lower errors.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Conclusion: DGRPT为玻璃态聚合物膜分离复杂液体混合物提供了一种自洽且准确的理论框架，其高阶扩展版本已被审查和评估，有望进一步拓展适用范围。

Abstract: This manuscript reviews the development, application and extensions of the dry glass reference perturbation theory (DGRPT) closure to the non-equilibrium thermodynamics of glassy polymers (NETGP). DGRPT was developed to allow for the self-consistent and accurate predictions of sorption from complex liquid mixtures into glassy polymers. ### [82] [Order by inertia in spinning active matter: holey fluids and spin-textured crystals](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28386)
*Camille Jorge,Denis Bartolo*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文通过实验研究高雷诺数下宏观自旋体的二维组装，揭示了惯性活性物质（inertial active matter）中的两个相变：低密度下的渗透转变形成稀薄空穴液体，以及高密度下的一级相变形成自旋有序晶体，证明惯性流中的 hydrodynamic feedback 可以促进而非破坏多体有序。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 惯性活性物质能否在多体层面维持真正的内聚（cohesion）与有序尚不清楚，这挑战了以往认为结构-流动反馈会破坏晶体或液晶有序的观点。实验已表明惯性流体流动可稳定少数自旋体的束缚态，但多体情形尚未被探索。

Method: 研究了宏观自旋体（macroscopic spinners）在雷诺数（Reynolds number）较高的条件下形成的二维组装，观测其从低密度到高密度的结构演化。

Result: 低密度下，惯性流产生各向异性吸引和横向马格努斯力（Magnus forces），导致键的持续断裂与重组，驱动渗透转变形成动态重构的“空穴液体”（holey liquid），类似于平衡态斑块胶体（patchy colloids）中的空穴液体态。高密度下，自旋对齐与粒子位置的反馈抑制横向重组，发生一级相变形成自旋有序晶体（spin-ordered crystal）。

Conclusion: 在过阻尼极限（overdamped limit）之外，流体动力学反馈（hydrodynamic feedback）可以促进而非破坏集体有序，揭示了一个由惯性流主导的多体活性物质（many-body active matter）的新相态区域。

Abstract: Active matter sustains emergent flows at the expense of preserving structural order. The feedback between structure and viscous flows typically disrupts crystalline and liquid-crystalline organization by amplifying the very deformations they generate. Yet this destabilizing paradigm has recently been challenged by experiments showing that inertial fluid flows can stabilize few-body bound states of active spinners. Whether inertial active matter can sustain genuine cohesion and order at the many-body level, however, remains elusive. Here we investigate two-dimensional assemblies of macroscopic spinners operating at high Reynolds number and uncover two phase transitions leading to the emergence of a dilute percolating fluid and a dense spin-textured crystal. At low density, inertial flows generate two competing interactions: anisotropic attractions and transverse Magnus forces that continuously break and reconfigure bonds. Together they drive a percolation transition toward a dynamically rearranging holey liquid reminiscent of the empty-liquid states observed in equilibrium patchy colloids. At high density, the feedback between spin alignment and particle positions suppresses transverse rearrangements and yields a first-order transition toward a spin-ordered crystal. Our results demonstrate that, beyond the overdamped limit, hydrodynamic feedback can promote rather than destroy collective order, revealing a distinct regime of many-body active matter governed by inertial flows.

### [83] [Complex abelian varieties and quantum error correction: a mathematical framework for GKP codes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28784)
*Maxence Mayrand,Baptiste Royer*

Main category: math.AG

TL;DR: 本文通过复阿贝尔簇（complex abelian varieties）的几何结构研究了一类由Gottesman–Kitaev–Preskill（GKP）引入的量子纠错码，建立了GKP码理论与阿贝尔簇经典理论之间的精确数学词典，并证明了编码的渐近等距性、逻辑Clifford门的Gaussian幺正实现，以及小方差噪声下失效率由极化同源核中最短非平凡位移（systolic不变量）主导等关键结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子纠错码（quantum error-correcting codes）中的GKP码在物理文献中常以启发式形式出现，缺乏严格的数学基础。本文旨在通过复阿贝尔簇的几何语言，为GKP码提供精确的数学表述，填补理论空白。

Method: 利用辛积分格（symplectically integral lattices）构造GKP码与极化复阿贝尔簇（polarized complex abelian varieties）之间的对应关系，建立包含代码空间、逻辑Pauli门、逻辑Clifford门及级联操作在内的数学词典；并基于此框架分析编码的渐近等距性质、Gaussian幺正实现及失效率的systolic约束。

Result: 证明了编码是渐近等距的（asymptotically isometric）；每个逻辑Clifford门均可由Gaussian幺正（Gaussian unitary）实现；在小方差噪声下，失效率（failure probability）的一阶行为由极化同源核（kernel of the polarization isogeny）中最短非平凡位移决定，即底层极化结构的systolic不变量（systolic invariant）。

Conclusion: 该工作为GKP码建立了严格的数学基础，将物理问题转化为极化阿贝尔簇模空间（moduli space of polarized abelian varieties）上的优化问题，为量子纠错码的理论与性能分析开辟了几何视角。

Abstract: We study a class of quantum error-correcting codes through the geometry of complex abelian varieties. These codes, introduced by Gottesman--Kitaev--Preskill, are built from symplectically integral lattices and therefore naturally define polarized complex abelian varieties. We give a precise mathematical formulation of this relationship and extend it to a dictionary between the main structures of GKP code theory and classical objects in the theory of abelian varieties. For instance, under this dictionary, the finite-dimensional code space becomes the space of theta functions $H^0(X, L)$, logical Pauli gates arise from the theta group, passive logical Clifford gates correspond to automorphisms of the polarized abelian variety, and concatenation with stabilizer codes corresponds to isogeny. We also prove several key results that give precise mathematical formulations of statements about these codes that often appear in heuristic form in the physics literature. In particular, we prove that the encoding is asymptotically isometric, that every logical Clifford gate is realized by a Gaussian unitary, and that, for noise of small variance, the failure probability is governed to first order by the shortest nontrivial displacement in the kernel of the polarization isogeny, a systolic invariant of the underlying polarization. This leads naturally to optimization problems on the moduli space of polarized abelian varieties.

</details>

### [84] [High-temperature instability of artificial cuprorivaite: a study using thermal analysis, X-ray powder diffractometry and polarized light microscopy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27455)
*Vladimir A. Yuryev,Sergey V. Kuznetsov,Alexander A. Alexandrov,Tatyana V. Yuryeva*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本研究通过差示扫描量热法（DSC）、热重分析（TG）、X射线粉末衍射（XRD）和偏光光学显微镜（polarization optical microscopy）等手段，系统研究了CaCuSi₄O₁₀（铜硅钙石）从室温至1450°C的热分解行为。结果表明，铜硅钙石在约1020°C开始发生不一致熔融（incongruent melting），DSC吸热峰最低点在1064.4°C；该分解不可逆，后续循环退火无法使其重新合成。经两次退火至1450°C后，样品转变为由单斜鳞石英（monoclinic tridymite）针状晶体与CuO–Cu₂O–CaO–SiO₂成分的绿色玻璃组成的两相体系，两者质量比约为12:13。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: CaCuSi₄O₁₀（cuprorivaite）是一种历史悠久的蓝色颜料（埃及蓝），其高温稳定性与分解机制对文物保护和材料科学具有重要意义。此前对该化合物在高温下的相变与分解产物缺乏系统研究，尤其是其熔融行为、产物组成及可逆性尚不明确。本研究旨在填补这一空白，为相关应用提供热力学和结构依据。

Method: 采用差示扫描量热法（differential scanning calorimetry, DSC）和热重分析（thermogravimetry, TG）在室温至1450°C范围内以20°C/min的升降温速率进行热分析。同时，利用X射线粉末衍射（powder X-ray diffraction, XRD）和偏光光学显微镜（polarization optical microscopy）表征不同热处理阶段产物的物相组成与微观形貌。

Result: CaCuSi₄O₁₀在约1020°C开始发生不一致熔融（incongruent melting），对应的DSC吸热峰最低点位于1064.4°C。该分解过程不可逆，即使在1450°C下进行多次循环退火（cyclic annealing）也无法重新合成原始相。经两次退火至1450°C后，样品转变为两相体系：单斜鳞石英（monoclinic tridymite）针状晶体与成分为CuO–Cu₂O–CaO–SiO₂的绿色玻璃，鳞石英与玻璃的质量比约为12:13。

Conclusion: CaCuSi₄O₁₀在高温下发生不可逆的不一致熔融分解，无法通过热循环重新合成。其完全分解产物为由鳞石英晶体和含铜钙硅酸盐玻璃组成的两相混合物，具体质量比为12:13。该结果明确了铜硅钙石的热稳定性上限及分解路径，为相关材料的高温应用与保护提供了关键参考数据。

Abstract: CaCuSi$_4$O$_{10}$ powder was studied by differential scanning calorimetry and thermogravimetry methods in the range from room temperature to 1450$\,^{\circ}$C at heating and cooling rates of 20$\,^{\circ}$C/min.
  The process of decomposition of cuprorivaite, the composition and transformations of its decomposition products during successive heat treatments were also studied by powder X-ray diffraction and polarization optical microscopy techniques.
  It was found that CaCuSi$_4$O$_{10}$ starts to decompose by incongruent melting at a temperature of about 1020$\,^{\circ}$C, with the minimum of the endothermic DSC peak associated with this process being at 1064.4$\,^{\circ}$C.
  CaCuSi$_4$O$_{10}$ decomposes irreversibly and subsequent cyclic annealings up to a temperature of 1450$\,^{\circ}$C at heating and cooling rates of 20$\,^{\circ}$C/min do not cause its re-synthesis.
  CaCuSi$_4$O$_{10}$ transforms into a two-phase system consisting of acicular crystals of monoclinic tridymite fused with green glass with the composition CuO$\,-\,$Cu$_2$O$\,-\,$CaO$\,-\,$SiO$_2$, with the weight ratio of tridymite to glass being about $12:13$, as a result of two successive annealings up to the temperature of 1450$\,^{\circ}$C.

</details>

Abstract: Reducing coating thermal noise in future gravitational-wave detectors requires identifying the atomic motifs that control mechanical loss in amorphous optical coatings. We combine grazing-incidence X-ray pair distribution function measurements with atomic-structure modeling to study amorphous TiO$_2$-doped GeO$_2$ films over Ti cation concentrations from $\sim$11 % to $\sim$48 %, before and after annealing. The structural analysis reveals systematic composition- and annealing-dependent changes in short- and intermediate-range order. Increasing Ti content raises the average Ti coordination and promotes edge- and face-sharing polyhedral connections, while Ge remains predominantly fourfold coordinated. Annealing reduces these compact shared-polyhedron motifs and sharpens the first sharp diffraction peak, indicating a more relaxed intermediate-range network. Among the structural descriptors examined, the clearest correlation with the annealing-induced reduction in mechanical loss is the decrease in edge- and face-sharing polyhedra. These results connect composition, annealing, atomic structure, and mechanical dissipation in TiO$_2$-doped GeO$_2$, providing microscopic guidance for optimizing low-noise mirror coatings.

Abstract: The recent discovery of altermagnetism has sparked growing interest in compensated magnetic systems as promising platforms for highly scalable spintronics. To date, experimental verification of altermagnetic order has been achieved predominantly through bulk-sensitive techniques, including spin-dependent electronic spectra and transport responses. However, direct atomic-scale evidence that explicitly correlates crystal symmetry, local structural distortions, and magnetic ordering has remained unexplored. ### [87] [Relaxation-driven topological domains in moiré materials](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27548)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Spatial control of topology is highly desirable for realizing tunable quantum functionalities in materials. Moiré superlattices formed by twisting van der Waals heterostructures provide a natural platform for spatially modulated electronic phases, yet the emergence of tunable topological domains in these systems remains largely unexplored. Here we show that structural relaxation in twisted bilayer BiSb drives the formation of a distinct moiré topological phase, characterized by coexisting topologically nontrivial (Z$_2$ = 1) and trivial (Z$_2$ = 0) domains within a single moiré unit cell. Together, these results establish twisted BiSb as a promising platform for programmable topological domain patterning, where intrinsic networks of edge channels can be continuously tuned and electrically reconfigured in moiré materials.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Conclusion: 实验结果确立了RuO2作为高效自旋源（spin source）的地位，并展示了交变磁体在无场自旋电子器件（field-free spintronic devices）中的应用潜力。

Abstract: Altermagnets are a recently identified class of collinear antiferromagnets that host large spin-split electronic bands, offering a promising platform for efficient spin-current generation. Among proposed candidates, the metallic oxide RuO2 is predicted to exhibit strong altermagnetic spin splitting; however, whether it sustains robust magnetic order beyond the ultrathin thickness limit remains unresolved. Here, we employ optical probes to investigate charge-to-spin conversion in a 12-nm-thick (101)-oriented RuO2 film grown on sapphire. Polarization-resolved second-harmonic generation reveals nonlinear optical responses consistent with the surface symmetry and Néel order of RuO2. Under an applied current, both second-harmonic generation and polar magneto-optical Kerr effect measurements detect a pronounced, directionally anisotropic spin polarization, exhibiting enhanced signals for current along [010] and strongly suppressed responses for current along [-101], in agreement with the symmetry of the altermagnetic spin-splitter effect. Non-magnetic or Rashba-type mechanisms cannot explain this symmetry-selective response. Scanning transmission electron microscopy further reveals that substantial strain persists even in relatively thick films, providing a possible explanation for the observed behavior. Therefore, these results establish RuO2 as an efficient spin source and demonstrate the potential of altermagnets for field-free spintronic devices.

### [89] [Machine-learning-accelerated discovery of synthesizable high-temperature altermagnets with giant spin splitting](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27888)
*Yi-Fei Jiang,Jia-Xuan Guo,Zhen Zhang,Xin-Wei Yi,Jing-Yang You*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 开发了机器学习加速的高通量框架，对 8640 种四方相 AB₂C₂D 化合物进行筛选，利用第一性原理自旋分裂数据训练可解释的 XGBoost 模型，结合对称性分析与热力学稳定性评估，最终对代表性材料进行第一性原理计算验证。

Result: 筛选出 1347 个满足交变磁对称性的反铁磁候选物；XGBoost 模型识别出 34 个低能候选材料（含 4 个已知材料），其非相对论自旋分裂超过 1.5 eV；RbMn₂Te₂O 最大自旋分裂约 1.88 eV，Néel 温度约 390 K，且动态稳定；发现 SrMn₂Te₂O 中软模驱动的结构相变与层间维度交叉，但交变磁自旋分裂在晶格重构后保持稳健；静水压可非单调调控自旋分裂费米面。

Conclusion: 四方相 AB₂C₂D 化合物是一类可调的无杂散场自旋电子学材料平台，本工作提供了一种通用的数据驱动策略，用于发现具有巨自旋分裂的稳健交变磁体。

Abstract: Altermagnets offer a route to spin-polarized electronic states without macroscopic magnetization, because compensated magnetic order can generate momentum-dependent spin splitting through crystal-symmetry-controlled exchange fields. However, experimentally viable altermagnets combining large spin splitting, thermodynamic stability and high magnetic ordering temperatures remain scarce. Here, we develop a machine-learning-accelerated high-throughput framework to explore the tetragonal AB$_2$C$_2$D compounds. Screening 8640 variants identifies 1347 compensated antiferromagnetic candidates satisfying altermagnetic symmetry. An interpretable XGBoost model trained on first-principles spin-splitting data then isolates 34 low-hull-energy candidates,including four previously reported, with giant non-relativistic spin splittings exceeding 1.5 eV near the Fermi level. Detailed first-principles calculations of the representative RbMn$_2$Te$_2$O confirm a maximum spin splitting of $\sim$1.88 eV with dynamical stability and an estimated Néel temperature of $\sim$390 K. The giant splitting originates from symmetry-locked Mn-sublattice exchange fields amplified by directional Mn-d/Te-p hybridization. Furthermore, we uncover a profound soft-mode-driven structural transition associated with an interlayer dimensionality crossover in SrMn$_2$Te$_2$O, yet the unfolded electronic structure demonstrates that the altermagnetic spin splitting remains robust after lattice reconstruction. Hydrostatic pressure provides an additional tuning route, producing non-monotonic modulation of the spin-split Fermi surface governed by local coordination and orbital hybridization. These results establish tetragonal AB$_2$C$_2$D compounds as a tunable materials platform for stray-field-free spintronic devices and provide a general data-driven strategy for discovering robust giant-splitting altermagnets.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 氢-空位相互作用在体心立方（body-centered cubic, BCC）金属中主导着氢的输运和氢脆行为，然而不同BCC金属中氢捕获、脱陷及扩散的微观机制尚不完全清楚。

Method: 采用多尺度方法，结合密度泛函理论（density functional theory, DFT）与动力学蒙特卡洛（kinetic Monte Carlo, kMC）模拟，并利用微动弹性带方法（climbing-image nudged elastic band method）计算迁移和脱陷能垒，同时结合Bader电荷分析评估捕获强度。

Result: DFT计算表明Cr中氢的捕获强于Fe；脱陷能通常随氢占据数增加而降低，但Fe中第六个氢原子仍表现出有限能垒，与以往部分报道不同。kMC模拟显示空位缺陷显著降低氢的迁移率并增加有效激活能，且在Cr中效应更为显著。

Abstract: Hydrogen-vacancy interactions play an important role in governing hydrogen transport and embrittlement in body-centered cubic (BCC) metals. In this study, a multiscale approach combining density functional theory (DFT) and kinetic Monte Carlo (kMC) simulations is employed to investigate hydrogen behavior in BCC Fe and Cr. The DFT-calculated binding energies and Bader charge analysis indicate stronger hydrogen trapping in Cr than in Fe. Migration and detrapping energy barriers are determined using the climbing-image nudged elastic band method, showing that the detrapping energy generally decreases with increasing hydrogen occupancy. However, the sixth hydrogen atom in Fe exhibits a finite barrier, contrary to some previous reports. kMC simulations are then used to evaluate hydrogen diffusion over extended time and length scales. The results demonstrate that vacancy defects significantly reduce hydrogen mobility and increase the effective activation energy, with a more pronounced effect observed in Cr due to stronger trapping. The combined DFT-kMC framework provides detailed insight into the mechanisms of hydrogen trapping, detrapping, and diffusion in BCC metals, offering important implications for understanding hydrogen embrittlement in structural materials.

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 聚合物与生物基材料中的水分扩散常呈现非菲克（non-Fickian）行为，经典扩散模型无法描述。Langmuir模型虽能刻画此类现象，但其解析解仅适用于平板几何（planar geometries），圆柱形系统通常依赖数值方法，缺乏简洁的解析框架。

Method: 在圆柱坐标（cylindrical coordinates）下对Langmuir扩散模型进行解析求解，得到圆柱体内水分含量的局部演变与全局吸湿动力学（global moisture uptake kinetics）的解析表达式，并通过有限差分法（finite difference scheme）进行数值验证。

Result: 解析解与独立数值解在全球吸湿动力学和径向水分分布（radial moisture profiles）上均表现出高度一致性，验证了该解析公式的准确性。

Conclusion: 所提出的解析框架为研究圆柱形系统（如天然纤维）中的非菲克水分扩散提供了一种简单高效的分析工具，并有助于从实验数据中提取模型参数（model parameters）。

Abstract: Moisture diffusion in polymers and bio-based materials frequently exhibits non-Fickian behavior that cannot be described by classical diffusion models. The Langmuir model, which accounts for the coexistence of mobile and bound water molecules, has been widely used to represent such phenomena. However, analytical solutions of this model are generally limited to planar geometries, while cylindrical systems are typically investigated using numerical methods. In this work, the Langmuir diffusion model is solved analytically in cylindrical coordinates. The resulting solution provides both the local evolution of moisture content within the cylinder and the corresponding global moisture uptake kinetics. The analytical solution is validated through comparison with an independent numerical solution based on a finite difference scheme, showing excellent agreement for both the global absorption kinetics and the radial moisture profiles. The proposed formulation therefore provides a simple and efficient analytical framework for studying non-Fickian moisture diffusion in cylindrical systems such as natural fibers, and facilitates the identification of model parameters from experimental data.

### [92] [Search for high-pressure phases of yttrium via a data assimilation approach](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28171)

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 钇（Y）在高压下出现的畸变面心立方（distorted face-centered-cubic, dfcc）相的具体晶体结构尚存争议，已有研究提出了包括$R\overline{3}m$在内的多种候选结构，但缺乏系统性的验证与确认。

Method: 采用基于数据同化（data assimilation）的结构搜索方法，结合高分辨率粉末X射线衍射（XRD）数据与机器学习原子间势（machine-learning interatomic potentials），对包含至多128个原子的超胞进行探索；通过声子计算评估动力学稳定性，并利用PBE与r$^{2}$SCAN泛函进行焓计算，辅以Rietveld精修对粉末XRD数据进行拟合。

Result: 识别出三种低焓相：此前报道的$I4_1/a$结构以及两种新结构$Ibam$和$R\overline{3}$；先前提出的$R\overline{3}m$相未能在数据同化结构搜索中得到重现。声子计算表明$I4_1/a$、$Ibam$和$R\overline{3}$具有动力学稳定性，而$R\overline{3}m$在$Γ$点附近存在虚频模式，显示动力学不稳定。四种候选结构的焓值差异在约10 meV/atom以内，其中$R\overline{3}m$焓值始终最高，r$^{2}$SCAN计算在整个dfcc压力范围内均支持$I4_1/a$。60 GPa下的Rietveld精修进一步将可行结构模型缩小至$I4_1/a$和$Ibam$。

Conclusion: 综合能量排序、动力学稳定性与XRD拟合结果，$I4_1/a$被确定为钇dfcc相最可能的结构，$Ibam$则为紧密竞争的候选结构，尤其在该相区的高压侧具有竞争力。

Abstract: We investigate the distorted face-centered-cubic (dfcc) phase of yttrium (Y) using a data-assimilation-based structure search that combines high-resolution powder x-ray diffraction (XRD) data with machine-learning interatomic potentials. By exploring supercells containing up to 128 atoms, we identify three low-enthalpy phases: the previously reported $I4_1/a$ structure and two additional structures, $Ibam$ and $R\overline{3}$. No data-assimilation-derived structure relaxes to the previously proposed $R\overline{3}m$ phase. Phonon calculations show that $I4_1/a$, $Ibam$, and $R\overline{3}$ are dynamically stable, whereas $R\overline{3}m$ exhibits imaginary modes near the $Γ$ point, indicating dynamical instability. Enthalpy calculations using both PBE and r$^{2}$SCAN place the four candidate structures within about 10 meV/atom, indicating a complex energy landscape with multiple competing minima, although $R\overline{3}m$ is consistently highest in enthalpy and r$^{2}$SCAN favors $I4_1/a$ throughout the dfcc pressure range. Rietveld refinements of the powder XRD profile at 60 GPa further narrow the viable structural models to $I4_1/a$ and $Ibam$, both of which reproduce the experimental data better than $R\overline{3}m$ and $R\overline{3}$. Taken together with the energetic ordering and dynamical stability, these results identify $I4_1/a$ as the most plausible structure of the dfcc phase of Y, with $Ibam$ remaining a close competing candidate, particularly toward the high-pressure side of the dfcc region.

At excitation fluences above 3 mJ/cm^2, nonlinear frequency mixing occurs, including sum- and difference-frequency generation, indicative of strain-induced nonlinear elasticity. These findings provide insight into the mechanical limits of semiconductor nanostructures under intense optical excitation and suggest new pathways for material characterization and optomechanical control at the nanoscale. ### [94] [High Temperature Jahn-Teller Distortion and Short Range Order in CsCuCl$_3$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28288)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用三种互补的原位实验方法：（1）粉末中子衍射的原位对分布函数（pair distribution function, PDF）；（2）原位粉末X射线衍射（powder X-ray diffraction）；（3）原位单晶X射线衍射（single crystal X-ray diffraction）。

Abstract: CsCuCl$_3$, chiral and Jahn-Teller distorted at room temperature, takes a more symmetric structure above 423K. Describing this 'simpler' high temperature structure is far from simple and has been the subject of many, sometimes contradicting, studies. Here we reinvestigate the high temperature structure of CsCuCl$_3$, its thermal stability, and its effect on room temperature chirality. In situ pair distribution function data from powder neutron diffraction confirms that CsCuCl$_3$ is Jahn-Teller distorted both below and above T$_c$, and provides a quantitative view of short range order in the high temperature structure. In situ powder x-ray diffraction shows that CsCuCl$_3$ does not undergo any additional structural changes above 423K and is congruently melting. In situ single crystal x-ray diffraction experiments reveal that the phase transition induces domains of mixed handedness in originally homochiral crystals.   <summary>Details</summary>

Method: PCM的开关过程由热驱动，因此提升能效主要通过两种策略：将活性相变材料区域缩小至亚10纳米（sub-10 nm）尺度；以及增强PCM器件内部的热约束（heat confinement），以减少向周围环境的热耗散。

Result: PCM技术已实现每比特仅数十飞焦耳（femtojoules per bit）的能耗。理论极限可达到每立方纳米存储材料单阿焦耳（single attojoules per cubic nanometer），但实际应用中受到电学和热学寄生效应（electrical and thermal parasitics）的显著制约，尤其在接触点和界面处。

Conclusion: 尽管通过缩小活性区域和优化热约束已显著提升了PCM的能效，但接触和界面的电热寄生效应是目前实现理论极限的主要障碍。

Abstract: Phase change memory (PCM) relies on a reversible transition between amorphous and crystalline states of a material, and stands as a promising candidate for next-generation, energy-efficient data storage and neuromorphic hardware. Here, we review key innovations that have driven PCM technology to achieve energy consumption down to only tens of femtojoules per bit, and could further advance it closer to its fundamental limits. Because PCM switching is induced thermally, we highlight improvements in energy-efficiency through two primary strategies: by minimizing the active phase change material region to sub-10 nm dimensions, and by enhancing heat confinement within PCM devices to reduce thermal dissipation into the surrounding environment. While the theoretical limits could reach single attojoules per cubic nanometer of memory material, realizing these limits in practice is significantly constrained by electrical and thermal parasitics, particularly at contacts and interfaces.

Method: 采用经典$J_1$-$J_2$-$J_3$海森堡模型（Heisenberg model）进行理论分析，并结合密度泛函理论（density functional theory, DFT）计算。

*Kushal Ramakrishna,Mani Lokamani,Attila Cangi*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文系统评估了MACE势函数（MACE potentials）在铁镍合金（Fe-Ni alloys）中的表现，基于特殊准随机结构（special quasirandom structures, SQS）数据集训练了专用模型MACE-sqs，其在能量和力的验证误差分别为2.0 meV/原子和24.3 meV/埃。与MACE基础模型（foundation models）相比，MACE-sqs在状态方程、弹性常数和热膨胀等性质上与密度泛函理论（DFT）和实验最为一致，但在bcc-to-hcp相变中无法正确预测镍含量对转变压力的影响，暴露出高压磁坍缩（magnetic collapse）和磁弹效应（magnetoelastic effects）建模的不足。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 铁镍合金的相稳定性（phase stability）依赖于结构、弹性、磁性和有限温度性质的准确描述，而现有的机器学习原子间势（machine learning interatomic potentials）在该体系中的系统评估尚不充分。本文旨在通过对MACE势函数的基准测试（benchmark），评估SQS训练数据的有效性，并识别当前模型在磁坍缩相关相变预测中的局限性。

Method: 基准参考数据集基于自旋极化（spin-polarized）PBE密度泛函理论（DFT）计算，涵盖化学无序特殊准随机结构（SQS），覆盖不同成分、bcc与fcc晶体结构以及体积与剪切变形。训练了一个体系专用模型MACE-sqs，并与多个MACE基础模型（含Hubbard U校正模型）进行比较。

Result: MACE-sqs在能量和力上分别达到2.0 meV/原子和24.3 meV/埃的验证误差。在bcc和fcc Fe-Ni合金的状态方程、平衡体积、弹性常数和热膨胀趋势上，MACE-sqs与DFT和实验的吻合度优于所有测试的基础模型。在bcc-to-hcp纯铁转变压力预测上，MACE-sqs更接近实验值，但所有模型均错误地预测转变压力随镍含量增加而升高。

Conclusion: 针对性SQS基训练显著提升了MACE势函数在Fe-Ni合金中的精度，但高压磁坍缩和成分依赖的磁弹效应尚未被充分捕获，导致相稳定性预测在磁性转变条件下仍存在关键局限，这为未来模型开发指明了方向。

Abstract: We present a systematic benchmark of MACE potentials for iron-nickel alloys, focusing on structural, elastic, magnetic, and finite-temperature properties relevant to phase stability. The reference dataset comprises spin-polarized PBE density functional theory (DFT) calculations for chemically disordered special quasirandom structures (SQS), spanning compositions, bcc and fcc crystal structures, and volumetric and shear deformations. A system-specific MACE-sqs model trained on this dataset achieves validation errors of 2.0 meV/atom for energies and 24.3 meV/Angstrom for forces. Compared with several MACE foundation models, including models trained with Hubbard U corrections, MACE-sqs gives the most consistent agreement with DFT and experiment for equations of state, equilibrium volumes, elastic constants, and thermal expansion trends in bcc and fcc Fe-Ni alloys. For the bcc-to-hcp transition, MACE-sqs predicts a pure-Fe transition pressure closer to experiment than the tested foundation models, but all models predict an incorrect increase of transition pressure with Ni content. This failure indicates that high-pressure magnetic collapse and composition-dependent magnetoelastic effects are not yet fully captured. Overall, targeted SQS-based training substantially improves the accuracy of MACE potentials for Fe-Ni alloys, while phase stability under magnetic collapse remains a key limitation for future model development.

</details>


### [100] [Electron-beam induced methane decomposition for in-situ carbon doping of hexagonal boron nitride](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28564)
*Barbara Maria Mayer,Manuel Längle,Umair Javed,Toma Susi,E. Harriet Åhlgren,Jani Kotakoski*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本研究展示了一种利用电子束辐照和低压甲烷气氛实现六方氮化硼（hBN）碳掺杂的方法，通过同时产生空位并分解甲烷，实现了纳米级精度的碳原子空间可控掺杂。实验发现碳富集区主要集中于辐照区域，并形成尺寸不超过约1纳米的六方排列碳团簇，影响了局部电子环境及光学性质。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 控制碳原子在六方氮化硼（hexagonal boron nitride, hBN）中的空间掺入对于工程化具有光学活性的缺陷至关重要，但现有方法缺乏纳米级精度和碳源供给的可控性。

Method: 在低压甲烷（methane）气氛中利用电子束辐照（electron-beam irradiation）对hBN进行碳掺杂，电子束同时产生空位并将甲烷分解为单个碳原子和氢原子。采用环形暗场扫描透射电子显微镜（annular dark-field scanning transmission electron microscopy）观察形貌变化，并利用时间分辨电子能量损失谱（time-resolved electron energy-loss spectroscopy, EELS）映射碳掺入过程及局部电子环境。

Result: 增加甲烷分压可抑制孔洞生长，并通过氢对氮的选择性刻蚀形成三角形硼终止孔洞。碳富集区中84±7%局限于电子束辐照区域，部分碳原子扩散至辐照区外平均4.7±0.5纳米的距离。掺入的碳原子在晶格内形成尺寸不超过约1纳米的六方排列碳团簇。EELS精细结构分析表明这些区域局部电子环境发生改变。

Conclusion: 该方法实现了对hBN中碳掺杂的纳米级空间控制，碳原子以六方排列形成小尺寸团簇并改变局部电子环境，有望影响相应碳相关缺陷的光学性质。

Abstract: Controlling the spatial incorporation of carbon into hexagonal boron nitride (hBN) is essential for engineering optically active defects, yet existing approaches lack nanoscale precision and control over the carbon supply. Here, we demonstrate a method for carbon doping of hBN using electron-beam irradiation in a low-pressure methane atmosphere, where the beam simultaneously generates vacancies and decomposes methane into individual carbon and hydrogen atoms. Using annular dark-field scanning transmission electron microscopy, we show that increasing the methane partial pressure suppresses pore growth and drives the formation of triangular boron-terminated pores through preferential hydrogen etching of nitrogen. Time-resolved electron energy-loss spectroscopy (EELS) mapping reveals progressive carbon incorporation into the lattice, accompanied by boron and nitrogen depletion. Carbon clustering occurs predominantly within the irradiated area: 84+-7% of carbon-rich regions are confined to the area exposed to the electron beam, while some carbon atoms are also found to diffuse up to an average distance of 4.7+-0.5 nm beyond it. The incorporated carbon atoms arrange in a hexagonal pattern within the lattice, forming patches that do not exceed ~1 nm in size. Analysis of the EELS fine structure indicates modifications to the local electronic environment within these regions, with implications for the optical properties of the resulting carbon-related defects.

</details>


### [101] [Ultrafast dynamics of excitons in black phosphorus](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28611)
*Geoffroy Kremer,Juan F. P. Mosquera,Joël Morf,Aymen Mahmoudi,Frédéric Chassot,Viktor Christiansson,Maxime Rumo,Manuele Balestra,Fabian O. von Rohr,Philipp Werner,Michael Schüler,Claude Monney*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本研究通过时间分辨光电子能谱实验与量子动力学理论框架，揭示了黑磷中激子（exciton）在皮秒时间尺度上经由声子散射退相干为暗激子（dark exciton）的机制，并量化了早期非平衡动力学中的关键参数。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 识别激子在早期非平衡动力学中的退相干机制（decoherence mechanism），对于实现光诱导半导体能带工程（light-induced band-structure engineering）至关重要。

Method: 在直接带隙半导体黑磷（black phosphorus）中利用共振中红外光激发产生激子，通过时间分辨角分辨光电子能谱（time- and angle-resolved photoemission spectroscopy）追踪其超快动力学，并建立量子动力学理论框架（quantum-kinetic theoretical framework）模拟激子通过声子散射（phonon scattering）退相干为暗激子的过程。

Result: 结合模拟与实验，量化了描述激子早期动力学的关键参数。研究发现，声子介导的谷内散射（phonon-mediated intravalley scattering）是单谷半导体中相干激子现象（coherent exciton phenomena）的基本限制因素。

Conclusion: 声子介导的谷内散射是限制单谷半导体中相干激子现象的根本机制，该发现为理解和调控半导体中激子的相干性提供了定量依据。

Abstract: Excitons are key quasiparticles determining the optical properties of solids. As such, they can be utilized to coherently control the electronic structure of materials using optical femtosecond pulses. Identifying the decoherence mechanism during the early non-equilibrium dynamics is crucial to achieve light-induced band-structure engineering in semiconductors. Here, we generate excitons in the direct band gap semiconductor black phosphorus with a resonant mid-infrared photoexcitation. Using time- and angle-resolved photoemission spectroscopy, we track their complex ultrafast dynamics on the few-picosecond time scale. We develop a quantum-kinetic theoretical framework to model the decoherence of excitons into dark excitons via phonon scattering. By combining simulation and experiment, we quantify key parameters describing the early dynamics of the excitons. Our work highlights phonon-mediated intravalley scattering as a fundamental limitation for coherent exciton phenomena in single-valley semiconductors.

### [102] [Universal Stability of Ga Split Vacancies across α-, β-, and κ-Ga2O3 Polymorphs: A Machine-Learning Accelerated Study](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28743)
*Mohamed Abdelilah Fadla,Myrta Grüning,Lorenzo Stella*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文利用机器学习原子间势（MLIPs）加速寻找非局域缺陷重构，并结合HSE06杂化密度泛函理论（hybrid DFT）准确量化了β、α和κ三种Ga₂O₃多晶型物中分裂空位（split vacancy）与替代施主缺陷的性质。研究发现分裂空位是所有多晶型物的基态空位，其稳定性显著优于简单空位，且施主缺陷效率受分裂空位补偿限制；贫氧生长是抑制此类缺陷、实现高n型电导率的普适条件。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 分裂Ga空位是β-Ga₂O₃中主要的本征受主缺陷，但其在α和κ相中的作用长期被忽视或被假设为不利。为优化基于Ga₂O₃器件的电导率和光学性质，亟需深入理解这些缺陷的行为。

Method: 采用机器学习原子间势（MLIPs）加速非局域缺陷重构的搜索，随后使用HSE06杂化密度泛函理论（hybrid DFT）精确量化单空位（V_Ga）、分裂空位（V_Ga^i）及替代施主（Hf_Ga和Si_Ga）在氧化学势广泛实验相关范围内的缺陷性质。

Result: 分裂空位是β、α和κ三种多晶型物的基态空位，比简单空位分别稳定约0.75 eV（β）、0.41 eV（α）和0.14 eV（κ）。MLIPs正确识别了特定分裂空位基态，且缺陷构型的能量排序与HSE06结果高度一致。Hf和Si形成能低、为浅施主（shallow donor），尤其在贫氧条件下，但其效率受分裂空位补偿限制。

Conclusion: 贫氧生长条件是抑制分裂空位补偿、实现Ga₂O₃各多晶型物高n型电导率的普适要求。

Abstract: Split Ga vacancies are the dominant native acceptor in $β$-$Ga_2O_3$; however, their role in $α$ and $κ$ phases has been largely overlooked or assumed to be unfavorable. A detailed understanding of these defects is critical for tailoring the electrical conductivity and optical properties and optimising $Ga_2O_3$-based devices. In this work, we used machine learning interatomic potentials (MLIPs) to accelerate the discovery of non-local defect reconstructions, followed by HSE06 hybrid DFT to accurately quantify defect properties of single vacancy $V_{\text{Ga}}$, split vacancy $V_{\text{Ga}}^{\text{i}}$ and substitutional donors ($\mathrm{Hf_{Ga}}$ and $\mathrm{Si_{Ga}}$) across a wide range of experimentally relevant conditions for the oxygen chemical potential. We find that split vacancies are the ground-state vacancy for all studied polymorphs ($β$, $α$, and $κ$). Split vacancies are more stable than simple vacancies by ~0.75 eV ($β$), ~0.41 eV ($α$), and ~0.14 eV ($κ$). Notably, MLIPs correctly identified the specific split-vacancy ground states and yielded an energetic ordering of symmetry-inequivalent defect configurations in excellent agreement with HSE06 results. While Hf and Si show low formation energy and act as shallow donors, especially under oxygen-poor conditions, their efficiency is limited by split-vacancy compensation. The growth under oxygen-poor conditions is a universal requirement to suppress these defects and achieve high n-type conductivity across the $Ga_2O_3$ polymorph.

</details>


### [103] [Synthesis and properties of bulk Mg$_3$WN$_4$ in a wurtzite-derived structure](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28799)
*Anna A. Berseneva,Christopher L. Rom,Layton Rudolph,Yunseung Kuk,P. Shiv Halasyamani,Rebecca W. Smaha,James R. Neilson,Andriy Zakutayev*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文首次报道了通过固态复分解反应（solid state metathesis reaction）体相合成纤锌矿衍生结构（wurtzite-derived crystal structure）的Mg₃WN₄。结合原位与非原位表征手段，揭示反应路径、竞争相及缺陷行为，并证明通过控制热预算可实现相纯三元氮化物（ternary nitrides）的选择性合成。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 实验合成具有受控元素配位环境（elemental coordination environments）的理论预测材料，有望实现如易离子输运或铁电开关等有用性质。在Mg-W-N组成空间中，已有多种新稳定和亚稳态三元氮化物被预测并合成，但Mg₃WN₄的体相合成此前尚未实现。

Method: 采用固态复分解反应（solid state metathesis reaction）从Li₆WN₄ + 3 MgCl₂前驱体合成Mg₃WN₄ + 6 LiCl产物。利用原位同步辐射粉末X射线衍射（in situ synchrotron powder X-ray diffraction）监测反应进程，结合非原位粉末合成（ex situ powder synthesis）、二次谐波产生（second harmonic generation, SHG）测量、光学吸收光谱、化学组成分析及电子显微镜成像进行表征。

Result: 反应在~380 °C缓慢开始，至600 °C完成，中间在440 °C以上出现竞争性的无序岩盐衍生相（disordered rocksalt-derived phase）(Mg,W)N。非原位合成于400 °C、0.5小时、10%过量MgCl₂条件下获得阳离子有序（cation-ordered）的纤锌矿衍生结构，SHG测量证实其极性对称性。光学吸收光谱、元素分析及电镜成像表明体相纤锌矿Mg₃WN₄易于形成缺陷。

Conclusion: 通过精心控制反应热预算（thermal budget），并借助原位测量指导，可以实现相纯三元氮化物的选择性非原位合成。该工作为纤锌矿Mg₃WN₄的性质表征铺平了道路。

Abstract: Experimental synthesis of theoretically predicted materials with controlled elemental coordination environments can lead to realization of useful properties, such as facile ion transport or ferroelectric switching. Among such materials are new ternary nitrides in the Mg-W-N composition space, where several new stable and metastable compounds have been predicted and synthesized recently in bulk and film forms. Here, we report for the first time on the bulk synthesis of Mg$_3$WN$_4$ in a wurtzite-derived crystal structure via a solid state metathesis reaction. $In$ $situ$ synchrotron powder X-ray diffraction shows how the ion exchange proceeds from Li$_6$WN$_4$ + 3 MgCl$_2$ precursors to Mg$_3$WN$_4$ + 6 LiCl products, with the reaction starting slowly near 380 $^\circ$C and completing by 600 $^\circ$C, including the presence of a competing disordered rocksalt-derived phase (Mg,W)N above 440 $^\circ$C. The follow up $ex$ $situ$ powder synthesis at 400 $^\circ$C for 0.5 hour with 10% excess MgCl$_2$ reveals the cation-ordered nature of the wurtzite-derived Mg$_3$WN$_4$ structure with polar symmetry confirmed by second harmonic generation measurements. Optical absorption spectra, chemical composition analysis, and electron microscopy imaging suggests that bulk wurtzite Mg$_3$WN$_4$ is prone to defect formation. Overall, this study shows that selective $ex$ $situ$ synthesis of the phase pure ternary nitrides, informed by \textit{in situ} measurements, is possible by carefully controlling the thermal budget of the reaction, and paves a way towards property characterization of wurtzite Mg$_3$WN$_4$.

</details>


### [104] [A GPU-based Solver for Polarization Dynamics in Ferroelectric Materials](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28800)
*Ali Hasan,Edoardo Piccolo,Anna Giordano,Natalya Fedorova,Jorge Íñiguez-González,Davi Rodrigues,Giovanni Finocchio*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文提出了一个名为PETASPIN_microelectrics的完全基于GPU加速的可扩展数值求解器，用于基于Ginzburg-Landau形式体系计算铁电系统的完整极化矢量场，解决了现有CPU求解器在静电处理简化和降维表示方面的局限。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 铁电材料（ferroelectric materials）在非易失性、小尺寸、低功耗驱动和电可调谐等多重器件概念中具有重要应用前景，这要求高效且精确的模拟工具来描述极化纹理（polarization texture）。然而，现有的铁电求解器大多基于CPU，依赖于简化的静电处理和极化场的降维表示，难以捕捉有限尺寸效应和边界效应，限制了可模拟的畴结构（domain structure）和畴壁（domain wall）范围。

Method: 开发了名为PETASPIN_microelectrics的完全GPU加速可扩展数值求解器，基于Ginzburg-Landau形式体系（Ginzburg-Landau formalism）计算完整极化矢量场。求解器集成了经过优化和验证的全静电场计算，并支持多个模拟的并行执行。

Result: 通过多个基准问题进行系统验证，包括BaTiO3中的相变和铁电畴壁轮廓。模拟再现了BaTiO3中由温度驱动的滞回相变（hysteretic phase transition）和滞回线（hysteresis loop），并展示了PbTiO3/SrTiO3双层系统中三维混合斯格明子（skyrmion）的稳定化。结果与解析理论预测及先前实验研究定量一致。

Conclusion: 该求解器为铁电材料的大规模模拟（包括拓扑纹理（topological texture）的稳定化）提供了高效、准确的平台，支持下一代铁电器件设计的预测性建模。

Abstract: Ferroelectric materials can be used for the development of multiple device concepts combining non-volatility, small dimensions, low-power actuation, and electrical tunability. Such development demands efficient and precise design of simulation tools describing the polarization texture. However, most existing ferroelectric solvers are CPU-based and rely on simplified electrostatic treatments and reduced-dimensional representations of the polarization field. These approximations limit their ability to capture finite-size and boundary effects and restrict the range of domain structures and domain walls that can be realistically simulated. Here, we present a fully GPU (graphics processing units)-accelerated and scalable numerical solver, named PETASPIN_microelectrics, for computing the full polarization vector field of ferroelectric systems using the Ginzburg-Landau formalism. Our solver incorporates an optimized and validated calculation of the full electrostatic field and enables the parallel execution of multiple simulations. We systematically validated the solver with several benchmark problems, including phase transitions in BaTiO3 and ferroelectric domain wall profiles. Our simulations reproduce temperature-driven hysteretic phase transitions in BaTiO3. We also reproduce hysteresis loops and demonstrate stabilization of a three-dimensional hybrid skyrmion in a PbTiO3/SrTiO3 bilayer system. Our results show quantitative agreement with predictions from an analytical theory and prior experimental studies. The proposed solver provides an efficient, accurate platform for large-scale simulations of ferroelectric materials including stabilization of topological textures supporting predictive modeling for next-generation of ferroelectric device design.

</details>

### [105] [Hybrid neural denoising for resource-efficient near- and sub-threshold radio triggering of extensive air showers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28332)
*Alperen Aksoy,Ilja Bekman,Markus Cristinziani,Eric-Teunis de Boone,Vesselin Dimitrov,Qader Dorosti,Chimezie Eguzo,Stefan Heidbrink,Stefan van Waasen,Andre Zambanini*

Main category: astro-ph.IM

TL;DR: 本文提出一种混合神经触发（hybrid neural trigger）方法，将波形恢复与信号分类联合建模为部署约束下的单一问题，通过紧凑型卷积去噪器（convolutional denoiser）与分类器链在FPGA上实现微秒级低资源推理，在10^-4虚警率下对弱信号保留约41%的触发效率，而传统峰包络触发（peak-envelope trigger）完全失效。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 广延大气簇射（extensive air showers）的自发无线电触发需要在强射频干扰（radio-frequency interference）背景下保持对弱脉冲的灵敏度，同时兼容边缘硬件（edge hardware）资源限制。现有方法难以兼顾抗干扰能力、弱信号触发效率与硬件部署可行性。

Method: 将波形恢复与信号分类视为统一的部署约束问题，采用紧凑型卷积去噪器对单通道含噪迹线进行脉冲估计，再交由紧凑型分类器评估。模型选择与部署通过超参数优化（hyperparameter optimisation）、量化感知训练（quantisation-aware training）、定点量化（fixed-point quantisation）、hls4ml固件导出、高层次综合（high-level synthesis）及寄存器传输级验证（register-transfer-level validation）全流程耦合实现。

Result: 去噪器本身即可将简单峰包络判决转化为有效的弱脉冲触发；完整去噪器-分类器链在10^-4虚警率下弱信号基准中保留约41%的测试信号，而经典峰包络触发完全失效。清洗后的波形保留时序与峰值幅度结构，固件在典型FPGA上实现微秒级延迟与紧凑算术资源需求。

Conclusion: 混合神经去噪（hybrid neural denoising）为噪声环境中弱与倾斜大气簇射信号的纯无线电触发提供了一条实用路径。

Abstract: Autonomous radio self-triggering for extensive air showers must reject variable radio-frequency interference while preserving sensitivity to weak pulses and remaining compatible with station-level edge hardware. This work presents a hybrid neural trigger in which waveform recovery and signal classification are treated as a single deployment-constrained problem. A compact convolutional denoiser maps a noisy single-channel trace to a cleaned estimate of the air-shower pulse, which is then evaluated by a compact classifier. The method is tested with measured high-interference background traces and detector-folded air-shower pulses from the Pierre Auger Offline simulation chain, with signals concentrated in the near- and sub-threshold regime. Model selection and deployment are linked through hyperparameter optimisation, quantisation-aware training, fixed-point quantisation, hls4ml firmware export, high-level synthesis, and register-transfer-level validation. The denoiser alone turns a simple peak-envelope decision into an efficient weak-pulse trigger, showing that the cleaned waveform carries trigger-relevant information beyond a final classifier score. In the full denoiser-classifier chain, the hybrid trigger improves signal-background separation and efficiency at fixed false-positive rates: at a false-positive rate of 10^-4, it retains about 41% of held-out signal traces in the weak-signal benchmark, while the classical peak-envelope trigger retains none. The cleaned waveform preserves timing and peak-amplitude structure for station-level diagnostics, feature extraction, and selective readout. The firmware meets timing on representative FPGA targets with microsecond-scale latency and compact arithmetic-resource demand. These results establish hybrid neural denoising as a practical route toward radio-only triggering for weak and inclined air-shower signals in noisy environments.

</details>

### [106] [Influence of the QCD Analogue of the Inverse Compton Effect on the Transverse Momentum and Pseudorapidity Distributions of Secondary Particles in pp Collisions at sqrt (s)= 30 GeV, 510 GeV, and 14 TeV](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27468)
*M. Alizada,M. Suleymanov*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文通过PYTHIA 8.316数值模拟，研究QCD逆康普顿效应（ICE）对质子-质子碰撞中次级粒子横动量（p_T）和赝快度（eta）分布的影响，发现随着碰撞能量从√s=30 GeV升至14 TeV，ICE贡献逐渐增强，在高能下与小x区域胶子碰撞的增强有关。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探讨QCD框架下的逆康普顿效应（ICE）在夸克-胶子散射过程（qg→qg）中对次级粒子分布的影响，尤其是在不同碰撞能量下ICE与互补的DCE（直接康普顿效应） regime之间的相对贡献变化。

Method: 采用PYTHIA 8.316事件生成器进行数值模拟，在√s=30 GeV、510 GeV和14 TeV三个能量点上分析质子-质子碰撞中qg→qg散射过程产生的次级粒子的横动量（p_T）和赝快度（pseudorapidity, eta）分布。

Result: ICE与DCE的相对贡献强烈依赖于碰撞能量：能量从√s=30 GeV升至14 TeV时，ICE在宽p_T范围内贡献达到或超过DCE；ICE/DCE比值偏离1主要出现在中心赝快度区域（|η|≈0），对应于对称部分子组态（x₁∼x₂），而在边缘区域比值趋近于1。

Conclusion: 随着碰撞能量的增加，ICE类过程的贡献增长，其原因在于小x区域（small-x region）中胶子碰撞的作用增强。

Abstract: Within the framework of numerical simulations, this work investigates the influence of the QCD analogue of the inverse Compton effect (ICE) in the quark--gluon scattering process qg \rightarrow qg on the transverse momentum p_T and pseudorapidity eta distributions of secondary particles produced in proton--proton collisions at energies sqrt{s}=30 GeV, 510 GeV, 14 TeV. In the present context, ICE refers to a class of parton-level kinematic configurations in which the incoming quark carries a larger fraction of energy than the gluon, in contrast to the complementary DCE regime. The simulations were performed using the PYTHIA~8.316 event generator. It is shown that the relative contributions of ICE and DCE strongly depend on the collision energy. As the energy increases from sqrt{s}=30 GeV to sqrt{s}=14 TeV, the ICE contribution becomes comparable to or exceeds the DCE contribution over a broad p_T range. The analysis of pseudorapidity distributions demonstrates that deviations of the ICE/DCE ratio from unity appear predominantly in the central region |eta| simeq 0, corresponding to symmetric partonic configurations x_1 sim x_2, whereas in peripheral regions the ratio approaches unity. The obtained results indicate that, with increasing collision energy, the contribution of ICE-like processes grows due to the enhanced role of gluon collisions in the small-x region.

</details>


### [107] [Probing Dynamical Inverse Seesaw with Low-frequency Gravitational Waves](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27519)
*Debasish Borah,Sounak Dutta,Partha Kumar Paul,Indrajit Saha,Narendra Sahu*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究了通过脉冲星计时阵（pulsar timing arrays）在低频引力波（gravitational waves, GW）实验中探测动力学反跷跷板机制（dynamical inverse seesaw mechanism）的可能性，该机制用于解释轻中微子质量的起源。研究发现，反跷跷板模型中轻子数破缺项处于亚MeV能标，其动力学起源自然导致低标度一级相变（first-order phase transition），可在低频引力波实验中探测。此外，引力波实验与重中性轻子（heavy neutral lepton）搜索之间存在有趣的互补性：引力波实验对活性-惰性混合（active-sterile mixing）较小的参数空间仍然敏感，而这超出了大多数粒子物理实验的探测范围。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索通过低频随机引力波探测动力学反跷跷板机制的可能性，以解释轻中微子质量的起源，并寻找与现有重中性轻子搜索实验的互补性。

Method: 基于反跷跷板模型中轻子数破缺项处于亚MeV能标这一特征，分析其动力学起源如何导致低标度一级相变；通过脉冲星计时阵在低频引力波区间对上述相变信号进行理论探测可行性分析。

Result: 低频引力波实验能够探测由动力学反跷跷板机制诱发的低标度一级相变信号；引力波实验对活性-惰性混合较小的参数区间保持探测敏感性，而该区间是大多数传统粒子物理实验无法触及的。

Conclusion: 引力波探测与重中性轻子搜索在反跷跷板参数空间上具有互补性，低频引力波实验有望成为探索轻中微子质量起源的新途径。

Abstract: We study the possibility of probing the dynamical inverse seesaw mechanism for the origin of light neutrino masses via the detection of stochastic gravitational waves (GW) in the low-frequency regime currently being probed by pulsar timing arrays. As the lepton number-violating term in inverse seesaw typically remains in the sub-MeV ballpark, its dynamical origin naturally brings the possibility of a low-scale first-order phase transition, which can be probed at low-frequency GW experiments. We also find interesting complementarity with heavy neutral lepton searches, as GW experiments remain sensitive to parameter space with small active-sterile mixing, which is out of reach for most particle physics experiments.

### [108] [From WIMP to FIMP during reheating: collider vs non-collider probes for p-wave annihilation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27521)
*Dipankar Pradhan,Niloy Mondal,Abhik Sarkar,Anupam Ghosh,Shashwat Sharma,Mathew Thomas Arun,Basabendu Barman*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文在微扰重加热（perturbative reheating）框架下，通过六维有效算子的暗物质（dark matter, DM）与可见扇区相互作用，研究了从“冻出”（freeze-out）到“冻结”（freeze-in）DM产生机制的转变。结合直接/间接探测、不可见衰变、对撞机实验和引力波观测的约束，证明当前及未来实验灵敏度可用于探测并限制原初核合成（BBN）之前的宇宙时期及超出标准模型的新物理。特别地，对撞机实验能在强度与能量前沿对通常受天体物理观测弱约束的p波抑制（p-wave suppressed）导数算子施加强限制，从而显著缩小允许的重加热温度、DM质量及有效相互作用尺度参数空间。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索原初核合成时期（pre-BBN epoch）之前的宇宙性质是理解早期宇宙演化与新物理的关键。然而，该时期缺乏直接观测信息，亟需通过暗物质产生机制及多信使实验约束来间接揭示重加热时代的物理规律。

Method: 在微扰重加热框架下，假设暗物质通过六维有效算子与可见扇区相互作用，系统分析了从冻出到冻结的DM产生过渡过程。整合了直接探测、间接探测、不可见衰变、对撞机实验与引力波观测等多类实验约束，对重加热温度、DM质量及有效相互作用尺度进行联合参数空间限制。

Result: 强度前沿与能量前沿的对撞机实验能够对p波抑制的导数算子施加强约束，弥补了天体物理观测在这类相互作用上的弱限制。这些互补性搜索显著缩小了为再现观测DM丰度所需的重加热温度、DM质量及有效相互作用尺度的允许范围。

Conclusion: 当前及未来的多类实验灵敏度可作为强有力的探针，用于揭示原初核合成之前的宇宙时期以及超出标准模型的新物理。对撞机实验在约束特定类型DM相互作用方面具有不可替代的互补优势。

Abstract: By examining the transition from freeze-out to freeze-in dark matter (DM) production within the framework of perturbative reheating, where DM interacts with the visible sector through effective operators of dimension six, we have investigated how a broad range of new physics probes can reveal the nature of the pre-BBN Universe. Incorporating constraints from direct and indirect DM searches, invisible decay measurements, collider experiments, and gravitational wave observations, our analysis demonstrates that both current and forthcoming experimental sensitivities can serve as powerful tools for probing as well as constraining the post-inflationary era, together with new physics beyond the SM. Our analysis demonstrates that collider experiments at both the intensity and energy frontiers can impose strong bounds on derivative operators whose interactions are typically {\it p-wave suppressed}, and therefore only weakly constrained by astrophysical observations. In particular, these complementary searches can significantly restrict the allowed reheating temperature, DM mass and effective interaction scale required to reproduce the observed DM abundance for DM produced during the epoch of reheating.

</details>


### [109] [Hunting New Animalcula with Flavour Changing Processes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27525)
*Andrzej J. Buras*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文回顾了1676年列文虎克发现微生物的350周年纪念，并类比提出味物理（flavour physics）可在远小于对撞机能达到的距离尺度上搜索“新动物”（new animalcula），即新物理（New Physics, NP）。作者主张超越当前流行的全局拟合（global fits）策略，通过不同观测量（observables）之间的特征关联（correlations）来直接检验标准模型及其扩展。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 受列文虎克发现微生物的启发，作者希望将味物理作为探索极小距离尺度上新物理现象的途径。作者认为当前依赖全局拟合的方法不足以直接检验新物理，需要发展基于观测量之间特征关联的新搜索策略。

Method: 作者提出了多种搜索新物理的策略，核心是超越全局拟合方法，利用有效场论（如WET和SMEFT）中的Wilson系数（Wilson coefficients）框架，并强调不同观测量（如大量衰变的分支比（branching ratios））之间的关联——这些关联特征来自标准模型（Standard Model, SM）或特定新物理场景。

Result: 论文指出，精确测量各类观测量并进行精确的理论计算（包括标准模型内和超出标准模型的计算）是必不可少的。作者认为，对标准模型及其扩展的最直接检验来自于不同观测量之间的特征关联。

Conclusion: 味物理有望在远小于当前和本世纪未来对撞机直接可及的距离尺度上发现新物理。有效的搜索策略应关注观测量之间的特征关联，而非仅依赖全局拟合。

Abstract: This year marks the 350th anniversary of the discovery of the first animalcula (little animals) by van Leeuvanhoek in 1676.Flavour physics makes it possible to search for new animalcula at distance scales far shorter than those resolved by van Leeuwenhoek in 1676 and even shorter than those directly accessible at the Large Hadron Collider and the planned colliders in this century. I summarize various strategies for achieving this goal. While precise measurements of a wide variety of observables and their precise theoretical calculations, both within the Standard Model (SM) and beyond it, are indispensable in this context, in my view it is crucial to develop strategies for the search for New Physics (NP) that go beyond the global fits that are very popular today. While effective field theories such as WET and SMEFT are formulated in terms of Wilson coefficients of the relevant operators, with correlations characteristic of the SM and of specific NP scenarios, the most direct tests of the SM and its extensions are, in my opinion, correlations among different observables, like branching ratios of numerous decays, that are characteristic of particular new animalcula at work

</details>


### [110] [Tensor molecule $J/ψJ/ψ$: A candidate to the resonance $X(6200) $](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28015)
*S. S. Agaev,K. Azizi,H. Sundu*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文运用QCD求和规则（QCD sum rule）方法，对强子分子态（hadronic molecule）$\mathcal{M}=J/\psi J/\psi$进行了系统研究。计算得到其质量约为$6290\pm50$ MeV，总衰变宽度约为$149\pm21$ MeV。除主导的$J/\psi J/\psi$衰变道外，还预测了若干子主导衰变模式。通过与实验数据比较，提出该分子态可能是张量共振态$X(6200)$的候选者。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索由两个$J/\psi$介子构成的强子分子态$\mathcal{M}$的物理性质，评估其作为实验上观测到的张量共振态$X(6200)$候选者的可能性。

Method: 采用两点QCD求和规则（two-point QCD sum rule）计算分子态$\mathcal{M}$的质量和流耦合常数（current coupling）；运用三点QCD求和规则（three-point QCD sum rule）估算$\mathcal{M}$与各个介子对的强耦合常数（strong couplings），从而分析其衰变过程。

Result: 分子态$\mathcal{M}$的质量为$m=(6290\pm50)$ MeV，总衰变宽度为$\Gamma[\mathcal{M}]=(149\pm21)$ MeV。主要衰变道为$\mathcal{M}\to J/\psi J/\psi$，子衰变道包括$\mathcal{M}\to D_{(s)}^{(\ast)+}D_{(s)}^{(\ast)-}$、$DD_{1}(2420)$、$D_s D_{s1}(2460)$及$D_{(s)}^{(\ast)0}\bar{D}_{(s)}^{(\ast)0}$等，这些过程源于组份$\bar{c}c$夸克湮灭为轻夸克对$\bar{q}q$和$\bar{s}s$。

Conclusion: 通过质量与衰变宽度的比较，分子态$\mathcal{M}$被认为是张量共振态$X(6200)$的一个可能候选者。

Abstract: The hadronic tensor molecule $\mathcal{M}=J/ψJ/ψ$ is investigated in the framework of QCD sum rule method. We evaluate its mass and current coupling using the two-point SR approach. Our result $m=(6290 \pm 50)~ \mathrm{MeV}$ for the mass of $\mathcal{M}$ indicates that it can decay to a pair of mesons $J/ψJ/ψ$. Apart from this dominant channel there are subdominant modes of the molecule $\mathcal{M}$ generated due to annihilation of constituent $\overline{c}c$ quarks to pairs of light quarks $ \overline{q}q$ and $\overline{s}s$. This mechanism launches processes $ \mathcal{M} \to D_{(s)}^{(\ast )+}D_{(s)}^{(\ast )-}$, $DD_{1}(2420)$, $ D_sD_{s1}(2460)$ and $D_{(s)}^{(\ast )0}\overline{D}_{(s)}^{(\ast )0}$. The decays of $\mathcal{M}$ are explored by applying technical tools of the three-point sum rule approach which is necessary to estimate strong couplings at $\mathcal{M}$-meson-meson vertices. Comparing the mass $m$ of the molecule $\mathcal{M}$ and its decay width $Γ[\mathcal{M}]=(149 \pm 21)~ \mathrm{MeV}$ with available experimental data, we discuss the molecule $\mathcal{M}$ as a possible candidate to the tensor resonance $X(6200)$.

</details>

Abstract: We study the sensitivity of current and future collider observables to top-quark SMEFT operators through a one-operator-at-a-time analysis. Using data from the Tevatron, LEP, and LHC Run~2, as well as projections for the HL-LHC and future lepton colliders, we identify the measurements that provide the strongest individual constraints. ### [112] [A first extraction of gluon TMDs from Higgs data at the LHC](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28216)
*Simone Anedda,Valerio Bertone,Giuseppe Bozzi,Matteo Cerutti*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文首次在TMD因子化框架下，基于LHC上希格斯玻色子产生数据（ATLAS和CMS的$q_T$分布测量），提取了非极化胶子的横向动量依赖（TMD）部分子分布，计算精度达N$^3$LL，并考虑了线性极化胶子TMD的贡献。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 胶子TMD部分子分布（gluon transverse-momentum-dependent parton distribution）是理解量子色动力学（QCD）中胶子非微扰结构的关键，但此前从未通过希格斯玻色子产生数据直接提取。该研究旨在填补这一空白，并为未来多过程联合分析建立基线。

Method: 基于ATLAS和CMS在$\sqrt{s}=8$和$13$ TeV下希格斯玻色子$q_T$分布的测量数据（双光子与四轻子衰变道），在TMD因子化适用的小$q_T$区域进行分析。理论预言计算至N$^3$LL精度，并纳入线性极化胶子TMD $h_1^{\perp g}$的贡献；同时一致地引入了双体和四体末态的fiducial选择。

Result: 拟合结果同时复现了实验数据的形状与归一化，表明对胶子TMD的非微扰内容具有中等灵敏度。进一步评估了微扰级数收敛性以及所提取分布在$q_T$截断变化下的稳定性。

Conclusion: 该提取为未来结合LHC希格斯测量与更广泛硬标度范围的胶子敏感过程进行联合分析提供了基线。

Abstract: We present the first extraction of the unpolarised gluon transverse-momentum-dependent (TMD) parton distribution from Higgs-boson production data at the LHC within the framework of TMD factorisation. The analysis is based on the currently available set of ATLAS and CMS measurements of the Higgs $q_T$ distribution at $\sqrt{s} = 8$ and $13$ TeV in the diphoton and four-lepton decay channels, restricted to the small-$q_T$ region where TMD factorisation is applicable. Theoretical predictions are computed up to N$^3$LL accuracy, with the contribution of the linearly polarised gluon TMD $h_1^{\perp g}$ accounted for. Fiducial selections are consistently incorporated for both two- (diphoton) and four-body (four-lepton) final states. The fit reproduces both the shape and the normalisation of the experimental data, and yields a moderate sensitivity to the nonperturbative content of gluon TMDs. We further assess the convergence of the perturbative expansion and the stability of the extracted distribution under variations of the $q_T$ cut. This analysis provides a baseline for future extractions combining LHC Higgs measurements with other gluon-sensitive processes spanning a broader range of hard scales.

</details>


### [113] [Dark Matter Interpretation of the Super-Kamiokande Antineutrino Excess in $\mathrm{U}(1)_{L_μ-L_τ}$ model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28275)
*Motoi Endo,Yushi Mura,Tenta Tsuji*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文探讨利用U(1)_{L_μ-L_τ}模型中的MeV尺度暗物质湮灭产生中微子，以解释Super-Kamiokande观测到的弥散超新星中微子背景（DSNB）在约2.3σ水平的过剩信号。暗物质为质量约22 MeV的狄拉克费米子，通过轻Z'媒介子湮灭为ν_μ和ν_τ，经味振荡部分转化为反电子中微子，同时通过热退耦机制解释观测到的 relic abundance。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Super-Kamiokande各阶段数据分析显示，在能量约20 MeV的反电子中微子事件中存在约2.3σ水平的过剩信号，高于弥散超新星中微子背景（diffuse supernova neutrino background, DSNB）的预期。该研究旨在探索这一过剩是否可由MeV尺度暗物质湮灭为中微子来解释。

Method: 研究采用U(1)_{L_μ-L_τ}规范模型，将暗物质（dark matter）构建为质量约22 MeV的狄拉克费米子（Dirac fermion），通过轻Z'媒介子（mediator）湮灭为ν_μ\barν_μ和ν_τ\barν_τ对，再借助中微子味振荡（flavor oscillations）部分转化为\barν_e，从而匹配观测信号。

Result: 该暗物质湮灭方案能够同时解释Super-Kamiokande观测到的过剩信号，并通过热退耦（thermal freeze-out）机制再现暗物质观测丰度（relic abundance）。

Conclusion: 该模型在解释DSNB过剩方面具有可行性，但需进一步考虑中微子三段产生（neutrino trident production）、NA64-μ、Borexino实验以及有效中微子代数目增量ΔN_eff等相关实验室和宇宙学约束。

Abstract: Recent Super-Kamiokande analyses of the diffuse supernova neutrino background, based on data across all SK phases, indicate a mild preference over the zero-DSNB hypothesis at the level of about $2.3σ$ with electron-like antineutrino events at $E_{\barν_e} \simeq 20\,\mathrm{MeV}$. We investigate whether this excess can be explained by MeV-scale dark matter annihilation into neutrinos in a $\mathrm{U}(1)_{L_μ- L_τ}$ model. The dark matter is a Dirac fermion with $m_χ\simeq 22\,\mathrm{MeV}$ that annihilates via a light $Z'$ mediator into $ν_μ\barν_μ$ and $ν_τ\barν_τ$, which are partly converted into $\barν_e$ through flavor oscillations. We find that this scenario simultaneously accounts for the excess and the observed relic abundance via thermal freeze-out. We further discuss the relevant laboratory and cosmological constraints, including neutrino trident production, NA64-$μ$, Borexino, and the contribution to $ΔN_\mathrm{eff}$.

</details>


### [114] [Probing hidden-charm pentaquarks from the $πN\rightarrow J/ψN$ reaction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28285)
*Samson Clymton,Sun-Young Ryu,Jung-Keun Ahn,Hyun-Chul Kim*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文利用离壳耦合道形式（off-shell coupled-channel formalism）研究πN → J/ψN反应中隐粲五夸克共振态（hidden-charm pentaquark resonances）的动力学产生机制，发现u道Λ_c交换显著增强了通过\bar{D}^{(*)}Σ_c中间态的重散射贡献，从而在总截面上产生微巴量级的五夸克信号峰。部分波分析显示P_{c\bar{c}}(4312)和P_{c\bar{c}}(4457)分别以J^P=1/2^-和3/2^-的清晰峰结构出现，而P_{c\bar{c}}(4380)和J^P=5/2^-态则因缺乏所需张量相互作用而被强烈抑制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 受J/ψ光产生（photoproduction）实验中未观测到五夸克信号的启发，本文旨在分析在πN → J/ψN反应中是否存在动态生成隐粲五夸克共振态的可能性，并解释为何该反应能产生与光产生实验不同的结果。

Method: 采用离壳耦合道形式（off-shell coupled-channel formalism）构建反应框架；利用有效拉格朗日量（effective Lagrangians）构造包含t道介子交换和u道重子交换的两体核振幅（two-body kernel amplitudes），并显式评估重散射效应（rescattering effects）。

Result: u道Λ_c交换（该贡献在光产生核中不存在）大幅增强了通过\bar{D}^{(*)}Σ_c中间态的重散射贡献；\bar{D}^{(*)}Σ_c^{(*)}道的贡献达到与\bar{D}^{(*)}Λ_c道相当的量级，直接导致显著的五夸克信号。部分波分析表明，P_{c\bar{c}}(4312)和P_{c\bar{c}}(4457)分别以J^P=1/2^-和3/2^-的清晰峰结构出现，而P_{c\bar{c}}(4380)和J^P=5/2^-态被强烈抑制。总截面在峰位处达到微巴（microbarn）量级。

Conclusion: πN → J/ψN反应中，u道Λ_c交换的存在是产生隐粲五夸克共振信号的关键因素，这解释了为何该反应通道能展现光产生实验中缺失的五夸克结构；不同J^P态的产生与否由相互作用中是否包含所需的张量成分决定。

Abstract: We investigate the dynamical generation of hidden-charm pentaquark resonances in the $πN \to J/ψN$ reaction utilizing an off-shell coupled-channel formalism. Motivated by the absence of pentaquark signals in $J/ψ$ photoproduction, we evaluate rescattering effects with two-body kernel amplitudes constructed from effective Lagrangians that explicitly incorporate $t$-channel meson and $u$-channel baryon exchanges. We demonstrate that the $u$-channel $Λ_c$ exchange, of which an analogous contribution is absent in the photoproduction kernel, greatly enhances the rescattering contributions through the $\bar{D}^{(*)}Σ_c$ intermediate states. Consequently, the $\bar{D}^{(*)}Σ_c^{(*)}$ channels yield contributions of comparable magnitude to the $\bar{D}^{(*)}Λ_c$ channels, directly leading to prominent pentaquark signals. The partial-wave analysis reveals that the $P_{c\bar{c}}(4312)$ and $P_{c\bar{c}}(4457)$ states emerge as clear peak structures with $J^P=1/2^-$ and $3/2^-$, respectively. In contrast, the $P_{c\bar{c}}(4380)$ and $J^P=5/2^-$ states are strongly suppressed because the $Λ_c$ exchange does not provide the required tensor interactions. The result for the total cross section reaches the microbarn level at the peak positions.

Abstract: In this work, we further develop the application of the topological diagram approach (TDA) to charmed baryon weak decays $\mathcal{B}_c \to \mathcal{B} V$ with a vector meson in the final state. By incorporating the Korner-Pati-Woo theorem, we show that only five independent sets of TDA parameters are required. Relations among different decay channels arising from isospin, U-spin, and V-spin symmetries are explicitly derived within the TDA framework. Partial wave contributions and form factors associated with different topological diagrams are extracted from global fits to the experimental data. It is found that the form factors $A_2$ and $B_2$ induced from the tensor interaction of the vector mreson with octet baryons are comparable in magnitude to $A_1$ and $B_1$, implying the importance of the tensor coupling in $\mathcal{B}_c \to \mathcal{B} V$ decays. More physical observables, including up-down asymmetries, longitudinal polarizations as well as observables in the subsequent decays are also predicted. Our results provide a systematic framework for understanding charmed baryon weak decays with vector mesons and can be further tested with future experiments.

### [117] [Generation as Compositeness: A Subconstituent Interpretation of the $B$-Lattice Flavor Hierarchy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28608)
*Vernon Barger*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 该论文将B-晶格味框架解释为一种逐代复合层次结构（compositeness hierarchy）：三代费米子均为初态手征场，但第三代汤川耦合未被 dressing（Q=0），而轻代费米子通过自旋为0的子成分链（“跳”，hops）获得汤川耦合，其深度由Z9离散规范对称性计数。Z9电荷允许(a,b)双指标分解，识别出两种跳（α, β），并通过“九分之一阶梯”（ninths ladder）Λ×ε^(n/9)组织从电弱标度v_EW到普朗克标度M_Pl的所有基本尺度。该晶格结构生成了CKM和PMNS混合参数化、中微子跷跷板基准值m3≈51 meV、轴子质量窗口ma~7–12 μeV，以及tanβ≈10–16的预测，所有结果仅依赖两个参数（Λ和ε=14/75）。代依赖的Peccei-Quinn电荷将轴子-光子耦合（C_aγ≈0.6–1.0）从“回到不可见”压制中恢复。论文还给出了一个基于超色约束标量（hypercolor-confined scalars）并通过规范不变信使链与SM耦合的示例性紫外实现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有味物理框架中，三代费米子汤川耦合的层级结构（hierarchy）缺乏第一性原理解释；论文旨在通过B-晶格味框架的复合层次结构，将代间汤川耦合的差异归因于子成分跳链的深度，并用Z9离散对称性统一标度层次，从而用极少数参数同时解释费米子混合、中微子质量、轴子质量窗口及tanβ等观测特征。

Method: 提出B-晶格味框架，将三代费米子视为初态手征场，第三代汤川耦合为裸值（Q=0），而第一、二代通过深度由Z9电荷计数的自旋0子成分跳链获得汤川耦合；引入(a, b)双指标分解识别两种跳（α, β），构建“九分之一阶梯”Λ×ε^(n/9)以组织从电弱标度到普朗克标度的能级；利用该晶格结构导出CKM和PMNS混合参数化（混合指数表示为电荷差ΔQ加上±1/9的Fritzsch-Xing相移），并结合DFSZ-II双希格斯二重态模型推导tanβ预测。

Result: 仅用两个参数（Λ和ε=14/75）得到：CKM和PMNS混合参数化（所有混合指数可表达为电荷差ΔQ经Fritzsch-Xing相移±1/9修正）、中微子跷跷板基准质量m3≈51 meV、轴子质量窗口ma~7–12 μeV、tanβ≈10–16。代依赖的Peccei-Quinn电荷将轴子-光子耦合C_aγ从压制恢复至0.6–1.0。提供了基于超色约束标量经规范不变信使链与SM耦合的示例性紫外实现。

Conclusion: B-晶格味框架通过复合层次结构和Z9离散对称性，以极简参数集同时解释了费米子质量层级、混合角、中微子质量、轴子质量和tanβ等多项低能可观测量，展示了该框架的理论自洽性和预测能力。给出的紫外实现示例证明了该方案在更高能标下具有可行性。

Abstract: We interpret the $B$-lattice flavor framework as a compositeness hierarchy: all three fermion generations are elementary chiral fields, but third-generation Yukawa couplings are undressed ($Q=0$), while lighter generations acquire their Yukawa couplings through chains of spin-$0$ subconstituents (``hops'') whose depth is counted by the $\mathbb{Z}_9$ discrete gauge symmetry. The $\mathbb{Z}_9$ charge admits a two-index decomposition $q_9\mapsto(a,b)$ that identifies two hop species ($α$, $β$) and organizes all fundamental scales from $v_{\rm EW}$ to $M_{\rm Pl}$ on a ``ninths ladder'' $Λ\timesε^{n/9}$. The lattice structure yields the CKM and PMNS mixing parameterizations (with all mixing exponents expressible as charge differences $ΔQ$ dressed by a universal Fritzsch--Xing phase shift of $\pm 1/9$), a seesaw benchmark $m_3\simeq 51$~meV, the axion mass window $m_a\sim 7$--$12\;μ$eV, and the prediction $\tanβ\simeq 10$--$16$ (from the chain internal factor combined with the DFSZ-II two-Higgs-doublet structure), all from two parameters ($Λ$ and $ε= 14/75$). Generation-dependent Peccei--Quinn charges restore the axion--photon coupling ($C_{aγ}\simeq 0.6$--$1.0$) from ``back to invisible'' suppression. An illustrative UV realization in terms of hypercolor-confined scalars communicated to the SM by a gauge-invariant messenger chain is presented as an existence proof.

### [118] [Matching second-order classical and 1-loop quantum tensor power spectra in de Sitter spacetime](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27910)
*A. Hauser,M. Laine*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 暴胀张量功率谱的大幅修正可能来自二阶标量诱导经典效应或1-loop量子修正，但二者并非独立。需要厘清两者的关系及其对物理观测的影响。

Method: 以无质量极小耦合标量场为例，采用维数正规化（dimensional regularization）和动量截断（momentum cutoff）两种方法，将完整1-loop结果分解为经典部分和真空部分，分析其红外发散行为，并提出“非微扰重整化”（non-perturbative renormalization）程序。

Result: 经典部分在维数正规化下存在红外发散，对应小共动动量（comoving momenta）的长期影响；完整1-loop量子结果中这些发散相互抵消。引入动量截断后，红外敏感性表现为三次发散（cubic divergence）。

Conclusion: 如果“非微扰重整化”方法能在实际系统中实现，将有助于整合暴胀标量诱导引力波的数值研究。

Abstract: Large corrections to the inflationary tensor power spectrum have been speculated to emerge either as second-order scalar-induced classical effects, or as 1-loop quantum corrections. These two sources are not independent of each other. Choosing the example of a massless minimally coupled scalar field, we show how the full 1-loop result can be divided into its classical and vacuum parts. Working first in dimensional regularization, we show that the classical part is IR divergent, with IR referring to small comoving momenta that have an influence for a very long time. In the full 1-loop quantum result, these divergences cancel. Introducing then a momentum cutoff that permits for a numerical evaluation of the classical contribution, we show that the IR sensitivity manifests itself as a cubic divergence. We suggest a procedure of "non-perturbative renormalization" for extracting physical information not affected by the divergence. If this can be implemented in realistic systems, it could consolidate numerical studies of inflationary scalar-induced gravitational waves.

Method: 采用功能重整化群（functional renormalization group）方法，对包含 CP-破缺算符的低能有效理论进行重整化群（renormalization group）流分析，并允许规范耦合（gauge coupling）随能标跑动。

We find that allowing for the running gauge coupling, the $CP$-violating four-fermion interaction becomes relevant in the chirally broken phase. In the presence of a finite quark mass, the RG running of the $θ$-parameter is shown to be strongly suppressed toward the infrared. The present work clarifies how strong-$CP$ effects generated at UV can non-trivially be transferred to the infrared physics in QCD-like theories.

*Amelie Claussen,Sebastián Mendizabal*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究复标量场中由有限化学势产生的非平衡相干效应。在正常相下，通过求解Schwinger-Keldysh-Kadanoff-Baym方程发现，有限化学势将初始条件记忆转化为瞬态的粒子-反粒子干涉图案，该效应并非新的平衡模式，而是随阻尼在无穷长时间后消失的初始数据相位敏感残留。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索具有守恒U(1)荷的复标量场中由有限化学势（chemical potential）诱导的非平衡相干效应，以及该效应对初始条件记忆的影响。

Method: 将标量激发视为与平衡热库（thermal reservoir）耦合的探针，自能采用平衡核（equilibrium kernel），不考虑对热库的反作用。在正常相中，当化学势小于色散关系时，保持粒子和反粒子准粒子极点分离，求解Schwinger-Keldysh-Kadanoff-Baym方程。

Result: 源驱动的非均匀统计传播子由热库固定并弛豫到通常的退相干平衡形式。均匀解携带初始条件记忆，有限化学势通过分裂两个荷扇区的相位，将这种记忆转化为瞬态的粒子-反粒子干涉图案。该效应不是新的平衡模式，而是初始数据的相位敏感残留，在t→∞时被阻尼擦除。

Conclusion: 定义了从混合荷扇区项中提取的归一化干涉衬比度（normalized interference contrast），利用热标量φ⁴理论的等离激元阻尼率（plasmon damping rate）说明了弛豫过程，并指出该正常相解展示了先于玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚（Bose-Einstein condensation）的红外增强现象。

Abstract: We study a nonequilibrium coherent effect generated by a finite chemical potential in a complex scalar field with a conserved $U(1)$ charge. The scalar excitation is treated as a probe coupled to an equilibrium thermal reservoir, so the self-energy is an equilibrium kernel and there is no backreaction on the bath. Solving the Schwinger-Keldysh-Kadanoff-Baym equations in the normal phase, when the chemical potential is smaller than the dispersion relation, we keep the particle and antiparticle quasiparticle poles separate. The source-driven inhomogeneous statistical propagator is fixed by the reservoir and relaxes to the usual decoherent equilibrium form. By contrast, the homogeneous solution carries initial-condition memory; finite chemical potential turns this memory into a transient particle-antiparticle interference pattern by splitting the two charge-sector phases. The effect is not a new equilibrium mode, but a phase-sensitive remnant of the initial data that is erased by damping as $t\to\infty$. We define a normalized interference contrast extracted from the mixed charge-sector terms, illustrate the relaxation using the plasmon damping rate of hot scalar $φ^4$ theory, and show that the same normal-phase solution displays the infrared enhancement that precedes Bose-Einstein condensation.

</details>
