### [122] [Lattice-Trapped Atom Interferometry with a Bose-Einstein condensate: Observation and Control of Interactions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27777)
*Emmett Hough,Tahiyat Rahman,Forest Tschirhart,Subhadeep Gupta*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 本文实验实现了一种基于一维光学晶格（optical lattice）束缚的原子波包干涉仪，使用弱相互作用的镱（Ytterbium）玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚体（Bose-Einstein condensate）作为干涉源，通过脉冲光驻波进行相干分裂与束缚。实验直接观察到原子相互作用导致的干涉对比度变化与相移，并通过调控原子密度来优化干涉仪性能，实验结果与平均场（mean-field）理论模型吻合。该工作探索了从高相空间密度提升性能到超越单原子物理的边界，为实现多体效应增强的计量学应用打开了大门。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 基于一维光学晶格束缚原子波包的精密干涉测量在量子传感（quantum sensing）领域具有广泛应用前景，如重力测量、加速度测量、地球物理学及基础物理检验。然而，原子间相互作用对干涉仪性能的影响及其调控机制尚需实验探索。

Method: 干涉仪的两个干涉臂来源于弱相互作用的镱玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚体，通过脉冲光驻波（pulsed optical standing waves）实现相干分裂与束缚，之后进行复合。通过改变原子数或样品体积以调控密度，系统研究原子相互作用对干涉对比度（contrast）和相移（phase shift）的影响。

Result: 直接观测到由原子相互作用引起的干涉对比度变化和相移。通过改变原子密度，实现对相互作用的控制并优化了干涉仪性能。实验结果与平均场理论模型有效吻合。

Conclusion: 该工作实验上探索了从通过高相空间密度（phase space density）提升性能到超越单原子物理（single-atom physics）的边界，为在晶格束缚原子干涉平台上引入多体效应（many-body effects）以实现计量学（metrological）进步开辟了道路。

Abstract: Precision interferometry with atomic wavepackets confined in a one-dimensional optical lattice is an emergent paradigm in quantum sensing of forces and fields, with applications in gravimetry, accelerometry, geophysics, and fundamental physics tests. We report on the realization of a lattice-trapped interferometer where the two arms are sourced from a weakly-interacting ytterbium Bose-Einstein condensate, coherently split and trapped by pulsed optical standing waves before recombination. We directly observe atomic interactions through contrast changes and phase shifts of the interferometer. By changing either the atom number or the sample volume to vary the density, we demonstrate control over interactions and optimize interferometer performance. Our observations are effectively captured by a mean-field theoretical model of the system. This work experimentally probes the boundary where improved performance from source brightening through higher phase space density transitions into a regime beyond single-atom physics in lattice-trapped atom interferometry, and opens a door to incorporating many-body effects for metrological advances in such platforms.

</details>


### [123] [Dark-Soliton Branch Blocking in Transonic Bose--Einstein Condensate Flows](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27863)
*Edilberto O. Silva*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 本文研究了玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚体（Bose-Einstein condensate）中一维暗孤子（dark-soliton）分支在稳态跨声速流（stationary transonic flow）中能否维持上游运动的问题。研究表明，暗孤子的上游运动受分支存在性约束（branch-existence constraint），声速点（sonic point）是暗孤子分支的上游边界，而非硬壁或孤子测地线面。数值模拟验证了亚声速侧的上游传播、有限深度停滞以及超声速侧的下游平流等行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统上，玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚体中的声学视界（acoustic horizon）通过长波长Bogoliubov声子（Bogoliubov phonon）描述。本文旨在探索非线性视角：暗孤子分支是否能在稳态跨声速流中实现相对实验室坐标系（laboratory frame）的上游运动，从而揭示声学视界的非线性机制。

Method: 构造了稳态跨声速Gross–Pitaevskii背景（Gross–Pitaevskii backgrounds），并在开放非周期域（open, nonperiodic domain）中对完整序参数（order parameter）进行时间演化。通过收敛性检验、分支一致性（branch-consistency）、局域密度（local-density）、相位跃变（phase-jump）以及密集的无量纲上游尝试参数扫描来支持孤子类解释（soliton-like interpretation）。

Result: 数值模拟观察到：暗孤子在亚声速侧（subsonic side）可实现上游传播，在亚声速侧出现有限深度停滞（finite-depth stalling），而在超声速侧（supersonic region）初始化的缺陷（defect）若具有相对于流体的上游速度（upstream velocity），则表现为下游平流（downstream advection）。这表明声速点是暗孤子分支的上游边缘，而非硬壁或孤子测地线面。

Conclusion: 暗孤子上游运动的可行性受限于分支存在性约束，而非Gross–Pitaevskii场中任意密度极小值（density minima）的严格下界（rigorous lower bound）。这一结果为理解凝聚体声学视界的非线性行为提供了新的约束性视角。

Abstract: Acoustic horizons in Bose--Einstein condensates are usually characterized through long-wavelength Bogoliubov phonons. We study a nonlinear counterpart: whether a one-dimensional dark-soliton branch can sustain upstream laboratory motion in a stationary transonic flow. The mechanism is local at leading order. A regular dark soliton has a bounded fluid-frame velocity, limited by the local sound speed; therefore, in the supersonic region, the background flow exceeds the largest upstream velocity available to the soliton branch. The sonic point is thus the upstream edge of the local dark-soliton branch, rather than a hard wall or a soliton geodesic surface. We construct stationary transonic Gross--Pitaevskii backgrounds and evolve the full order parameter in an open, nonperiodic domain. The simulations show upstream propagation on the subsonic side, finite-depth stalling on the subsonic side, and downstream advection for defects initialized in the supersonic region with upstream velocity relative to the fluid. Convergence, branch-consistency, local-density, phase-jump, and a dense scan of dimensionless upstream attempts support the soliton-like interpretation. The result is a branch-existence constraint, not a rigorous lower bound on arbitrary density minima of the Gross--Pitaevskii field.

</details>


### [124] [Hall effect in multi-leg bosonic ladders](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28090)
*Edmond Orignac,Roberta Citro,Thierry Giamarchi*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 本文利用玻色化（bosonization）方法分析通量贯穿下相互作用玻色子N腿梯子（N-leg ladders）的基态霍尔响应（ground state Hall response）。推导出带曲率（band curvature）微扰展开中霍尔失衡（Hall imbalance）的显式表达式，并保留完整相互作用项；发现小磁场下霍尔电阻（Hall resistance）正比于电荷刚度（charge stiffness）对数对密度的导数，推广了两腿情形结果；同时证明在迈斯纳相（Meissner phase）低温下霍尔电阻的修正呈指数小。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解和推广相互作用玻色子体系在梯子几何（ladder geometry）下的霍尔响应，尤其是从两腿情况推广至多腿（N腿）情形，并系统考虑相互作用、带曲率及温度效应的贡献。

Method: 采用玻色化（bosonization）方法对通量贯穿的N腿玻色子梯子模型进行理论分析；在带曲率（band curvature）微扰展开下推导出霍尔失衡（Hall imbalance）的显式表达式，并在该过程中完全保留相互作用项。

Result: 小磁场下霍尔电阻（Hall resistance）正比于电荷刚度（charge stiffness）对数对密度的导数，该结果推广了原有的两腿情形结论。此外，在迈斯纳相（Meissner phase）中，低温对霍尔电阻的修正呈指数小（exponentially small）。

Conclusion: 通过玻色化方法，成功将两腿梯子的霍尔响应关系推广到N腿情形，并揭示了温度在迈斯纳相中对霍尔电阻的指数抑制效应，为理解多腿玻色子梯子中的霍尔效应提供了理论依据。

Abstract: We use bosonization to analyze the ground state Hall response of interacting bosonic N-leg ladders threaded by a flux. We derive an explicit expression of the Hall imbalance in a perturbative expansion in the band curvature, retaining fully the interactions. For small magnetic field the Hall resistance is proportional to the derivative of the logarithm of the charge stiffness with respect to density, generalizing the result obtained in the two leg case. We also consider the effect of temperature, and establish that at low temperature, corrections to the Hall resistance are exponentially small in the Meissner phase.

</details>


### [125] [Wetting of quantum fluids: a route to free-standing shell-shaped quantum droplets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28469)
*Francesco Ancilotto*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 本文通过密度泛函方法研究三组分玻色混合体（$^{23}$Na, $^{39}$K, $^{41}$K）中自束缚量子液体之间的浸润现象（wetting phenomena），发现通过调谐散射长度可驱动从部分浸润到完全浸润的转变，并在完全浸润区形成无外约束的自束缚核壳状量子液滴，该液滴可维持量子化涡旋激发。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索多组分量子液滴中由表面张力调控驱动的浸润转变，以及利用浸润效应构建自由站立（free-standing）的壳状量子液滴的可行性。

Method: 采用包含平均场相互作用（mean-field interactions）和Lee-Huang-Yang量子涨落修正（quantum-fluctuation corrections）的密度泛函方法（density-functional approach），研究由组分(1,2)和(2,3)构成的两种二元量子液体，通过调谐组分间的散射长度 $a_{12}$ 调控表面张力。

Result: 增大 $a_{12}$ 可使(1,2)液体的表面张力显著变化，驱动从部分浸润（partial wetting）到完全浸润（complete wetting）的转变；圆柱帽几何中提取的接触角（contact angle）随 $a_{12}$ 增加连续减小，在临界值 $a_{12}^{c}= -42\,a_0$ 处消失；完全浸润区中，(1,2)液体包裹球形(2,3)液滴形成自束缚核壳液滴，组分-1密度呈壳状空心投影；此类液滴可维持量子化涡旋激发。

Conclusion: 浸润效应为制备自由站立壳状量子液滴提供了新途径，并为在多组分量子液滴中研究毛细现象（capillarity）、拓扑结构（topology）和超流性（superfluidity）开辟了新可能性。

Abstract: We investigate wetting phenomena between self-bound quantum fluids in a three-component Bose mixture of $^{23}$Na, $^{39}$K, and $^{41}$K atoms. Within a density-functional approach including mean-field interactions and Lee-Huang-Yang quantum-fluctuation corrections, we consider two binary quantum liquids, formed by components $(1,2)$ and $(2,3)$, and study the adsorption of the softer $(1,2)$ liquid on a stiffer $(2,3)$ substrate. By tuning the interspecies scattering length $a_{12}$, we show that the surface tension of the $(1,2)$ liquid can be strongly varied, driving a transition from partial wetting to complete wetting of the $(2,3)$ phase. The contact angle extracted from cylindrical-cap geometries decreases continuously with increasing $a_{12}$ and vanishes near a critical value $a_{12}^{c}= -42\,a_0$. In the complete-wetting regime, a finite amount of $(1,2)$ liquid wraps around a spherical $(2,3)$ droplet, producing a self-bound core-shell droplet without external confinement, whose component-1 density has a shell-like, hollow projection. We further show that such shell-shaped quantum droplets can sustain quantized vortical excitations. These results identify wetting as a route to engineering free-standing shell-shaped quantum liquids and suggest new possibilities for studying capillarity, topology, and superfluidity in multicomponent quantum droplets.

</details>


### [126] [Fractional short-time dynamics in driven quantum gases](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28606)
*Uri Sharell,Tilman Enss*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 本文发现具有短程吸引相互作用的量子气体在含时相互作用下，其小间距配对振幅满足分数阶微分方程（FDE），并推导了动力学解析解，揭示了从短时共形标度到长时流体力学吸引子（hydrodynamic attractor）的完整演化图像。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解量子气体在含时短程吸引相互作用下的配对动力学行为，特别是从非平衡短时间标度到长时弛豫的完整演化过程。

Method: 建立分数阶微分方程（FDE）描述小间距配对振幅，并通过突然淬火（quench）和幂律驱动（power-law drive）两种方式解析求解配对演化，同时结合Müller-Israel-Stewart型方程描述长时流体动力学行为。

Result: 短时间发现由共形不动点（conformal fixed point）控制的普适动力学，其动量分布呈现非热自相似标度（self-similar scaling），与实验定量吻合；长时间多体效应导致弛豫至平衡态，FDE退化为Müller-Israel-Stewart型流体力学吸引子方程。

Conclusion: 短程吸引量子气体在含时相互作用下的配对动力学可由分数阶微分方程统一描述，跨越从共形标度短时行为到流体力学吸引子长时弛豫的多时间尺度演化。

Abstract: Quantum gases with short-range attractive interaction have a tendency to form pairs. For time-dependent interaction we find that the pairing amplitude at small separation satisfies a fractional differential equation (FDE). We derive analytic solutions of the pairing evolution for sudden interaction quenches and power-law drives toward resonant scattering. We observe universal short-time dynamics governed by a conformal fixed point at which the momentum distribution exhibits nonthermal, self-similar scaling in time, in quantitative agreement with experiment. At longer times, many-body effects induce relaxation toward an equilibrium state. In this limit, the FDE turns into a Müller-Israel-Stewart type equation that describes a hydrodynamic attractor approaching equilibrium.

</details>

### [127] [Formation of bound composite vortices of a singly-quantized $^1$S$_0$ vortex and half-quantized $^3$P$_2$ vortices in the $^1$S$_0$-$^3$P$_2$ coexisting phase in neutron stars](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28718)
*Tatsuhiro Hattori,Muneto Nitta,Kazuyuki Sekizawa*

Main category: nucl-th

TL;DR: 本文通过Gross-Pitaevskii方程二维模拟，研究了中子星壳-核边界处$^1\text{S}_0$单量子涡旋（SQV）与$^3\text{P}_2$半整数量子涡旋（HQV）之间的耦合。发现约瑟夫森（Josephson）项诱导的强吸引力可使一个SQV与两个HQV形成紧密束缚的复合涡旋，并能驱动涡旋脱钉，为脉冲星自转突变（pulsar glitch）的多样性提供了候选机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 脉冲星自转突变被认为源自中子星超流内部量子化涡旋的动力学，而中子星外核中的$^3\text{P}_2$自旋三重态超流（spin-triplet superfluid）具有半整数量子涡旋（HQV），与内壳层$^1\text{S}_0$单量子涡旋（SQV）性质迥异。近期有理论提出两类涡旋耦合可形成大尺度涡旋网络，为解释观测到的脉冲星自转突变现象多样性提供可能机制，但该耦合的具体物理效应尚需定量研究。

Method: 采用描述$^1\text{S}_0$和$^3\text{P}_2$凝聚体的Gross-Pitaevskii方程，在壳-核边界共存相（coexistence phase）中对一个SQV和两个HQV进行二维数值模拟，系统变化密度-密度耦合常数和约瑟夫森耦合常数。

Result: 发现由两凝聚体相对相位产生的约瑟夫森项（Josephson term）在两个HQV与一个SQV之间诱导出强吸引力，其主导地位超过密度-密度耦合效应。当对HQV和SQV施加空间分离的钉扎势（pinning potentials）时，该吸引力足够强，可驱动涡旋脱钉（vortex depinning）。

Conclusion: 两个HQV和一个SQV可在壳-核边界处形成紧密束缚的复合涡旋（composite vortex），这一发现对理解中子星自转突变机制具有重要启示意义。

Abstract: Pulsar glitches are believed to originate from the dynamics of quantized vortices in the neutron superfluid interior. The outer core of a neutron star hosts a $^3\text{P}_2$ spin-triplet superfluid, whose half-integer quantum vortices (HQVs) are qualitatively different from the $^1\text{S}_0$ singly quantized vortices (SQVs) in the inner crust. It has recently been proposed that the coupling between these two vortex species gives rise to a large-scale vortex network, providing a candidate mechanism for the diversity of observed pulsar glitch phenomena. Using the Gross--Pitaevskii equations for the $^1\text{S}_0$ and $^3\text{P}_2$ condensates, we perform two-dimensional simulations of one SQV and two HQVs in a coexistence phase near the crust-core boundary, varying the density--density and Josephson coupling constants. We find that the Josephson term, arising from the relative phase between the two condensates, induces a strong attractive interaction between the two HQVs and the SQV, which dominates over the density--density coupling. When pinning potentials are applied to the HQVs and the SQV at spatially separated locations, this attraction is found to be sufficiently strong to drive vortex depinning. These results suggest that two HQVs and one SQV can form a tightly bound composite vortex at the crust-core boundary, with implications for the glitch mechanism in neutron stars.

</details>


### [128] [Three-dimensional orbital-free density functional theory description of nuclear pasta in the inner crust of neutron stars](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28783)
*Yo Nakamura,Kazuyuki Sekizawa*

Main category: nucl-th

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于无轨道密度泛函理论（OF-DFT）的自洽扩展托马斯-费米（SC-ETF）方法，用于高效、非经验地计算中子星内壳中各种核意面（nuclear pasta）结构，并通过三维计算成功再现并拓展了已知的复杂几何构型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 中子星内壳底部预期存在多种被称为"核意面"（nuclear pasta）的晶体结构，天体物理应用需要了解其在广泛条件下的性质。然而，三维全微观计算计算量巨大，难以开展系统性研究。

Method: 采用Skyrme能量密度泛函（energy density functional, EDF）的二阶扩展托马斯-费米（extended Thomas-Fermi, ETF）展开，构建仅依赖于中子与质子数密度的EDF；基于变分原理导出欧拉-拉格朗日方程（Euler-Lagrange equations），自洽求解最优的中子和质子密度分布，称为自洽ETF（self-consistent ETF, SC-ETF）方法。

Result: 在不同计算盒尺寸下进行三维SC-ETF计算，成功获得了随平均核子数密度变化的各种意面结构，与早期研究一致；此外还发现了弯曲和/或连接的杆、带孔板等其他奇异结构，突显了自洽形式化的优势。

Conclusion: SC-ETF方法可视为无轨道密度泛函理论（orbital-free DFT, OF-DFT）的一种实现，是一种有前景的工具，能够在不依赖几何形状经验假设的前提下高效描述复杂的核意面结构。

Abstract: Background: In the bottom layer of the inner crust of neutron stars, various crystalline structures are expected to emerge that are collectively called ``nuclear pasta.'' It is desired to know properties of nuclear pasta in a wide variety of conditions for astrophysical applications. However, three-dimensional fully-microscopic calculations require huge computational effort that makes it still challenging to carry out systematic calculations.
  Purpose: In this paper, we propose an efficient method to calculate various nuclear pasta configurations in a non-empirical manner, based on three-dimensional orbital-free density functional theory (OF-DFT). We demonstrate the feasibility of the proposed approach by applying it to densities throughout the inner crust of neutron stars.
  Methods: As a first application of OF-DFT for nuclear pasta, we employ the second-order extended Thomas-Fermi (ETF) expansion of Skyrme energy density functional (EDF) to construct an EDF that depends only on neutron and proton number densities. Based on the variational principle, we derive Euler-Lagrange equations to determine optimal neutron and proton density distributions and solve them self-consistently. In this work, we call this approach the self-consistent ETF (SC-ETF) method.
  Results: We perform three-dimensional SC-ETF calculations with various box sizes. We successfully obtain various pasta structures, depending on given average nucleon number densities, consistent with earlier studies. Moreover, we find other exotic structures, such as bending and/or connected rods, slabs with a hole, etc., underlining the advantage of the self-consistent formalism.
  Conclusions: We demonstrate that the SC-ETF method proposed in this study, which can be regarded as a realization of OF-DFT, is a promising tool that can efficiently describe complex pasta structures without empirical assumptions on geometric shapes.

</details>

### [129] [On the Validity of the Effective Theory of (Multi-)Field Inflation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27505)
*Andrea Ambrosi de Magistris,Alberto Salvio*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文在不依赖亚视界极限（sub-horizon limit）的条件下，确定了（多）场暴胀（inflation）低能有效理论中量子微扰的希尔伯特空间（Hilbert space）与振幅，利用狄拉克括号（Dirac brackets）处理标量场中的场混合与第二类约束，并估计了高阶导数修正（higher-derivative corrections）的量级，最后将结果应用于若干有限截断（finite cutoff）Λ 的暴胀模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 针对暴胀理论中的跨普朗克问题（trans-Planckian issues），现有的量子微扰处理通常依赖亚视界极限（sub-horizon limit），但该近似在高能截断下可能失效。作者希望在更一般的低能有效理论框架下，不依赖该极限，直接确定希尔伯特空间（Hilbert space）与微扰振幅，从而为高阶导数修正（higher-derivative corrections）的大小提供可靠估计。

Method: 作者在（多）场暴胀（multi-field inflation）的低能有效理论中，考虑标量场的场混合（field mixings）与第二类约束（second-class constraints），利用狄拉克括号（Dirac brackets）处理约束系统，从而确定量子微扰的希尔伯特空间（Hilbert space）与振幅。在此基础上，进一步估计高阶导数修正（higher-derivative corrections）的量级。

Result: 在慢滚暴胀（slow-roll inflation）的具体情形下，高阶导数修正（higher-derivative corrections）的量级可用第一慢滚参数（first slow-roll parameter）ε 和截断 Λ 表达。将该方法应用于希格斯暴胀（Higgs inflation）、斯塔罗宾斯基模型（Starobinsky model）、自然暴胀（natural inflation）和山顶暴胀（hilltop inflation）等有限 Λ 的暴胀模型中，获得了相应的估计结果。

Conclusion: 该研究为不依赖亚视界极限（sub-horizon limit）处理暴胀量子微扰提供了系统框架，尤其适用于存在场混合与第二类约束的标量扇区。所得的高阶导数修正（higher-derivative corrections）估计可推广至多种具体暴胀模型，为跨普朗克问题（trans-Planckian issues）的检验提供理论依据。

Abstract: Motivated by trans-Planckian issues in inflation, we determine the Hilbert space and amplitudes of quantum perturbations in the general low-energy effective theory of (multi-)field inflation without relying on the sub-horizon limit. The scalar sector is the most intricate, featuring field mixings and second-class constraints, which we handle using Dirac brackets. These results enable us to estimate the magnitude of higher-derivative corrections. In the specific case of slow-roll inflation, such estimate can be expressed in terms of the first slow-roll parameter $ε$ for a given cutoff $Λ$. We apply our results to several inflationary models with finite $Λ$: Higgs inflation, the Starobinsky model, natural inflation and hilltop inflation.

</details>


### [130] [Many-Body Quantum Chaos At All Time Scales](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27512)
*Antonio M. García-García,Lucas Sá,Jacobus J. M. Verbaarschot,Jie-Ping Zheng*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 通过结合 scramblon 形式论与随机矩阵理论（random-matrix-theory）技术，本研究解析描述了四体 N-马约拉纳 Sachdev-Ye-Kitaev 模型中多体量子混沌系统在所有时间尺度上的格林函数（Green's function）与超出时间序关联函数（out-of-time order correlation, OTOC）的动力学行为，揭示了从早期指数增长到晚期与系统尺寸呈指数关系的复杂弛豫模式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多体量子混沌系统在不同时间尺度上的动力学行为尚未被统一描述，特别是从早期指数增长到晚期随机矩阵行为的完整时间演化缺乏解析理解。本文旨在填补这一空白。

Method: 采用 scramblon 形式论与随机矩阵理论（random-matrix-theory）相结合的方法，对四体 N-马约拉纳 Sachdev-Ye-Kitaev 模型中的格林函数和 OTOC 进行解析求解，覆盖所有时间尺度。

Result: OTOC 在早期呈现指数增长，随后以格林函数主导的速率（即领头复 Ruelle-Pollicott 共振的实部）发生指数衰减。在随系统尺寸 N 呈指数增长的晚期时间尺度上，当 N mod 8 = 2, 6 时，两种关联函数均呈现 dip-ramp-plateau 模式，该模式因矩阵元与特征值的局域能量相关性而显著偏离遍历预言（ergodic prediction），即使在 Heisenberg 时间之后亦然。

Conclusion: 本文建立了从早期混沌增长到晚期量子遍历行为的完整解析框架，并指出在特定系统尺寸下，晚期动力学因局域能量相关性而偏离标准随机矩阵遍历行为，揭示了 SYK 模型中超越 Heisenberg 时间的非遍历结构。

Abstract: We describe the dynamics of many-body quantum chaotic systems at all time scales by studying the Green's and out-of-time order correlation (OTOC) functions of the four-body, $N$-Majorana Sachdev-Ye-Kitaev model. By combining the scramblon formalism and random-matrix-theory techniques, we obtain analytical expressions for these functions at all times. The early exponential growth of the OTOC is followed by an exponential decay at a rate governed by that of the Green's function (the real part of the leading complex Ruelle-Pollicott resonances). For late times that scale exponentially with $N$, both functions have a dip-ramp-plateau pattern for $N \mathrm{mod}8 = 2, 6$ that deviates substantially from the ergodic prediction due to local-in-energy correlations of matrix elements and eigenvalues, even after the Heisenberg time.

</details>


### [131] [Solitonic Construction of Artificial Neural Networks from Nonlinear Field Theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27568)
*R. A. C. Correa*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文通过非线性标量场论（nonlinear scalar field theory）中的孤子（soliton）自由度，构建了一类人工神经网络（artificial neural networks）的场论构造方案。该构造从连续场作用量出发，通过孤子集体坐标约化（collective-coordinate reduction）推导出神经网络层，并明确指出激活函数、权重矩阵、偏置和深度分别对应孤子的响应映射、有效相互作用能中的Hessian矩阵、外部源或边界条件以及孤子模空间上的离散演化参数。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 提出一种从场论第一性原理出发构造神经网络的系统方案，而非简单地将神经网络术语重新命名为孤子语言，旨在建立非线性场论与神经网络结构之间的可控映射关系。

Method: 从连续场作用量出发，将理论限制在包含局部稳定解的非微扰（nonperturbative）孤子扇区，通过集体坐标约化方法，将神经层推导为约化后孤子动力学的有限维输入-输出映射。激活函数对应于孤子响应分布或散射映射（scattering map），权重矩阵为孤子间有效相互作用能的Hessian矩阵或交叠矩阵，偏置由外部源、真空不对称性或边界驱动诱导，深度为孤子模空间上的离散演化参数。以φ⁴扭结（kink）为例，推导出tanh和logistic sigmoid激活函数，并通过算子分裂（operator-splitting）近似得到多层前馈形式。

Result: 在φ⁴扭结模型中，tanh激活和logistic sigmoid函数自然地从扭结（kink）轮廓产生；神经网络架构仅在指定场作用量、孤子假设、模空间度规（moduli-space metric）、相互作用泛函和投影映射之后才被得到，从而建立了从非线性场论到神经网络结构的可控路径。

Conclusion: 该构造方案的核心贡献在于提供了一条从非线性场论到神经网络结构的受控路线，其鲁棒性（robustness）源于孤子扇区内在的能量稳定性与拓扑稳定性（topological stability）。

Abstract: We present a field-theoretic construction of a class of artificial neural networks from solitonic degrees of freedom in nonlinear scalar field theory. The purpose is not to rename a standard neural layer in the language of solitons, but to start from a continuum action, restrict the theory to a nonperturbative sector containing localized stable solutions, perform a collective-coordinate reduction, and derive the neural layer as the finite-dimensional input-output map of the reduced solitonic dynamics. In this construction, the computational unit is a projected collective coordinate of a localized field configuration rather than an elementary point variable; the activation function is the solitonic response profile or scattering map; the weight matrix is the Hessian or overlap matrix of an effective interaction energy among solitons; the bias is induced by external sources, vacuum asymmetry, or boundary forcing; and depth is a discrete evolution parameter on the solitonic moduli space. We develop the construction explicitly for the \(φ^4\) kink, where the \(\tanh\) activation and the logistic sigmoid arise from the kink profile, and then derive the multilayer feedforward form from an operator-splitting approximation to collective-coordinate gradient flow. We emphasize the novelty criterion: the neural architecture is obtained only after specifying the field action, the solitonic ansatz, the moduli-space metric, the interaction functional, and the projection map. The result is a controlled route from nonlinear field theory to neural-network structure, with robustness tied to the energetic and topological stability of the solitonic sector.

</details>


### [132] [Robin holography in AdS and BTZ: double-trace RG flow and exceptional points](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27641)
*Yiru Wang,Juanyi Yang*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文精确构造了 AdS_{d+1} 和 BTZ 黑洞上的 Robin 型体-边界传播子（Robin bulk-to-boundary propagator），将双迹重整化群流（double-trace RG flow）几何实现为一族边界条件，并揭示了沿此族存在的例外点（exceptional point）作为非厄米相边界（non-Hermitian phase boundary），可在有限实动量和温度下通过调节 Robin 耦合达到。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为了将双迹重整化群流（double-trace RG flow）几何实现为一族边界条件，并研究该族参数空间中体-边界对应关系（bulk-boundary correspondence）的拓扑结构，尤其是例外点（exceptional point）的物理意义。

Method: 精确构造了 Breitenlöhner–Freedman 标量场在 AdS_{d+1} 和 BTZ 黑洞上的 Robin 型体-边界传播子（Robin bulk-to-boundary propagator）；从边值问题（boundary-value problem）本身导出核的紫外（UV）和红外（IR）链展开，无需辅助场退耦（auxiliary-field decoupling）；在 BTZ 上得到闭合形式的 Robin 核（Robin kernel）及对应的准正规模（quasinormal mode）轨迹族。

Result: 识别出沿双迹流参数族存在例外点（exceptional point）轨迹，在该点两条准正规模轨迹合并为 Jordan 块；该例外点构成非厄米相边界（non-Hermitian phase boundary），越过它时全局极点配对拓扑（pole-pairing topology）发生重组；该相变与通过解析延拓动量或频率达到的全息例外点不同，可在有限实动量和温度下通过调节物理 Robin 耦合实现。

Conclusion: 双迹重整化群流（double-trace RG flow）不仅实现了几何上的边界条件插值，还隐含着非厄米拓扑相变结构；例外点（exceptional point）提供了一个在有限实动量和温度下可观测的全息相变信号，拓展了全息对偶中边界条件可观测效应的理解。

Abstract: We construct the exact Robin bulk-to-boundary propagator for a Breitenlöhner--Freedman scalar on AdS$_{d+1}$ and the BTZ black hole, realizing the double-trace RG flow between standard and alternate quantization geometrically as a one-parameter family of bulk boundary conditions. We derive the UV and IR chain expansions of the kernel intrinsically from the boundary-value problem, without an auxiliary-field decoupling, and identify a branch split at each order that separates the local data the boundary CFT observes from finite-bulk-depth structure visible only to bulk probes -- the part of $K_f$ that distinguishes holographic reconstruction from boundary calculation.
  On BTZ we obtain the closed-form Robin kernel and the corresponding family of quasinormal-mode trajectories, each connecting an alternate-quantization pole at $g=0$ to a standard one at $g\to\infty$. We locate an exceptional-point locus along this family at which two trajectories coalesce into a Jordan block, and show it acts as a non-Hermitian phase boundary for the double-trace flow itself: crossing it reorganizes the global pole-pairing topology of the spectrum. Unlike holographic EPs reached by analytic continuation in momentum or frequency, this transition lives on the interpolation between quantizations and is reachable at finite real momentum and temperature by tuning the physical Robin coupling.

</details>


### [133] [Twistor approach to classical and quantum D0-brane](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27754)
*Igor Bandos,Mirian Tsulaia*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文建立了D0-膜（D0-brane）的超扭量（supertwistor）方法，该模型是十维时空中的IIA型有质量超粒子。通过受约束的OSp(32|1)超扭量变量，展示了与旋量动框架（spinor moving frame）表述的联系，并用两种方法完成了量子化。量子态谱描述了线性化IIA型超引力的有质量对应物。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索D0-膜（有质量IIA型超粒子）的严格理论表述，填补其在超扭量方法中的空白，并建立与旋量动框架表述之间的桥梁。

Method: 采用受约束的OSp(32|1)超扭量（supertwistor）十六重态（haxadecuplet）作为基本变量，该构造与描述11维无质量超粒子（即M0-膜）的超扭量类似但不完全相同。通过约束超扭量表述推导其与旋量动框架（spinor moving frame）方法的关系，并采用两种不同的方法进行量子化。

Result: 成功建立了D0-膜的超扭量公式化表述，证明了该表述与旋量动框架方法的等价性。两种量子化方法得到的结果与旋量动框架表述的量子化结果一致，量子态谱对应于线性化IIA型超引力（linearized type IIA supergravity）的有质量对应物。

Conclusion: 超扭量方法为D0-膜提供了自洽的理论框架，其量子化结果揭示了D0-膜与IIA型超引力有质量模式之间的深层联系，为弦理论中膜动力学的研究提供了新视角。

Abstract: We develop the (super)twistor approach to D$0$-brane, which is the massive type IIA superparticle in ten dimensional spacetime. The basic variables are haxadecuplet of constrained $OSp(32|1)$ supertwistors similar but not identical to the ones which have been used for the description of 11D massless superparticle, also known as M$0$-brane. We show how the constrained supertwistor formulation is related to the spinor moving frame approach to D$0$-brane. We perform the quantization of the model by two different methods and discuss the relation of the results with the quantization of the spinor moving frame formulation of D$0$-brane. The quantum state spectrum describes the massive counterpart of the linearized type IIA supergravity.

</details>


### [134] [Sampling Triangulations and Calabi-Yau Threefolds with Autoregressive GNNs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27770)
*Nate MacFadden*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文提出 dualGNN——一种自回归消息传递图神经网络，用于对凸多面体的精细规则三角剖分（fine regular triangulations, FRTs）进行均匀采样。该模型基于三角剖分对偶图（dual graph）的推广，利用符号电路（signed circuits）这一来自定向拟阵论（oriented matroid theory）的组合不变量来编码规则性（regularity）。模型规模小（约9.2万参数），训练速度快（单GPU约7.5小时），在未见过多边形（N_pts ≤ 40）上实现了当前最优的均匀采样性能，并在弦论（string theory）中成功应用于Calabi-Yau三维流形的均匀采样，覆盖范围达到h^{1,1}=128，比此前方法提升一个数量级且模型小约1000倍。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 凸多面体的精细规则三角剖分（FRT）在组合几何、离散数学和理论物理（如弦论中Calabi-Yau流形的构造）中具有重要应用，但均匀采样FRT在计算上极具挑战性。现有方法要么缺乏均匀性保证，要么计算代价过高，难以扩展到大规模问题。本文旨在开发一种高效、可泛化且保证均匀性的FRT采样方法。

Method: 提出dualGNN，一种自回归消息传递图神经网络，操作在三角剖分对偶图（dual graph）的推广结构上，其中边由符号电路（signed circuits）标记，后者是来自定向拟阵论（oriented matroid theory）的组合不变量，被证明是刻画规则性（regularity）的充要条件。模型与多面体顶点数无关，且在保定向对称群（SL(d,Z) ⋉ Z^d）下具有不变性。通过引入特定的掩码（masking）过程，可在二维情况下保证每次生成结果都是精细三角剖分（fine triangulation）。

Result: 在未见过多边形（N_pts ≤ 40）上，dualGNN在所有测试的FRT采样器中均匀性最优；仅在一个多边形上训练的模型也能很好地泛化到其他多边形。模型参数约9.2万，在单张消费级GPU上训练约7.5小时，可在M1 MacBook Pro上无需修改直接运行。在弦论应用中，成功实现了Calabi-Yau三维流形在h^{1,1}=86下的均匀采样，并在h^{1,1}=128下与均匀性一致，覆盖范围比此前基于学习的方法提升一个数量级，模型规模小约1000倍。

Conclusion: dualGNN提供了一种高效、可泛化且均匀的FRT采样框架，其关键创新在于将对偶图与定向拟阵论（oriented matroid theory）中的符号电路（signed circuits）相结合，从而在保持模型紧凑性的同时实现了对规则性的精确刻画和均匀采样。该方法在弦论中展现了显著的实用价值，未来有望推广到更广泛的组合几何和离散数学问题。代码和预训练模型已开源。

Abstract: We introduce `dualGNN', an autoregressive message-passing GNN for sampling fine, regular triangulations (FRTs) of convex polytopes. dualGNN operates on a generalization of the dual graph of a triangulation, with edges labeled by `signed circuits' -- combinatorial invariants from oriented matroid theory which we show are both necessary and sufficient for exposing regularity. The model is independent of the number of points in the polytope and invariant under the polytope's orientation-preserving symmetries ($\mathrm{SL}(d,\mathbb{Z}) \ltimes \mathbb{Z}^d$). When implemented with a certain masking procedure, one can also guarantee that every rollout produces a fine triangulation (in $2$D). On unseen polygons with $N_\mathrm{pts} \leq 40$, dualGNN is the most uniform FRT sampler we tested, and even a model trained on a single polygon generalizes well to other polygons. The model is small ($\sim92$k parameters), trains in $\sim7.5$ hours on a single consumer GPU, and runs without modification on an M1 MacBook Pro. We apply dualGNN to string theory, uniformly sampling Calabi-Yau threefolds at $h^{1,1}=86$ and consistent with uniformity at $h^{1,1}=128$. This is an order of magnitude beyond previous learned methods with a model $\sim1000\times$ smaller. Code, training scripts, and pretrained models are available at https://github.com/natemacfadden/dualGNN .

</details>


### [135] [Revisiting boundary electromagnetic duality and edge modes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27870)
*Keito Shimizu,Sotaro Sugishita*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该论文重新审视了带有限空间边界（finite spatial boundary）的四维麦克斯韦理论（Maxwell theory）和量子电动力学（QED）中的电、磁表面荷（surface charges）与边缘模式（edge modes），通过S-wall实现电磁对偶（electromagnetic duality），澄清了表面荷的对偶结构。研究表明，标准Neumann和Dirichlet边界条件下的大规范变换（large gauge transformations）及边缘模式变换属于规范冗余（gauge redundancies），而非物理边界对称性；而对于修正边界条件，大规范变换可成为由拓扑面算子（topological surface operators）生成的物理边界对称性，边缘模式也可变为物理的。论文还构造了这些修正边界条件的电磁对偶新边界条件。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究对带边界的量子场论中表面荷与边缘模式的对偶结构理解尚不清晰，大规范变换在不同边界条件下的物理本质（是规范冗余还是真实物理对称性）存在争议。本文旨在通过电磁对偶（如S-wall）统一澄清这些问题。

Method: 作者在四维Maxwell理论和QED中引入有限空间边界，利用S-wall（电磁对偶的实现工具）分析表面荷的对偶结构；分别考察标准Neumann/Dirichlet边界条件与修正边界条件下的大规范变换行为，并借助拓扑面算子与Wilson/'t Hooft环（Wilson or 't Hooft loops）的边界插入进行解释。

Result: 标准Neumann和Dirichlet边界条件下，大规范变换及对应的边缘模式位移属于规范冗余而非物理对称性；奇异大规范变换（singular large gauge transformations）可视为在边界上插入Wilson环或't Hooft环。在修正边界条件下，大规范变换可成为由拓扑面算子生成的物理边界对称性，边缘模式也具有物理意义。此外，作者构造了修正边界条件的电磁对偶新边界条件。

Conclusion: 边界条件的选取决定了大规范变换与边缘模式的物理性质：标准条件下它们为规范冗余，修正条件下则变为真实的物理对称性和物理模式。电磁对偶在统一理解这些现象中起关键作用，新构造的对偶边界条件进一步丰富了边界对称性的图像。

Abstract: We revisit electric and magnetic surface charges and edge modes in four-dimensional Maxwell theory and QED on a spacetime with a finite spatial boundary. Using the S-wall, which implements electromagnetic duality, we clarify the dual structure of surface charges. We show that, for the standard Neumann and Dirichlet boundary conditions, large gauge transformations and the corresponding shifts of edge modes are gauge redundancies rather than physical boundary symmetries. We also consider singular large gauge transformations and interpret them as insertions of Wilson or 't Hooft loops on the boundary. For modified boundary conditions, we show that large gauge transformations can become genuine physical boundary symmetries generated by topological surface operators, and that the corresponding edge modes can become physical. We further construct new boundary conditions that are electromagnetic duals of the modified boundary conditions.

</details>


### [136] [Worldline Higher Spin Gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27956)
*Minkyeu Cho,Euihun Joung,Taehwan Oh,Tung Tran*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于扭量（twistor）作用的AdS₄中高自旋引力（higher-spin gravity, HSG）的世界线（worldline）表述。该模型具有自然的双线（double-line）诠释，类似于弦理论中弦的拼接，并以此构建了所有无质量高自旋场的顶点算符（vertex operators），通过世界线路径积分计算了A型和B型HSG的n点关联函数，其在边界极限下重现了自由玻色子和自由费米子矢量模型的高自旋流关联函数。论文还讨论了该世界线理论嵌入泊松西格玛模型（Poisson sigma model）的若干推广。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 高自旋引力缺乏一个简洁且具有几何直观性的世界线或世界面（worldsheet）表述，现有框架难以系统处理相互作用顶点与关联函数的构造。

Method: 基于扭量作用提出AdS₄中HSG的世界线表述；通过双线诠释为相互作用顶点提供几何规则，构建满足Bargmann-Wigner方程的AdS协变顶点算符，并利用世界线路径积分计算n点关联函数；进一步将世界线理论嵌入泊松西格玛模型以赋予双线结构几何起源。

Result: 构建了所有无质量高自旋场的AdS协变顶点算符；计算了A型和B型HSG的n点关联函数；在边界极限下，这些关联函数再现了自由玻色子和自由费米子矢量模型的高自旋流关联函数。

Conclusion: 该工作为HSG提供了类似于弦理论的世界线表述，建立了HSG与矢量模型之间更系统的对应关系，并展示了进一步向世界面表述发展的可能路径（包括分数膜（fractional branes）、圈展开（loop expansion）、无定向投影（unoriented projection）等）。

Abstract: We propose a worldline formulation of higher-spin gravity (HSG) in $\mathrm{AdS}_4$, based on a simple twistor action. Taken at face value, the model describes only the free propagation of massless higher-spin fields. The central observation of this work is that the model admits a natural double-line interpretation, which supplies a geometric prescription for gluing worldlines at interaction vertices, in close parallel with the joining of strings in string theory. Building on this picture, we construct $\mathrm{AdS}$-covariant vertex operators for all massless higher-spin fields, show that they satisfy the Bargmann-Wigner equations, and use them to compute the n-point correlation functions of type-A and type-B HSG as worldline path integrals of these vertex operators. In the boundary limit these correlators reproduce the higher-spin current correlators of free boson and free fermion vector models. We further discuss the embedding of the worldline theory into Poisson sigma model, where the doubled-line structure acquires a geometric origin as the two edges of an open string worldsheet, together with several consequences of this enlarged framework -- fractional branes, loop expansion, unoriented projection, and the prospect of a worldsheet formulation of HSG.

### [138] [The effective gravitational action of a massless chiral fermion and the absence of parity-odd contributions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28045)
*J. Anero,Carmelo P. Martin*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文通过BPHZL重整化方案证明，四维闵可夫斯基时空中左手无质量费米子与引力子背景场耦合时，在引力子场数展开至四阶下，重整化引力有效作用量（renormalized gravitational effective action）中不存在奇宇称（parity-odd）贡献。此外，该有效作用量等于狄拉克费米子非手性耦合引力的相应作用量的一半，且外尔反常（Weyl anomaly）纯为偶宇称（parity-even），其值也为狄拉克费米子情形的一半。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究量子无质量左手费米子在引力背景下的宇称性质，特别是验证重整化有效作用量中是否存在奇宇称项，这是理解手征费米子（chiral fermion）与引力相互作用中宇称破坏可能性的核心问题。

Method: 采用BPHZL重整化方案（BPHZL renormalization scheme）对四维闵可夫斯基时空上左手无质量费米子与引力子场h_{μν}的量子场论进行微扰分析，在引力子场数展开至四阶的层次上系统检查奇宇称贡献的存在性。

Result: 在引力子场数展开至四阶时，重整化引力有效作用量中无奇宇称贡献；该有效作用量模去紫外有限微分同胚不变偶宇称抵消项后，等于狄拉克费米子非手性耦合引力的相应作用量的一半；外尔反常纯为偶宇称，其值为狄拉克费米子情形的一半。

Conclusion: 在所述微扰阶数下，左手费米子与引力耦合不产生宇称破坏的有限量子效应，且其有效作用量及外尔反常均可由狄拉克费米子情形缩半得到，表明手征性在引力背景下的量子效应受到强对称性约束。

Abstract: We consider the field theory of a quantum massless left handed fermion coupled to a background graviton field, $h_{μν}$, on four-dimensional Minkowski spacetime. By using the BPHZL renormalization scheme, we prove that, up to order four in the number of graviton fields, there are no parity-odd contributions to the renormalized gravitational effective action. As a side result, we show that, modulo arbitrary UV finite diffeomorphism invariant parity-even counterterms, the gravitational effective action in question is equal, up to order four in the number of graviton fields, to half the corresponding gravitational action for a Dirac fermion non-chirally coupled to gravity. Also as a side result, we conclude the the Weyl anomaly is purely parity-even and that its value is half the value of the Weyl anomaly for a Dirac fermion non-chirally coupled to gravity.

### [139] [Fermionic Bubble Loop in Cosmological Collider Revisited: Exact signals from spectral and Mellin-Barnes methods](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28054)
*Shuntaro Aoki,Zhehan Qin,Masahide Yamaguchi,Yuhang Zhu*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文针对宇宙学 collider 物理中费米子气泡圈图（fermionic bubble loop）对信号贡献的计算难题，发展了两套解析方法（谱分解法与梅林-巴恩斯表示法），精确求解了任意耦合下的费米子双圈信号，并发现 Yukawa 相互作用下对应的双谱（bispectrum）信号严格为零。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 费米子自由度是宇宙学 collider (cosmological collider) 物理的关键要素，且受标准模型之外诸多现象学模型的驱动，但由于圈图计算困难，其信号尚未被充分探索。本文旨在精确计算费米子气泡圈图对宇宙学 collider 信号的贡献。

Method: 发展了两套平行的解析方法：第一套方法类似于谱分解（spectral decomposition），基于传播子乘积的恒等式，将气泡信号转化为无穷级数的树图交换信号之和；第二套方法基于梅林-巴恩斯表示（Mellin-Barnes representation），通过不同极点族的留数重构结果。此外还证明了费米子气泡可通过适当的微分算符作用从标量气泡生成。

Result: 对于费米子与暴胀子（inflaton）之间的 Yukawa 相互作用，对应的双谱（bispectrum）信号严格为零；通过谱分解方法，该消失现象可追溯至关联树图对应的场重定义（field redefinition）。

Conclusion: 提供了任意耦合下费米子气泡圈图的精确解析解，两套方法的一致性构成了对结果的非平凡验证，并揭示了 Yukawa 类型宇宙学 collider 信号的消失机制。

Abstract: Fermionic degrees of freedom are essential ingredients in cosmological collider physics and are well motivated by many phenomenological models beyond the Standard Model, but their signals remain largely unexplored due to the difficulty of computing loop diagrams. In this work, we ask how fermionic bubble loops contribute to cosmological collider signals and provide an exact answer for arbitrary couplings. We develop two parallel analytical methods whose agreement provides a non-trivial check of the result. The first method is similar in spirit to spectral decomposition and is built directly from an identity for the product of propagators, which turns the bubble signal into an infinite sum of tree-level exchange signals. The second method is based on the Mellin-Barnes representation, where the result is reconstructed from the residues of distinct families of poles. We also show that the fermionic bubble can be generated from the scalar bubble by the action of appropriate differential operators. As a phenomenologically important application, we consider Yukawa interactions between fermions and the inflaton, finding that the resulting bispectrum signal vanishes identically. Through the spectral decomposition, this vanishing can be traced to a field redefinition of the associated tree-level counterparts.

Abstract: We study the modular symmetry in magnetized compactifications. The zero-modes with different Scherk-Schwarz phases transform each other. A generic model does not include modes with all the Scherk-Schwarz phases. Incomplete multiplet representations appear. Thus, the modular symmetry is violated as group-like symmetry. However, the modular symmetry still controls coupling terms in those models. Modular forms of the full symmetry appear as coupling constants.

### [141] [Hilbert Space and Defect Hilbert Spaces Associated with Categorical Symmetries](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28485)

Conclusion: 线算子的卷积作用与已知的Verlinde公式以及半经典S-核存在深刻对应关系，表明该量子力学方法能够统一地处理不同规范群下的模数据，为理解线算子与拓扑量子场论结构提供了系统性框架。

Abstract: We present a quantum mechanical approach to understanding the Hilbert space and the defect Hilbert spaces associated with line operators of BF theory combined with level-$k$ Chern-Simons theory. The defect Hilbert spaces are closely related to the category of $*$-representations of the $C^*$-algebra of the compactly supported sections of the Fell line bundle over the conjugation action groupoid $G//_{\mathrm Ad} G$, and the structure of this category and the groupoid action on the objects of this category is interpreted quantum mechanically. We show that the action of the line operators on the Hilbert space of the $BF+kCS$ TQFT is given concretely by a convolution between the kernels that represent the line operators, and that the codimension-$2$ twist and the codimension-$1$ prequantum line bundle arise as two transgressions of the same universal level $k\in H^4(BG,\mathbb{Z})$. For finite gauge group, the resulting convolution-eigenvalue formula is identified with the Verlinde formula for the (twisted) Drinfeld double $D^ω(G)$ via an explicit phase-by-phase match with the known finite modular data. For compact Lie group, the convolution-kernel eigenvalues coincide in the regular sector with the semiclassical Hopf-link $S$-kernel, identifying two complementary derivations of the same modular data.

### [142] [Radiative Correction to the Casimir Energy for Massive Scalar Field in The Network](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28519)
*M. A. Valuyan*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文计算了在由三条边连接于单一中心结点构成的网络（network）上，受φ⁴相互作用支配的有质量洛伦兹破缺标量场（massive Lorentz-violating scalar field）的卡西米尔能量（Casimir energy）的领头阶和二阶辐射修正（radiative corrections）。研究采用位置依赖的抵消项（position-dependent counterterms）进行重整化，并结合箱截断方案（box subtraction scheme）与截断正则化（cutoff regularization）消除真空能发散。结果表明，无论是否存在洛伦兹破缺效应，领头阶和一阶卡西米尔能量均为负值，符合一般物理预期。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 扩展卡西米尔效应研究至网络几何结构，考察洛伦兹破缺（Lorentz violation）和有质量标量场对卡西米尔能量的辐射修正影响，并验证位置依赖的抵消项在边界条件存在时重整化方案的有效性。

Method: 在由三条边连接于单一中心结点构成的网络上，定义1+1维有质量洛伦兹破缺标量场，并施加狄利克雷边界条件（Dirichlet boundary conditions）于各边的外端。采用位置依赖的抵消项系统地进行重整化，将边界条件影响纳入重整化程序；同时运用箱截断方案与截断正则化消除真空能发散，计算领头阶和一阶辐射修正。

Result: 领头阶和一阶卡西米尔能量均为负值，无论是否引入洛伦兹破缺效应，且结果符合一般物理预期。

Conclusion: 该工作验证了在网络几何结构下，使用位置依赖的抵消项计算卡西米尔能量辐射修正的可行性，并表明洛伦兹破缺效应在此情形下不改变卡西米尔能量的负定性。

Abstract: In this paper, we compute the leading-order and first-order radiative corrections to the Casimir energy of a massive Lorentz-violating scalar field governed by a $φ^4$ interaction on a network. For simplicity, the network is chosen to consist of three edges connected at a single central junction, with the scalar field defined in 1+1 dimensions on each edge. Dirichlet boundary conditions are imposed at the outer ends of the edges, thereby confining the field on the network. Beyond addressing the massive case of a Lorentz-violating scalar field, a key novelty of this work lies in the calculation of the radiative corrections to the Casimir energy using position-dependent counterterms. These counterterms emerge from a systematic renormalization program that consistently incorporates the effects of boundary conditions into the renormalization procedure. To eliminate divergences arising from vacuum energy contributions, we employ the box subtraction scheme in conjunction with cutoff regularization. Our results show that both the leading-order and first-order Casimir energies are negative, regardless of the presence or absence of Lorentz-violating effects, and are in agreement with general physical expectations.

</details>


### [143] [Non-integral geometry: additional term $f_A$ as a regularizing term](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28670)
*I. V. Anikin*

Main category: hep-th

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决传统积分几何（integral geometry）方法中积分测度对称性破缺带来的问题，并改进图像重建过程。

Method: 基于非整数几何理论，引入非对称积分测度（非不变测度），推导出维数无关的通用逆算子（universal inverse operator），相比积分几何方法增加了复数形式的附加贡献项。

Conclusion: 非整数几何框架下的复数积分测度扩展可有效改善图像重建，附加项 $f_A$ 作为正则化项可消除重建中的复数奇异性。

Abstract: In the present paper, we first describe the principal basis of non-integral geometry. In turn, the non-symmetric integration measure (the non-invariant measure) leads to the complex form of the universal, dimension-independent inverse operator with the additional contributions compared to the methods of integral geometry. The additional term with the complex integration measure serves to the extension that improves the image reconstruction procedure. Then, we proof that this additional term $f_A$ in the universal inverse Radon transforms plays a role of the regularizing contribution. ### [144] [Krylov complexity has it all](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28681)
*Wolfgang Mück*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文证明Krylov复杂度（Krylov complexity）包含量子算符动力学的全部信息，与Lanczos系数（Lanczos coefficients）、返回振幅（return amplitude）和谱密度（spectral density）等物理量在信息上等价，并阐明了Krylov复杂度与扩展复杂度（spread complexity）之间的本质区别。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子算符动力学（quantum operator dynamics）需要一种完整的描述方式。已有多个等价量可用于此目的，但Krylov复杂度是否同样具有这种完备性尚未被严格证明，需要建立其与其他标准量之间的等价关系。

Method: 构造了一个显式递归算法（explicit recursive algorithm），从Krylov复杂度在t=0附近的泰勒展开（Taylor expansion）出发，反向计算Lanczos系数，从而证明两者之间的信息等价性。

Result: 成功建立了从Krylov复杂度的短时泰勒展开到Lanczos系数的递归映射，从而证明了Krylov复杂度与Lanczos系数、返回振幅、谱密度在信息上的完全等价。此外，指出扩展复杂度由于缺乏类似的结构，无法在不引入额外动力学输入的前提下建立类似的递归算法。

Conclusion: Krylov复杂度可以作为量子系统中算符演化的完全刻画（complete characterization），这一结果为将该量作为量子动力学的统一描述工具提供了“原理性证明”（proof of principle）。

Abstract: This paper establishes that Krylov complexity contains the entire information about the dynamics of a quantum operator, extending the list of equivalent quantities that can serve this purpose, such as the Lanczos coefficients, the return amplitude, and the spectral density. To demonstrate this equivalence, an explicit recursive algorithm is constructed to calculate Lanczos coefficients from the Taylor expansion of the Krylov complexity around $t=0$. Furthermore, the paper discusses the distinction between Krylov and spread complexity, clarifying why a similar recursive algorithm cannot exist for the latter without additional dynamical input. These results provide a ``proof of principle'' for using Krylov complexity as a complete characterization of operator evolution in quantum systems.

</details>


### [145] [Complex BPS Black Holes in AdS$_3\times S^3$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28737)
*Finn Larsen,Kartik Sharma*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文证明超对称指标的正确引力表示是光滑复解（smooth complex solution），而非洛伦兹BPS黑洞的朴素欧几里得延拓。作者通过两种独立途径——四维双中心BPS解带有复偶极荷（complex dipole charges）以及六维黑弦施加BPS关系——构造了STU模型中具有AdS₃×S³边界条件的此类鞍点，并得到相同有限温度BTZ×S³几何。光滑性与周期性条件恰好是全局良定义超对称与超对称指标热力学势所必需的条件。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 超对称指标的超对称（supersymmetric index）对应于有限温度下的配分函数，其引力构造需要正确的鞍点几何。传统的洛伦兹BPS黑洞的朴素欧几里得延续无法给出正确结果，因此需要寻找光滑复解作为超对称指标的引力表示。

Method: 包括两条独立构造路径：一是从四维双中心（two-center）BPS解出发，引入复偶极荷；二是从六维黑弦（black string）出发，在守恒荷之间施加BPS关系。两者最终都得到相同的有限温度BTZ×S³几何。在此基础上分析了光滑性条件（smoothness conditions）与周期性条件（periodicity conditions）。

Result: 两种独立方法得到了相同的有限温度BTZ×S³几何；求解得到的光滑性与周期性条件恰好是全局良定义超对称（globally well-defined supersymmetry）以及超对称指标热力学势所要求的条件。

Conclusion: 超对称指标的正确引力表示是光滑复解，而非洛伦兹BPS黑洞的朴素欧几里得延续。研究为STU模型中的AdS₃×S³边界条件提供了具体构造，并明确了光滑解所需满足的物理条件。

Abstract: The correct gravitational representation of the supersymmetric index is a smooth complex solution, rather than the naïve Euclidean continuation of the Lorentizan BPS black hole. We construct such saddles for black holes with \(\mathrm{AdS}_3\times S^3\) boundary conditions in the STU model. We arrive at the same finite-temperature BTZ \(\times S^3\) geometries in two independent ways: from two-center four-dimensional BPS solutions with complex dipole charges, and from six-dimensional black strings after imposing the BPS relation among conserved charges. We analyze the resulting smoothness and periodicity conditions and show that they are precisely those required for globally well-defined supersymmetry and for the thermodynamic potentials of the supersymmetric index.

### [146] [Filtering out Erratic Observables: Wormholes from Gauging Nonlocal Symmetries](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28748)
*Qi-Feng Wu*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文在(2+1)维引力中证明，单边边界引力子（boundary gravitons）的观测子代数具有非平凡的中心，需通过单值数据（monodromy data）的观测子代数完成完备化，后者可视为单边黑洞的有效描述。通过引入正性限制（positivity restriction）过滤掉不规则的巨大N（large-N）行为，进而规范非局域对称性（nonlocal symmetries）可等价地消除这些不规则可观测量。对于两个CFT，规范非局域对称性后保留的希尔伯特子空间描述虫洞（wormholes），其配分函数表现为量子门（quantum gates）的系综平均，其中虫洞项来自两个CFT不规则可观测量的关联。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解虫洞（wormhole）对引力路径积分的贡献如何解释为对偶共形场论（CFT）中不规则巨大N（large-N）行为之间的平滑残余关联。

Method: 基于渐近对称性（asymptotic symmetries）自举出一个一般的泊松括号（Poisson bracket）来构造边界引力子的完备化；通过引入正性限制过滤不规则巨大N行为；通过规范非局域对称性在量子层面消除不规则可观测量。

Result: 单边边界引力子的观测子代数存在非平凡的中心；其交换子由单值数据的观测子代数给出，后者解释为单边黑洞的有效描述；规范非局域对称性等价于过滤不规则可观测量；对于两个CFT，过滤后的配分函数是纠缠两个CFT单值自由度的量子门的系综平均；不规则可观测量的关联保留为虫洞项。

Conclusion: 虫洞贡献可解释为对偶CFT中不规则巨大N行为的残余关联；规范非局域对称性可系统地移除不规则的巨大N行为，并揭示虫洞作为系综平均的结构。

Abstract: The wormhole contribution to the gravitational path integral may be interpreted as smooth remnant of correlations among the erratic large-$N$ behaviors of dual CFTs. In this work, we investigate this idea in (2+1)-dimensional gravity. We show that one-sided boundary gravitons are intrinsically incomplete in the sense that the associated observable algebra has a nontrivial center regardless of choices of boundary conditions. Based on asymptotic symmetries, we bootstrap a general Poisson bracket to construct completions of the boundary gravitons. In the simplest completion, the commutant of the boundary graviton observable algebra is given by an observable algebra of monodromy data which we interpret as an effective description of one-sided black holes. We show that, to describe Lorentzian multi-boundary wormholes, only the monodromy data with a positivity restriction is needed. The positivity restriction results in emergent erratic large-$N$ behaviors for some observables. We filter out the erratic observables by restricting to a subspace on which they act trivially. The monodromy observables generate nonlocal symmetries lack of corresponding local currents. We show that gauging the nonlocal symmetries is equivalent to filtering out the erratic observables. For one CFT, gauging the nonlocal symmetries at the quantum level removes all black hole states. Filtering the partition function of CFTs leads to an apparent ensemble averaging. For two CFTs, a Hilbert subspace describing wormholes survives after gauging global part of the nonlocal symmetries. The filtered partition function of the two CFTs is an ensemble average over quantum gates entangling the monodromy degrees of freedom the two CFTs. The correlation between the erratic observables of the two CFTs is preserved, which contributes to the filtered partition function as a wormhole term.

</details>


### [147] [Inflation with vector fields revisited: non-Gaussianities](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28752)
*Chong-Bin Chen*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文通过参数 $h$（矢量场动能与标量场动能之比）系统研究了动能耦合矢量场暴胀（inflation）的双谱（bispectrum）。在强矢量区域（$h\gg1$）推导了低能有效场论（low-energy effective field theory, EFT），发现曲率模的虚数声速会导致视界交叉前的瞬态增长，并识别出多种新的双谱信号（标度律分别为 $h^3$、$h^2$ 和 $h$），这些信号间的竞争使得双谱能够区分各向同性背景下的矢量场暴胀动力学。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 已有的研究主要关注 $h\ll1$ 弱矢量区域，其中矢量场在视界外持续转移产生增强的局部型（local-type）贡献（标度为 $h^2 N_K^3$）。本文的核心动机是填补 $h\gg1$ 强矢量区域的空白，理解该区域的双谱特征，并探究矢量场暴胀是否能在完全各向同性的背景下通过非高斯性特征被区分出来。

Method: 作者以参数 $h$ 组织动力学分析，在强矢量区域（$h\gg1$）对系统的双谱进行解析评估，并推导了适用于大 $h$ 区域的低能有效场论（EFT）。在 $h\gg1$ 条件下，通过积掉重熵扰动（entropic perturbation），将系统约化为单一的曲率模，并分析了该模的声速特性及视界交叉前的动力学行为。

Result: 对于 $h\gg1$，曲率模具有虚数声速（imaginary sound speed），导致其在视界交叉前经历瞬态增长（transient growth）。与 $h\ll1$ 区域（产生标度为 $h^2 N_K^3$ 的局部型信号）不同，强矢量区域出现多种新双谱信号：标度为 $h^3$ 的扁平增强（flattened-enhanced）信号（已知）、标度为 $h^2$ 的扁平增强信号（新发现），以及标度为 $h$ 的显著局部投影（local projection）信号。这些信号的竞争导致：中等 $h$ 时局部型占主导，较大 $h$ 时扁平型占主导。

Conclusion: 即使暴胀背景完全各向同性（exactly isotropic），双谱的标度行为和形状特征（局部型与扁平型的竞争）仍可有效区分矢量场支持的暴胀动力学。这一发现拓展了对矢量场暴胀非高斯性特征的理解，为从宇宙微波背景（cosmic microwave background, CMB）和大尺度结构数据中识别此类模型提供了观测窗口。

Abstract: We revisit the resulting bispectrum of inflation with kinetic-coupled vector fields by organizing the dynamics in terms of $h$, which measures the vector kinetic contribution relative to that of the scalar field. We evaluate the bispectrum in the strong-vector regime and derive a low-energy effective field theory (EFT) for the large-$h$ regime. For $h\gg1$, the entropic perturbation becomes heavy and can be integrated out; the remaining curvature mode has an imaginary sound speed and undergoes transient growth before horizon crossing. In contrast to $h\ll1$ regime, where transfer from the vector sector persists outside the horizon and produces a local-type contribution enhanced as $h^2N_K^3$, we find that in addition to the known flattened-enhanced signals scaling as $h^3$, a flattened-enhanced signal scaling as $h^2$ and a pronounced local projection scaling as $h$. Their competition yields a local-dominated signal for intermediate $h$ and a flattened-dominated signal at larger $h$. The bispectrum therefore distinguishes vector-supported inflationary dynamics even for an exactly isotropic background.

</details>


### [148] [GR from RG, $2d$ Example: JT-Gravity Induced from Renormalization Group Flow](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28753)
*M. M. Sheikh-Jabbari,V. Taghiloo*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文在“GR from RG”纲领框架下，展示了二维引力如何从全息重整化群（holographic RG）流动中涌现。以三维爱因斯坦-AdS引力为对偶的二维共形场论（2d CFT）为出发点，研究表明任意能量标度下的RG修正作用量包含一个二维标量-张量引力理论，其中最简单情形下诱导出Jackiw-Teitelboim（JT）引力。在Fefferman-Graham极限下，标准T\bar{T}形变作为特例被恢复。该结果在非Fefferman-Graham规范下为有限截断处的JT引力提供了第一性原理推导。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在全息对偶（holographic duality）框架下，理解有限截断（finite cutoff）处引力理论的涌现机制是一个核心问题。本文旨在通过"GR from RG"纲领，从第一性原理出发，论证二维引力（特别是JT引力）如何作为全息重整化群流动的内在体现自然产生。

Method: 选取一个具有三维全息描述（纯爱因斯坦-AdS₃引力）的通用二维共形场论（2d CFT）。研究其全息RG流（holographic RG flow），分析作用量在不同能量标度下的重整化群（renormalization group, RG）修正形式，并在非Fefferman-Graham规范（non-Fefferman-Graham gauge）下推导RG诱导的引力理论结构。

Result: RG修正后的作用量包含一个二维标量-张量引力理论（scalar-tensor gravity theory），最简单情形下诱导出Jackiw-Teitelboim（JT）引力，其中体径向往返函数（radial lapse function）充当了JT引力的动态膨胀子场（dynamical dilaton field）。标准T\bar{T}形变在Fefferman-Graham极限（Fefferman-Graham limit，即lapse固定时）作为特例恢复。该结果在全息重整化下具有一致性，且可推广到单参数族边界条件。

Conclusion: 本文为有限截断处的JT引力提供了第一性原理推导（first-principles derivation），表明其本质上是全息RG流在非Fefferman-Graham规范下的内在表现形式。研究确立了RG诱导引力图景的鲁棒性。

Abstract: We demonstrate how the two-dimensional gravity emerges within ``GR from RG'' program initiated in \cite{Adami:2025pqr, Sheikh-Jabbari:2026uol}. To achieve this, we consider a generic 2d CFT with a 3d holographic description, which we assume to be well-described by pure Einstein-AdS$_3$ gravity in the bulk. We study the holographic RG flow for the 2d CFT action and show that the renormalization group (RG) corrected action at an arbitrary energy scale contains a 2d scalar-tensor gravity theory. In the simplest case, the flow induces Jackiw-Teitelboim (JT) gravity, where the bulk radial lapse function seeds the dynamical dilaton field of the JT gravity. We show that the standard T$\bar{\text{T}}$ deformation of the 2d CFT is recovered as a special case in the Fefferman-Graham limit where the lapse is fixed. We further establish the robustness of the RG induced gravity picture by verifying its consistency under holographic renormalization and by generalizing the result to a one-parameter family of boundary conditions. Our results provide a first-principles derivation of the JT gravity at a finite cutoff as an intrinsic manifestation of the holographic RG flow in a non-Fefferman-Graham gauge

</details>

### [149] [AtomComposer: Discovering Chemical Space from First Principles with Reinforcement Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28287)
*Bjarke Hastrup,Francois Cornet,Tejs Vegge,Arghya Bhowmik*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出AtomComposer，一种无需预训练数据的自引导智能体（self-guided agent），通过在线强化学习（online reinforcement learning）自主构建化学计量约束下的有效3D异构体，能够在未见过的化学式上发现比现有基线方法多一个数量级的有效异构体。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有分子生成模型依赖大规模预构建数据集，引入了数据偏差并限制了新颖化学空间的探索；同时缺乏一种无需预训练、能自主映射未知化学空间的方法。

Method: 提出AtomComposer智能体，采用在线强化学习（online reinforcement learning）进行训练，无需任何预训练数据；构建多组分训练方案（multi-composition training scheme），基于能量和有效性奖励（energy- and validity-based rewards）引导智能体在多种化学组成上实现广泛泛化。

Result: 在未见过的测试化学式上，AtomComposer发现的有效异构体数量比现有的单组分强化学习基线方法（使用每步能量奖励）高出最多一个数量级。

Conclusion: 在线强化学习是一种可扩展的、从零开始探索化学构型空间（chemical configuration space）的强大范式，能够有效克服预训练数据带来的偏差。

Abstract: Discovering novel stable molecules without training data remains a grand scientific challenge. Current molecular generative models are trained on large, pre-curated datasets, which introduce biases and limit exploration of novel chemistry. In contrast, we propose a new paradigm: autonomous, generalized agents capable of mapping vast, unknown chemical spaces without any pretraining. For the first time, we present AtomComposer, a self-guided agent that autonomously constructs valid 3D isomers under stoichiometric constraints and is trained exclusively online using reinforcement learning. Unlike existing approaches that generally overfit to a specific chemical formula, we establish a multi-composition training scheme that enables a broad generalization across diverse chemistry, guided by energy- and validity-based rewards. Our agent can discover up to an order of magnitude more valid isomers on unseen test formulas than existing single-composition reinforcement-learning baselines trained with per-step energy rewards. These results fulfill the promise of online reinforcement learning as a powerful paradigm for scalable, from-scratch exploration of chemical configuration space.

### [150] [LEIA: Learned Environment for Interactive Architected Materials](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28368)
*Haiqian Yang,Yuan Cao,Markus J. Buehler*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出LEIA，一种面向超构材料（architected materials）的交互式世界模型（world model），能够实时响应工程师施加的边界条件并生成变形与应力场；同时引入MicroPlate基准测试，验证LEIA在微观结构显式与隐式建模两种机制下的性能，并展示其在快速代理引导的超构材料设计搜索中的应用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有世界模型已在游戏环境交互与机器人操作中取得进展，但物理工程领域仍难以应用：真实材料表现出非线性本构关系（nonlinear constitutive laws）、历史依赖的内部状态、惯性动力学以及跨多尺度的层级结构。作者旨在构建一个能够处理上述复杂性的学习环境，用于超构材料的实时交互式仿真与设计。

Method: LEIA采用自回归生成（autoregressive generation）方式，逐步响应工程师指定的边界条件（boundary conditions），实时输出变形场与应力场。模型支持大型三维非结构化网格（unstructured meshes）。作者还提出MicroPlate基准测试，包含两种微结构建模机制的板状超构材料数据集：一是通过三维几何显式解析微结构的点阵（architected lattices），二是通过内部自由度隐式建模微结构变化的均质板（homogeneous plate）。

Result: 在MicroPlate基准上，LEIA与四种基线方法在两种微结构建模机制下进行了评估；结果表明LEIA能够高效生成候选设计并对其进行排序（ranking），用于快速代理引导的超构材料新设计搜索，其中应力精确的候选排序结果经有限元（finite element）真实验证。

Conclusion: LEIA作为一种面向超构材料的世界模型，成功将交互式仿真能力拓展到物理工程领域，在支持复杂几何与非线性物理的同时，为超构材料的快速设计优化提供了有效代理（surrogate）工具。

Abstract: World models have enabled interactive exploration of game environments and robotic manipulation, but physical engineering remains beyond their reach: real materials exhibit nonlinear constitutive laws, carry history-dependent internal state, undergo inertial dynamics, and may possess hierarchical structures spanning multiple length scales. We present LEIA (Learned Environment for Interactive Architected materials), a world model that lets engineers apply boundary conditions step by step and observe the resulting deformation and stress fields in real time. LEIA handles large three-dimensional unstructured meshes and generates autoregressive responses to user-specified loading. We introduce MicroPlate, a benchmark of architected plates spanning two regimes of microstructure modeling: architected lattices that resolve microstructure explicitly through three-dimensional geometry, and a homogeneous plate where microstructural change is modeled implicitly through internal degrees of freedom. MicroPlate is used to assess LEIA alongside four baseline methods across both regimes. Finally, we demonstrate that LEIA enables efficient candidate generation and ranking for fast surrogate-guided search for de novo designs of architected materials, with stress-accurate candidate ranking validated by finite element ground truth.

</details>


<div id='astro-ph.GA'></div>

# astro-ph.GA [[Back]](#toc)

### [151] [Transient axion streams from disrupted miniclusters](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28005)
*Luca Visinelli,Momchil Naydenov*

Main category: astro-ph.GA

TL;DR: 本文通过蒙特卡洛（Monte Carlo）模拟与示踪粒子重构相结合的方法，研究了银河系晕中轴子微团簇（axion minicluster）因恒星潮汐瓦解（tidal disruption）形成的轴子流（axion stream）的演化。结果表明，剥离物质的动能通常超过其自引力束缚能，导致流密度在星系时间尺度上可衰减约10⁻⁹量级，因此太阳附近稳态稠密流极为稀少；探测事件主要由罕见的近时、近距离瓦解主导。尽管密度极低，流仍保持动力学冷（dynamically cold），其线宽（linewidth）远窄于当前射电寻迹实验（haloscope）的腔体带宽。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解轴子微团簇因恒星飞掠（stellar flyby）潮汐瓦解后形成的轴子流的形成与演化过程，并评估此类亚结构对局域暗物质分布及直接探测实验的影响。

Method: 采用大规模蒙特卡洛（Monte Carlo）方法处理重复恒星飞掠，并结合示踪粒子重构（tracer reconstruction）技术追踪剥离碎屑的相空间演化。研究覆盖广泛的银心半径范围，分析不同轨道位置处流的形成与稀释行为。

Result: 剥离物质的动能通常超过其自引力束缚能，流的发展以各向异性自由膨胀和轨道剪切（orbital shear）为主，密度在星系演化时间尺度上可下降约10⁻⁹倍。在太阳半径处，仅有极小比例实现能在10年曝光时间内产生非零相遇概率，表明可观测流主要来自罕见近时事件。流仍保持动力学冷，线宽范围为Δν_stream~10⁻⁷–10¹ Hz，远低于当前射电寻迹实验腔体带宽。

Conclusion: 轴子微团簇潮汐瓦解产生的流在长时间尺度上高度稀释，难以形成持久的过密亚结构，但残存流的动力学冷特性使其线宽极窄，为未来更高分辨率的射电寻迹实验提供了独特探测窗口。

Abstract: We investigate the formation and evolution of axion streams generated by the tidal disruption of axion miniclusters through stellar encounters in the Milky Way halo. Combining a large-scale Monte Carlo treatment of repeated stellar flybys with a tracer reconstruction of the stripped debris, we follow the phase-space evolution of the streams across a broad range of galactocentric radii and assess their contribution to the local dark matter distribution. We find that the kinetic energy of the stripped debris typically exceeds its residual self-gravitational binding energy at formation, so that the subsequent evolution is dominated by anisotropic free expansion and orbital shear. As a result, stream densities can decrease by factors as large as $\sim10^{-9}$ over Galactic timescales, strongly suppressing the steady-state abundance of dense streams near the Solar circle. At the Solar radius, only a small fraction of realizations yields a nonzero encounter probability over a 10 year exposure, implying that observable streams are dominated by rare recent and nearby disruption events rather than by a persistent population of long-lived overdense substructure. Despite this rapid dilution, the streams remain dynamically cold and produce detector-frame linewidths many orders of magnitude narrower than the cavity bandwidths of current haloscope experiments. For representative haloscope configurations, we find characteristic stream linewidths in the range $Δν_{\rm stream}\sim10^{-7}-10^{1}\,{\rm Hz}$, while the corresponding Doppler drift remains well below the cavity response width.

</details>

### [152] [Surface Contact Approximation for Magneto-Thermal Finite Element Analysis of No-Insulation HTS Coils](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28574)
*Erik Schnaubelt,Louis Denis,Mariusz Wozniak,Julien Dular,Arjan Verweij*

Main category: physics.comp-ph

TL;DR: 本文针对无绝缘（NI）高温超导（HTS）线圈的匝间接触层（T2TCL），提出了一种磁热表面接触近似（SCA）方法，用于有限元分析。SCA 将薄体积接触层替换为基于接触电阻和热接触电导的表面弱形式，无需定义厚度，在保证精度的同时比传统的薄壳近似（TSA）更易用、更鲁棒。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 无绝缘（NI）高温超导（HTS）线圈中，电流可通过匝间接触层（T2TCL）局部旁路正常区域，因此需要准确模拟 T2TCL 的电热行为。现有薄壳近似（TSA）存在厚度选择困难与计算效率低下的问题。

Method: 提出磁热表面接触近似（SCA）方法，将其作为薄壳近似（TSA）的一种特例进行推导，忽略了 T2TCL 内的切向表面电流和涡流效应，将薄体积接触层替换为基于电接触电阻和热接触电导的表面弱形式。SCA 在开源有限元淬火模拟器的 Pancake3D 模块中实现。

Result: 通过瞬态磁热模拟验证，SCA 能准确再现相关的电磁和热行为。TSA 存在厚度与电阻率之间的权衡问题：厚度过大且电阻率过小会导致结果不准确，厚度过小且电阻率过大会增加求解难度和计算量。SCA 由于直接使用接触电阻和电导，无需定义厚度，更易用且鲁棒。

Conclusion: SCA 方法无需定义 T2TCL 厚度，避免了 TSA 中的厚度选择矛盾，在保持精度的前提下简化了建模流程，提高了计算鲁棒性和易用性。

Abstract: High-temperature superconducting (HTS) coated conductors (CCs) can be wound into no-insulation (NI) coils, in which electrical current can partially bypass local normal zones via turn-to-turn contact layers (T2TCLs). Accurate magneto-thermal simulation of such coils, therefore, requires an efficient representation of the electrical and thermal behavior of the T2TCLs. This paper introduces a magneto-thermal surface contact approximation (SCA) for finite element analysis of NI HTS coils. The formulation is derived as a special case of the more general thin shell approximation (TSA) by introducing suitable approximations such as negligible tangential surface currents and eddy-current effects inside the T2TCL. The resulting SCA formulation replaces the thin volumetric contact layer with a dedicated surface weak formulation based on the electric contact resistance and thermal contact conductance. In contrast, the TSA formulation requires the definition of electric resistivities and thermal conductivities as well as the thickness of the T2TCL. The SCA is implemented in the Pancake3D module of the free and open-source Finite Element Quench Simulator. It is verified through transient magneto-thermal simulations of a model NI pancake coil. Numerical results are compared against the established TSA formulation. The results show that the SCA accurately reproduces the relevant electromagnetic and thermal behavior. For the TSA, there is a trade-off between choosing large (potentially unphysical) thicknesses with low resistivities leading to inaccurate results, or small thicknesses with large resistivities making the linear system harder to solve, increasing the computational effort. In contrast, the SCA, thanks to using contact resistances and conductances directly without the necessity to define a thickness, is easy to use and robust.

</details>

### [153] [The BKT transition and surface tension differentiability](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28473)
*Thibault Durand,Piet Lammers*

Main category: math.PR

TL;DR: 本文证明二维XY模型的质量（mass）等于其对偶高度函数自由能在零斜率处的右导数，并给出了原点附近的均匀二次误差界；由此将大质量相精确刻画为角点（corner）区域，而BKT相的表面张力在零斜率处受二次函数界约束。证明结合了Kadanoff–Ceva对偶性、Ginibre不等式和适用于电缆高度函数的推动引理（pushing lemma，一种Russo–Seymour–Welsh型估计）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在二维XY模型与整数值高度函数（integer-valued height function）的对偶关系下，Berezinskii–Kosterlitz–Thouless（BKT）转变预期对应于表面张力（surface tension）中一个角点的消失；在退局域相（delocalised phase）中，其零斜率曲率应决定高斯自由场（Gaussian free field）的前因子。本文旨在严格建立这一对应关系。

Method: 证明方法结合了Kadanoff–Ceva对偶性（Kadanoff–Ceva duality）、Ginibre不等式（Ginibre's inequality），以及一个针对电缆高度函数（cable height function）的推动引理（pushing lemma，属于Russo–Seymour–Welsh型估计）。

Result: 证明了XY质量等于对偶高度函数自由能在零斜率处的右导数，并给出了原点附近的均匀二次误差界（uniform quadratic error bound）。由此得出：大质量相（massive phase）精确对应于角点区域（corner regime），而BKT相（BKT phase）的表面张力在零斜率处受二次函数界约束（quadratically bounded）。

Conclusion: 这一结果严格证实了在XY模型与高度函数的对偶框架下，BKT转变与表面张力角点消失之间的预期对应关系，并为退局域相中高斯自由场前因子的行为提供了量化刻画。

Abstract: Under the duality between the two-dimensional XY model and an integer-valued height function, the BKT transition is expected to correspond to the disappearance of a corner in the surface tension; in the delocalised phase, its zero-slope curvature should determine the Gaussian free field prefactor. We prove that the XY mass equals the right derivative at zero slope of the dual height function's free energy, with a uniform quadratic error bound near the origin. Thus the massive phase is exactly the corner regime, while in the BKT phase the surface tension is quadratically bounded at zero slope. The proof combines Kadanoff--Ceva duality, Ginibre's inequality, and a pushing lemma (an estimate of Russo--Seymour--Welsh type) for the cable height function.

### [154] [Convex order and faster transmission in first contact percolation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28766)
*Benedikt Jahnel,Jonas Köppl,Lukas Lüchtrath,Anh Duc Vu*

Main category: math.PR

TL;DR: 本文受首达渗流（first passage percolation）中时间常数的严格单调性标准启发，研究了点过程（point processes）的凸序（convex ordering）与首接触渗流（first contact percolation）中时间常数之间的关系。作者证明凸序能保证感染路径数量与存在性的单调性，但不足以确保感染渐近速度的严格单调性；为此提出了一种基于空概率（void probabilities）排序的准则，并在一维 $\mathbb{Z}$-平稳点过程体系中证明了速度增加。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 受首达渗流中时间常数严格单调性标准的启发，研究首接触渗流中点过程的凸序与感染渐近速度之间的关系，以理解感染传播模型中点过程排序对传播速度的影响。

Method: 基于点过程的凸序概念，分析首接触渗流中感染路径的存在性与数量；进而提出一种基于空概率排序的替代准则，用于证明一维 $\mathbb{Z}$-平稳点过程（$\mathbb{Z}$-stationary point processes）体系下的速度增加。

Result: 凸序保证了感染路径的数量与存在性的单调性，但不足以确保感染渐近速度的严格单调性；而基于空概率排序的新准则在一维 $\mathbb{Z}$-平稳点过程体系中实现了速度增加。

Conclusion: 点过程的凸序对感染路径存在性有单调性，但对渐近速度的严格单调性不足；空概率排序准则在一维体系下有效，为后续研究提供了新方向。

Abstract: Inspired by strict-monotonicity criteria for the time constant in first passage percolation, we investigate convex ordering of point processes in relation to the time constant in first contact percolation. In a nutshell, first contact percolation models the spread of an infection as a contact process without recovery based on a generalized graphical representation, where the usual homogeneous Poisson point processes on the edges are replaced by general simple point processes. Based on a notion of convex ordering for point processes, we prove monotonicity in the number and existence of infection paths. We argue that this convex ordering is however not enough to ensure strict monotonicities in the asymptotic speed of the infection. Instead, we propose a criterion based on an ordering of void probabilities and prove a speed-up for one-dimensional systems based on $\mathbb{Z}$-stationary point processes.

### [155] [Entropic and operational characterizations of dynamic quantum resources](https://arxiv.org/abs/2112.06906)
*Kaiyuan Ji,Eric Chitambar*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文基于熵概念和操作任务，提出了一套新方法，用于刻画封闭凸量子资源理论（包括动态资源）。通过推广量子条件最小熵而定义自由条件最小熵（FCME），为态或通道的自由可转换性提供了完备的熵条件，并给出了资源全局鲁棒性的信息论解释；同时，利用操作任务构造了动态资源的资源单调集，并证明了通道的鲁棒性度量等价于其在通信任务中的操作优势。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有量子资源理论（quantum resource theory）缺乏统一且完备的熵学刻画框架，尤其对于动态资源（如量子信道）的转换性和鲁棒性度量缺少信息论层面的系统解释。

Method: 提出自由条件最小熵（free conditional min-entropy, FCME）这一资源理论推广概念；基于FCME导出态和通道在封闭凸资源理论中自由可转换的完备熵条件；利用FCME构造互信息类量来解释资源全局鲁棒性（resource global robustness）；通过操作任务（operational tasks）构建完备的资源单调集（resource monotones）以检验通道的自由可转换性。

Result: 获得了封闭凸量子资源理论中态和通道自由可转换性的完备熵判据；建立了资源全局鲁棒性基于FCME的互信息类量的信息论解释；构造了用于动态资源的操作上有意义且完备的资源单调集；证明了任何良定义的基于鲁棒性的通道度量可解释为通道在通信任务中相对于自由通道的操作优势。

Conclusion: 该工作为封闭凸量子资源理论提供了熵学与操作任务双重视角的统一刻画工具，深化了对资源鲁棒性度量的信息论理解，并为动态资源的转换性检验和优势量化建立了新框架。

Abstract: We offer new methods for characterizing general closed and convex quantum resource theories, including dynamic ones, based on entropic concepts and operational tasks. We propose a resource-theoretic generalization of the quantum conditional min-entropy, termed the free conditional min-entropy (FCME), in the sense that it quantifies an observer's ``subjective'' degree of uncertainty about a quantum system given that the observer's information processing is limited to free operations of the resource theory. Using this generalized concept, we provide a complete set of entropic conditions for free convertibility between quantum states or channels in any closed and convex quantum resource theory. We also derive an information-theoretic interpretation for the resource global robustness of a state or a channel in terms of a mutual-information-like quantity based on the FCME. Apart from this entropic approach, we characterize dynamic resources by also analyzing their performance in operational tasks. We construct operationally meaningful and complete sets of resource monotones with these tasks, which enable faithful tests of free convertibility between quantum channels. Finally, we show that every well-defined robustness-based measure of a channel can be interpreted as an operational advantage of the channel over free channels in a communication task.
