### [156] [Converse bounds for quantum hypothesis exclusion: A divergence-radius approach](https://arxiv.org/abs/2501.09712)
*Kaiyuan Ji,Hemant K. Mishra,Milán Mosonyi,Mark M. Wilde*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文针对量子态排除（quantum state exclusion）与量子信道排除（quantum channel exclusion）任务，提出了一种不同于作者前期工作的替代性证明方法，基于非对称二元假设检验（asymmetric binary hypothesis testing）的强逆（strong converse）结论与散度半径（divergence radii）的几何论证，推导出相同的渐近误差指数（asymptotic error exponents）上界。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在假设排除（hypothesis exclusion）这一信息论任务中，需要从有限候选集中排除一个假假设，若被排除的恰好为真假设则产生错误。作者此前虽已通过非渐近分析（nonasymptotic analysis）给出了量子态与量子信道排除任务中渐近误差指数的可计算上界，但希望从不同概念路径验证该结果，以增强结论的可靠性。

Method: 本文采用了一种与前期工作中非渐近分析不同的新思路：将强逆结论应用于非对称二元假设检验，将每个候选假设分别与一个任意的“虚拟（dummy）”假设进行区分，再通过基于散度半径的几何论证导出所需的渐近误差指数上界。

Result: 通过这一替代性证明方法，本文得到了与前期工作相同的量子态排除与量子信道排除任务的渐近误差指数上界。该上界可表示为散度半径（divergence radii）的形式，且具有可计算性。

Conclusion: 本文提供了一种概念上独立于前期工作的新证明路径，验证了量子态与量子信道排除任务中渐近误差指数上界的正确性，并展示了强逆结论与几何论证在量子假设排除问题中的适用性。

Abstract: Hypothesis exclusion is an information-theoretic task in which an experimenter aims at ruling out a false hypothesis from a finite set of known candidates, and an error occurs if and only if the hypothesis being ruled out is the ground truth. For the tasks of quantum state exclusion and quantum channel exclusion -- where hypotheses are represented by quantum states and quantum channels, respectively -- efficiently computable upper bounds on the asymptotic error exponents were established in a recent work of the current authors [Ji et al., arXiv:2407.13728 (2024)], where the derivation was based on nonasymptotic analysis. In this companion paper of our previous work, we provide alternative proofs for the same upper bounds on the asymptotic error exponents of quantum state and channel exclusion, but using a conceptually different approach from the one adopted in the previous work. Specifically, we apply strong converse results for asymmetric binary hypothesis testing to distinguishing an arbitrary ``dummy'' hypothesis from each of the concerned candidates. This leads to the desired upper bounds in terms of divergence radii via a geometrically inspired argument.

</details>


### [157] [Quantum geometry of connected state manifolds: When diabolic points act as bridges between eigenstate manifolds](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28351)
*Jan Střeleček,Jakub Novotný,Pavel Cejnar*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出一种正则化方法，将参数哈密顿量中的二重点（diabolic points）视为相邻本征态流形之间的桥梁，将其粘合为单一连通态流形（connected state manifold），并据此修正贝里相位的拓扑规则，提升了数值稳定性并发现了新的测地线捷径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 参数哈密顿量（parametric Hamiltonians）中常出现点状的谱简并（即二重点或圆锥交叉点），这些点在Provost-Vallee度规（Provost-Vallee metric）中引发奇异性，导致数值不稳定和几何分析的困难，因此需要发展一种能够正则化该奇异性并统一处理本征态流形的方法。

Method: 通过坐标变换（coordinate transformation）对Provost-Vallee度规进行正则化（regularise the metric），将二重点重新解释为相邻本征态流形之间的桥梁，从而将多个流形粘合为一个单一连通的态流形。在此基础上，分析该结构的拓扑性质，并重新定义节线（nodal lines）与贝里相位（Berry phase）的关联规则。

Result: 连通态流形恢复了二重点附近的数值稳定性，扩大了测地线（geodesics）的类别，允许出现新的测地线捷径（geodesic shortcuts）。同时，该方法提供了一种新的贝里相位计算机制，即使路径穿过二重点也能适用。

Conclusion: 所提形式化框架不仅解决了二重点附近的奇异性和数值不稳定问题，还揭示了态流形更深层的拓扑结构，为量子几何和张量（quantum geometry and tensor）相关研究提供了新的分析工具。

Abstract: Parametric Hamiltonians often exhibit point-like spectral degeneracies (diabolic points, or conical intersections), which can lead to singularities in the Provost-Vallee metric of eigenstate manifolds. We regularise the metric by a coordinate transformation and develop a formalism in which diabolic points act as bridges between adjacent eigenstate manifolds, glueing them into a single connected state manifold. We characterise the topology of this structure and refine the rules for nodal lines governing the Berry phase. The connected state manifold restores the numerical stability near diabolic points, enlarges the class of geodesics allowing for new geodesic shortcuts, and provides a new mechanism for Berry phase computation, even along paths traversing diabolic points.

</details>


### [158] [Causal Order Cannot Be An Observable](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.25302)
*Declan Maguire,Fabio Costa*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于判别任务（discrimination tasks）的可观测性操作化定义，将其应用于量子过程（quantum processes）的因果结构分析，发现因果序（causal order）不满足可观测量的全部条件，因此不能被视为可观测量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子因果结构（quantum causal structures）的形式化发展已使其因果假设可被经验检验，而非先验前提。作者希望探究因果序是否能像可观测量（observable）一样被测量和解释，即这种类比是否成立。

Method: 以判别任务为基础，给出可观测量在操作层面的完全定义：先设定一组基础类别（相当于量子可观测量中的本征空间（eigenspace）），再施加三个关于类别之间在判别任务中关系的条件。将这一定义应用于编码因果结构的非态实体，即量子过程。

Result: 对具有严格因果序的量子过程类别进行分析发现：因果类别是“尖锐”（sharp）的，但违反了条件2或条件3。这表明因果序不满足可观测量定义的全部条件，因此不能被视为可观测量。

Conclusion: 因果序不能被视为可观测量。文献中声称相反结论的分析预设了等同于条件2和条件3的特殊条件，因此与本文发现并不矛盾。

Abstract: Recent developments in the formalisation of quantum causal structures have made it possible to test and compare hypotheses about causal structure empirically, rather than being a-priori assumptions. Such differences in causal structure may be leveraged to distinguish between the processes they belong to, akin to distinguishing between quantum states known to belong to different eigenspaces of an observable. So how far this analogy can be pushed? Can causal order be interpreted as a kind of observable? Can it be measured?
  To this end we construct a completely operational definition of observables in terms of `discrimination tasks'. This begins with some base set of classes (analogous to a quantum observable's eigenspaces) before we impose three conditions on how these classes relate under discrimination tasks. These conditions recover the properties of a standard observable, letting us apply this definition to non-state entities such as quantum processes, which naturally encode causal structure.
  These conditions can be described in plain language as (1) `members of any class are perfectly distinguishable from members of any other' (i.e. our classes are `sharp'), (2) `entities perfectly distinguishable pairwise are all perfectly distinguishable by a joint intervention', and (3) `if all members of a class are perfectly distinguishable from an entity, then the whole class is perfectly distinguishable from it jointly'.
  By analysing classes of quantum processes having strict causal orders, we find causal classes which are sharp but violate condition 2, and classes which violate condition 3. This implies that causal order cannot be an observable.
  We note cases in the literature which claim to prove the opposite, and discuss them. We find their analyses presume special circumstances equivalent to conditions (2) and (3), and so do not contradict our own findings.

</details>


### [159] [Expanding quantum magnetic field](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27426)
*Bogdan Damski*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该论文建立了瞬时开启并保持恒定的外部电流生成长程磁场的量子理论，精确求解了描述磁场膨胀的非平衡量子态，并与相应的量子静磁态进行比较。膨胀解展现出类似冲击波的前沿，将已形成磁场的区域与因果断开的区域分开。尽管膨胀场在波前之后局部趋近于静磁场，但对应的量子系统始终不同，尤其在能量、光子数及其涨落方面表现出明显差异。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索外部电流瞬间开启后，量子场论中磁场的因果形成（causal formation）过程，并为膨胀磁场与静磁场的量子态差异提供严格的解析证据。

Method: 基于量子场论，对瞬时开启并恒定维持的外部电流生成的长程磁场（long-range magnetic field）建立非平衡量子态（non-equilibrium quantum state）的精确解，并将其与量子静磁态（quantum magnetostatic state）进行对比分析。

Result: 膨胀磁场解展现出传播的冲击波状前沿（shockwave-like front），将已形成磁场的区域与因果断开区域分隔；膨胀场在波前之后局部趋近静磁场，但量子系统始终不同；能量、光子数及其涨落在膨胀与静磁两种构型中表现出明显差异。

Conclusion: 瞬时开启的电流产生的膨胀磁场与静磁场在量子层面不可等价，因果形成过程导致的非平衡量子态具有可观测的物理后果。

Abstract: We develop the quantum theory of the causal formation of a long-range magnetic field generated by an external current that is instantaneously switched on and subsequently kept constant in time. The resulting non-equilibrium quantum state, describing the expanding magnetic field, is obtained exactly and compared with the corresponding quantum magnetostatic state. In contrast to the magnetostatic case, the expanding solution exhibits a propagating shockwave-like front separating regions where the magnetic field has already been formed from those that remain causally disconnected from the source. We show that although the expanding field locally approaches the magnetostatic field behind the shockwave-like front, the associated quantum systems remain distinct at all times. In particular, we obtain manifestly different results for the energy, photon number, and their fluctuations in expanding and magnetostatic field configurations. Our results are first derived for a general external current and then illustrated with a specific example.

</details>


### [160] [Benchmarking Quantum Annealing for a Greenhouse-Inspired Control QUBO](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27670)
*Hamzeh Alavirad,Maryam Bahrami Zanjani*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文在温室启发二元优化问题（binary heater scheduling QUBO）上，系统对比了经典模拟退火、路径积分模拟量子退火和D-Wave量子退火工作流的性能。实验表明经典方法稳定且接近最优解，而D-Wave平台（包括混合求解器和QPU）在给定时间限制下可靠性较低，未展现出量子优势。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 评估当前退火优化（annealing-based optimization）工作流在实际结构化控制问题中的表现，特别是检验量子退火（quantum annealing）方案相较于经典基线方法是否具有优势。

Method: 以温室加热器调度为背景，构建二次无约束二元优化（quadratic unconstrained binary optimization, QUBO）问题，时间视界 H 表示逐小时控制决策次数。将求解器输出解码为加热器调度方案，并在原始温室模拟器中采用相同物理目标函数和可行性判据进行评估。对比了经典模拟退火（simulated annealing）、路径积分模拟量子退火（path-integral simulated quantum annealing）以及 D-Wave Leap Hybrid BQM 和直接 D-Wave QPU 执行。

Result: 经典模拟退火和路径积分模拟量子退火在所有重复实验中均能生成可行的近最优解，最优目标值接近精确最优解。D-Wave Leap Hybrid BQM 工作流在 15–60 秒时间限制下可靠性较低，未超越经典基线。直接 D-Wave QPU 在小规模实例（H=10, H=12）上可恢复精确最优解，但精确命中率在 H=14 时从 5/10 降至 2/10 再降至 0/10，方差显著高于经典方法。

Conclusion: 实验未发现量子优势（quantum advantage），但提供了一种可重复、基于物理解码的基准测试方法，揭示了经典、混合和直接量子退火工作流在结构化控制 QUBO 问题上的当前优势与局限性。

Abstract: We benchmark current annealing-based optimization workflows on a greenhouse-inspired quadratic unconstrained binary optimization problem for binary heater scheduling, where the horizon H denotes the number of hourly control decisions. For the main one-day instance (H=24), all solver outputs are decoded back into heater schedules and evaluated in the original greenhouse simulator using the same physical objective and feasibility criterion. Classical simulated annealing and path-integral simulated quantum annealing produce feasible near-optimal solutions in all repetitions, with best objectives close to the exact optimum. In contrast, the tested D-Wave Leap Hybrid BQM workflow is less reliable and does not outperform the classical baselines under 15--60~s requested time limits. Direct D-Wave QPU execution on reduced instances remains feasible in all runs and recovers the exact optimum for H=10 and H=12, but the exact-hit rate drops from 5/10 to 2/10 and then to 0/10 at H=14, with substantially higher variance than the classical baselines. The results do not indicate quantum advantage, but provide a reproducible, physically decoded benchmark that exposes the current strengths and limitations of classical, hybrid, and direct quantum annealing workflows on structured control QUBOs.

</details>


### [161] [Unified resonant-manifold framework for dynamical quantum phase transitions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.22915)
*Jesse J. Osborne,Cheuk Yiu Wong,Jad C. Halimeh*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出一个统一框架，从不同乘积态构型的能量结构出发，解释动力学量子相变（DQPT）中不同类型（流形型与分支型）的出现机制，并通过1+1维Z₂格点规范理论（LGT）中的淬火实验加以验证。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 以往研究虽区分了DQPT的不同类型（如正常与反常、流形型与分支型），但缺乏一个统一机制解释每种类型为何在特定场景中出现。

Method: 提出一个以初始态流形（initial state manifold）和过渡流形（transitional manifold）的能量共振结构为核心的统一框架；通过对1+1维Z₂格点规范理论（LGT）中两种不同构型的淬火（quench）到不同参数区域进行数值分析来验证该框架。

Result: 流形型DQPT由初始态流形内部的共振主导；分支型DQPT由与初始流形通过低阶过程动态连接的过渡流形的共振主导。分支型DQPT的（不）规则性与该过渡流形的多重性相关；还观察到回返率中扩展简并周期，其出现也依赖于过渡流形的结构。

Conclusion: 本研究揭示了分支型DQPT的动力学机制，将DQPT定位为约束希尔伯特空间（constrained Hilbert space）中共振连通性的探针，为全面理解动力学临界性的多层面性质奠定基础。

Abstract: Dynamical quantum phase transitions (DQPTs) are an exciting paradigm of out-of-equilibrium criticality in many-body systems manifested in nonanalytic behavior in the return rate to the initial state following a sudden quench. While previous work has tried to distinguish between distinct types of DQPTs, such as regular and anomalous, or manifold and branch, a comprehensive understanding of why each type appears in a given scenario is still lacking. In this work, we propose a unified framework addressing this gap in terms of the energy structure of different product state configurations. In particular, while manifold DQPTs are governed by resonances within the initial state manifold, branch DQPTs are governed by resonances with a transitional manifold of states dynamically connected to the initial manifold by low-order processes. We show that the (ir)regularity of branch DQPTs is related to the multiplicity of this transitional manifold, and we also observe exotic periods of extended degeneracy in the return rate (beyond the conventional level crossing of a DQPT) which are also conditioned on the structure of this transitional manifold. We demonstrate this by studying quenches of two different configurations in the 1 + 1D Z_2 LGT to various parameter regimes. Our findings provide a dynamical mechanism underlying branch DQPTs and frames DQPTs as probes of resonant connectivity in constrained Hilbert spaces, paving the way to a more complete understanding of the multifaceted nature of dynamical criticality.

</details>


### [162] [A multilevel tensor network compression technique for simulating Lindblad dynamics in superconducting circuits](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.27515)
*Adrien Moulinas,Xavier Waintal*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于张量网络（tensor network）的仿真技术，用于模拟超导量子电路（superconducting quantum circuits）中少数相互作用玻色子模式（interacting bosonic modes）的林德布拉德动力学（Lindblad dynamics）。该技术通过三层嵌套的张量网络压缩，分别处理密度矩阵的纯度、模式间适度的纠缠以及任意高的模式占据数，实现了对大型猫量子比特（cat qubits）和穿透型量子比特（transmon qubits）电离过程的高效仿真，计算速度比暴力方法提升数个数量级。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 设计超导量子硬件需要能够处理各种非理想情形的仿真工具，这进而要求自动检测某些结构并利用它们降低计算成本。现有方法在模式占据数很高时，朴素截断（naïve truncations）效率低下，需要更高效的仿真技术。

Method: 方法包含三个嵌套层次的张量网络压缩：(i) 使用密度矩阵的全局纯化（global purification）处理纯度较高的情况；(ii) 压缩不同模式之间的连接以利用适度的纠缠（moderate entanglement）；(iii) 使用量子化表示（quantics representation）处理福克占据数（Fock occupation number）。

Result: 在大型猫量子比特仿真和穿透型量子比特电离仿真中，该方法相比暴力方法实现了数个数量级的加速。后者将以前需要大型超级计算基础设施的仿真降低到了笔记本电脑级别。系统规模的扩展性（scaling）良好，有望实现真正的计算机辅助设计（computer assisted design）。

Conclusion: 该张量网络技术能够有效利用超导量子电路中常见的三种结构特征（纯度、适度纠缠、高占据数），大幅提升仿真效率，使大规模计算机辅助设计成为可能。

Abstract: Designing superconducting quantum hardware requires simulation tools that can account for various deviations from ideal scenarios. This, in turn, requires approaches that automatically detect certain structures and leverage them to make the computation affordable. Here, we develop a tensor network based technique to simulate the Lindblad dynamics of a few interacting bosonic modes with a focus on superconducting quantum circuits. The technique detects and takes advantage of two very common situations: (i) the density matrix being pure or not far from pure and (ii) the entanglement between different modes being moderate (typically qubit-like). However, (iii) the occupation of the modes can be arbitrarily high (making naïve truncations inefficient). To leverage these features, we use three different nested levels of tensor network compression: (i) we work with a global purification of the density matrix, (ii) we compress the connection between different modes to account for the moderate entanglement and (iii) we use a quantics representation of the Fock occupation number. We showcase the technique for the simulation of large cat qubits as well as for the ionization of transmon qubits, demonstrating orders-of-magnitude speed-up with respect to brute force approaches. In the latter example, it brings the simulation, previously reported on a large supercomputing infrastructure, to laptop level. The favorable scaling with system size should bring genuine computer assisted design of these systems within scope.

</details>


### [163] [A cryogenic apparatus for coupling two-dimensional materials to a confocal multimode optical cavity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.28815)
*Han S. Hiller,Pranav Parakh,Samuel H. Aronson,Kenji Maeda,Di Lao,Julian Stewart,Zengde She,Jierong Wang,Xiaodong Xu,Tony Heinz,Benjamin L. Lev*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文描述了一套为研究二维范德瓦尔斯材料中光驱动相干声子布居而设计的低温、超高真空、长度可调共焦法布里-珀罗腔实验装置，该装置通过腔内样品和光学超模显著增强光-物质耦合。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 二维范德瓦尔斯材料（two-dimensional van der Waals materials）展现出多种关联电子相（correlated electron phases），而光学驱动有望用于调控这些相。例如，腔增强的连续波（continuous-wave, CW）拉曼激发被认为可通过材料激子（excitons）相干且超辐射地布居声子或电荷密度波（charge density waves）。为实验实现这一目标，需要一套满足特定要求的高精度实验装置。

Method: 搭建了一套超高真空（ultrahigh-vacuum）系统，内含一个长度可调的共焦法布里-珀罗腔（confocal Fabry-Pérot cavity），样品置于腔内并低温冷却、抗振稳定。采用四轴纳米定位器（four-axis nanopositioner）对准样品并连接电极，用于载流子密度调制和输运测量。通过多模腔（multimode cavity）的透射光进行原位样品成像以辅助对准；研究中样品为过渡金属二硫族化物（transition metal dichalcogenide）。工作在近共焦几何（confocal geometry）下，光场被汇聚为局域超模（localized supermode），显著增强光-物质耦合（light-matter coupling）。尽管腔长处于毫米量级，仍保留了足够的样品对准与交换空间。

Result: 该装置在毫米级腔长下通过近共焦几何实现了光场的局域超模汇聚，从而显著增强了光-物质耦合。同时，装置保留了样品对准与交换的充足空间。

Conclusion: 所描述的装置满足了光驱动二维范德瓦尔斯材料相干声子布居等实验程序的核心要求，为实现腔增强拉曼激发和关联电子相调控提供了实验平台基础。

Abstract: Two-dimensional van der Waals materials exhibit a variety of correlated electron phases, and optical driving offers a promising route toward manipulating them. For example, cavity-enhanced, continuous-wave (CW) Raman excitation has been suggested as a way to coherently and superradiantly populate phonons or charge density waves via material excitons. A steady-state phonon population may be sustained with sufficiently strong electron-phonon coupling to drive novel collective response. We describe an apparatus built to meet the requirements of such an experimental program: Namely, an ultrahigh-vacuum system housing a length-tunable confocal Fabry-Pérot cavity with an intracavity sample, both cryogenically cooled and stabilized against vibrations. A four-axis nanopositioner aligns the sample and supports electrical leads for sample carrier density modulation and transport measurements. Transmission through the multimode cavity enables in situ sample imaging for alignment; the sample is a transition metal dichalcogenide in this work. Operating near the confocal geometry concentrates the optical field into a localized supermode that substantially enhances light-matter coupling. This enhancement is preserved despite the millimeter-scale cavity length, which provides room for sample alignment and exchange.

</details>
